abrhaminte putrnaydaviidinteputrnayyeshuvinte vamshavali :
abraham yisahakyine janippichau ; yisahak yakyobine janippichau ; yakyob yehoodayeyum avante sahodaranmareyum janippichau ;
yehoodtamarill paresineyum sarahineyum janippichau ; pares heresane janippichau ; heresan aaramine janippichau ;
aaram ammiinadabine janippichau ; ammiinadab nahashone janippichau ; nahashon shalemane janippichau ;
shaleman rahabill bovasine janippichau ; bovas roottill oabedine janippichau ; oabed yishshayiye janippichau ;
yishshayi daviid rajavine janippichau ; daviid uriiyavinte bhayarryayirunnavallill shalomone janippichau ;
shalomon rehabayame janippichau ; rehabayam abiiyave janippichau ; abiiyavu aasaye janippichau ; aasyoshaphattine janippichau ;
yoshaphat yoramine janippichau ; yoram ussiiyave janippichau ;
ussiiyavu yothamine janippichau ; yotham aahasine janippichau ; aahas hiskiiyave janippichau ;
hiskiiyavu manashshaye janippichau ; manashshaamosine janippichau ; aamos yoshiiyave janippichau ;
yoshiiyavu yekhonayaveyum avante sahodaranmareyum babell prvasakalattu janippichau .
babellprvasam kajhyinjidtu yekhonayvu sheyalatiiyeline janippichau ; sheyalatiiyell serubaabeline janippichau ;
serubaabell abiihoodine janippichau ; abiihood elayakyiimine janippichau ; elayakyiim aasorine janippichau ;
aasor sadokyine janippichau ; sadok aakhiimine janippichau ; aakhiim eliihoodine janippichau ;
eliihood eliiyasare janippichau ; eliiyasar matthane janippichau ; matthan yakyobine janippichau .
yakyob marriyayude bhattravayyosephine janippichau . avallillninu krisatu enu perullyeshu janichau .
ingane talamurrakall aake abrahammutall daviidvare patinnalum daviid mutall babellprvasattollam patinnalum babellprvasammutall krisatuvinollam patinnalum aakunu .
ennall yeshukrisatuvinte jananam ivannm aayirunu . avante ammyaymarriyyosephinu vivaham nischayikyppedtsheksham avar koodivarum mube parishuddhatmavinall gabharinniyayi enu kandu .
avallude bhattravayyoseph niitimanakakondum avallkyu lokapavadam varuttuvan avanu manassillaykakondum avalle gooddhamayi upekshippan bhavichau .
ingane ninachairikyuboll kattravinte dootan avanu spttill prtaykshanayi : daviidinte makanayyosephe , ninte bhayaaryaymarriyaye chettrukollvan shakkikyenda ; avallill ulpaditamayatu parishuddhatmavinall aakunu .
avall oru makane prsavikyum ; avan tante janatte avarude papangallill ninu rakshippanirikykondu nii avanu yeshu enu per idennam enu parranju .
" kanaykgabharinniyayi oru makane prsavikyum . avanu daivam nammodu koode ennatthrmullimmanuvell enu per villikyum . "
enu kattravu prvachakan mukhantaram arullicheeyattu nivrattiyakuvan itokyeyum sambhavichau .
yoseph urrakym unnanur kattravinte dootan kalpichaatu pole cheyatu , bhayaarye chettrukondu .
makane prsavikyum vare avan avalle parigrhichaill . makanu avan yeshu enu per villichau .
herodrajavinte kalattu yeshu yehoodayyile bettelhemill janichasheksham , kijhyakyuninu vidanmar yerooshalemill etti :
yehoodanmarude rajavayi pirrannavan evide ? njangall avante nakshatrm kijhyakyu kandu avane namaskarippan vannirikyunu enu parranju .
herodarajavu atu kedtidtu avanum yerooshalem okyeyum bhrmichau .
janattinte mahapurohitanmareyum shasrtimareyum ellam koodtivarutti : krisatu evide aakunu janikyunnatu enu avarodu chodichau .
avar avanodu : yehoodayyile bettelhemilltanne :
" yehoodaydeshattile bettelheme , nii yehooday prbhuky nmarill odtum cherrutall ; ente janamayyisrayeline meypanulltalavan ninnill ninu purrappedtuvarum . " enningane prvachakan mukhantaram ejhyutiyirikyunu enu parranju .
ennarre herodavu vidanmare rahasaymayi villichau , nakshatrm vellivaysamayam avarodu sookshmayi chodichaarrinju .
avare bettelhemilekyu ayachau : ningall chenu shishuvinekyurrichau sookshmayi anevkshippin ; kandettiyall njanum chenu avane namaskarikyendatinu , vanu enne arriyippin enu parranju .
rajavu parranjtu kedtu avar purrappedtu ; avar kijhyakyu kandnakshatrm shishu irikyunnsthlattinu miite vanu nilkyuvollam avakyrumumbayi poykyondirunu .
nakshatrm kandatukondu avar atayntam santokshichau :
aviidtill chenu , shishuvine ammyaymarriyayodukoode kandu , viinnu avane namaskyrichau ; nikshepapatrngalle turranu avanu ponum kunturukyvum moorum kvechau .
herodavinte adukyll madangippokarutu enu spttill arullappadundayidtu avar verre vajhyiyayi sdeshattekyu madangippoyi .
avar poyasheksham kattravinte dootan yosephinu spttill prtaykshanayi : nii ejhyunnettu shishuvineyum ammyeyum koodtikyondu misryiimilekyu oadippoyi , njan ninnodu parrayumvare avide pakyurka . herodavu shishuvine nashippikyendatinu avane anevkshippan bhavikyunu enu parranju .
avan ejhyunnettu shishuvineyum ammyeyum ratriyill tanne koodtikyondu purrappedtu misryiimilekyu poyi .
herodavinte marannattollam avan avide pattru : " misryiimillninu njan ente makane villichau varutti " enu kattravu prvachakan mukhantaram arullicheeyattu nivrattiyakuvan samgativanu .
vidanmar tanne kalliyakyi enu herodavu kandu vallare kopichau , vidanmarodu chodichaarrinjkalattinu ottvannm randu vayassum tajhyeyumullaankudtikalle okyeyum bettelhemilum atinte ellatirukallilum aallayachau kollichau .
" rramayill oru shabdam kedtu , karachaalum valiynilavilliyum tanne ; rrahell makylle cheealli karanju ; avar illaykayall aashasam kaikyollvan manassillatirunu "
enu yiremayaprvachakan mukhantaram arullicheeytatu anu nivrattiyayi .
ennall herodavu kajhyinjupoyasheksham kattravinte dootan misryiimillvechau yosephinu spttill prtaykshanayi :
shishuvinu prannahani varuttuvan nokyiyavar marichaupoyatukondu nii ejhyunnettu shishuvineyum ammyeyum koodtikyondu yisrayelldeshattekyu pokenu parranju .
avan ejhyunnettu shishuvineyum ammyeyum koodtikyondu yisrayelldeshattu vanu .
ennall yehoodayyill akyerlayos tante appnayherodavinu pakaram vajhyunu enu kedttukondu avide pokuvan bhayappedtu , spttill arullappadundayidtu galiilprdeshangallilekyu marrippoyi .
avan nasarrayin enu villikyppedum enu prvachakanmar mukhantaram arullicheeyattu nivrattiyavan takyvannm nasarret enngramattill chenu pattru .
akalattu yohannan sapakan vanu . yehoodaymarubhoomiyill prsamgichau :
srggrajaym samiipichairikyyall manasantarappeduvin enu parranju .
" marubhoomiyill villichau parrayunnavante vakyavitu : kattravinte vajhyi orukyi avante patnirappakyuvin " enningane yeshayaprvachakan parranjvan ivan tanne .
yohannanu odtkaromam kondulluduppum arayill tollvarrum undayirunu ; avante aaharamo vedtukyilliyum kadtutenum aayirunu .
anu yerooshalemayrum yehooday deshakyarokyeyum yodtrante irukareyumullellnadtukarum purrappedtu avante adukyll chenu
tangallude papangalle eettu parranju kondu yodtran nadiyill avanall sanam eettu .
tante sanattinnayi pariisharilum sadtookayrilum palar varunnatu kandarre avan avarodu parranjtu : sappr rsantatikalle , varuvanullkopatte ojhyinju oadippokuvan ningallkyu upadeshichau tannatu aar ?
manasantarattinu yogaymayphalam kaypin .
abraham njangallkyu pitavayidtu undu enu ullam kondu parravan tuniyarutu ; i kallukallillninu abrahaminu makylle ullavakyuvan daivattinu kajhyiyum enu njan ningallodu parrayunu .
ippoll tanne vrakshangallude chuvadtir kodali vechairikyunu ; nallaphalam kaykyatt vraksham ellam vedti tiiyill idtukallayunu .
njan ningalle manasantarattinnayi vellattill sanam eelpikyunnateyullu ; entepinnale varunnavano ennekyall balavan aakunu ; avante cherippu chumappan njan matiyayavanalla ; avan ningalle parishuddhatmavilum tiiyilum sanam eelpikyum .
viishumurram avante kayaill undu ; avan kallatte muttum vedippakyi kotambu kallappurayill koodtivekyyum patir kedatt tiiyill idtu chudtukallakayum cheyaum .
anantaram yeshu yohannanall sanam eelkyuvan galiilayillninu yodtrankare avante adukyll vanu .
yohannano avane vilakyi : ninnall sanam eelkyuvan enikyu aavashaym ; pinne nii ente adukyll varunnuvo enu parranju .
yeshu avanodu : ippoll sammtiky ; ingane sakalaniitiyum nivattrikyunnatu namukyu uchitam enu uttram parranju ; ennarre avan avane sammtichau .
yeshu sanam eett udane vellattill ninu kayarri ; appoll srggm turranu daivatmavu pravennapole irrangi tante mell varunnatu avan kandu ;
ivan ente priyaputrn ; ivanill njan prsadichairikyunu enu srggttillninu oru shabdam undayi .
anantaram pishachinall pariikshikyppeduvan yeshuvine aatmavu marubhoomiyilekyu nadatti .
avan nalpatu pakalum nalpatu ravum upavasichaasheksham avanu vishanu .
appoll pariikshakan aduttu vanu : nii daivaputrn ekkill i kallu appmayatiiruvan kalpiky enu parranju .
" manukshayn appmkondu matrmalla , daivattinte vayillkoodi varunnsakalavachanam kondum jiivikyunu " enu ejhyutiyirikyunu enu uttram parranju .
pinne pishachu avane vishuddh nagarattill kendupoyi daivalayattinte agrttinmell nirrutti avanodu :
nii daivaputrn ekkill tajhyattodtu chaduka ; " ninnekyurrichau avan tante dootanmarodu kalpikyum ; avan ninte kall kallinodu tadtatavannm ninne kayaill tangikyollum " enu ejhyutiyirikyunuvalelenu parranju . yeshu avanodu :
" ninte daivamaykattravine pariikshikyrutu " enum koode ejhyutiyirikyunu enu parranju .
pinne pishachu avane eettvum uyanneraru malamell koodtikyondupoyi lokattilullsakalrajayngalleyum avayude mahattteyum kannichau :
viinnu enne namaskyrichaall itokyeyum ninakyu taram enu avanodu parranju .
yeshu avanodu : sattane , enne vidtupo ; " ninte daivamaykattravine namaskarichau avane matrme aaradhikyavu " enu ejhyutiyirikynuvalelenu parranju .
appoll pishachu avane vidtupoyi ; dootanmar aduttuvanu avane shushrookshichau .
yohannan tadavill aayi enu kedtarre avan galiilekyu vangippoyi ,
nasarret vidtu sebooloonteyum naphataliyudeyum atirukallill kadalkyreyullkaphannarhoomill chenu pattru ;
" sebooloondeshavum naphatalideshavum kadalkyrayilum yodtrannakyreyumullnadum jatikallude galiilayum
ingane irudtill irikyunnjanam valiyoru vellichaam kandu ; marannattinte deshattilum nijhyalilum irikyunnavakyru prkasham udichau "
enu yeshayaaprvachakan mukhantaram arullicheeyattu nivrattiyakuvan idavanu .
anumutall yeshu : srggrajaym samiipichairikyyall manasantarappeduvin enu prsamgichau tudangi .
avan galiilakydalpurrattu nadakyubell paretas enu perullshimon , avante sahedaranayarentayas enningane miinpidikyarayrandu sahodaranmar kadalill valaviishunnatu kandu :
ente pinnale varuvin ; njan ningalle manukshayre pidikyunnavarakyum enu avarodu parranju .
udane avar valvidtechau avane anugamichau .
avideninu mubodtu poyarre sebediyude makan yakyobum avante sahodaran yohannanum ennverre randu sahodaranmar padakill irunu appnaysebadiyumayi valnannakyunnatu kandu avareyum villichau .
avarum udane padakineyum appneyum vidtu avane anugamichau .
pinne yeshu galiilayill okyeyum chutti sanchrichaukondu avarude pallikallill upadeshikyyum rajayttinte suvisheksham prsamgikyyum janattilullsakaldiinatteyum vayadhiyeyum sekhaymakyukayum cheytu .
avante shruti surriyayilokyeyum parannu nanavayadhikallalum badhakallalum valanjvar , bhootagrsatr , chandrrogikall , pakshavatakyar ingane sakalavidhdiinakyareyum avante adukyll konduvanu .
avan avare sekhaymakyi ; galiila , dekyppoli , yerooshalem , yehooday , yodtrnnakyre ennii idangallill ninu vallare puruksharam avane pintudanur .
avan puruksharatte kandarre malamell kayarri , , avan irunnsheksham shikshaynmar adukyll vanu .
avan tiruvayemajhyinju avarodu upadeshichaatentennall :
aatmavill daridrrayavar bhagayvanmar ; srggrajaym avakyrullatu .
du : khikyunnavar bhagayvanmar ; avakyru aashasam labhikyum .
semaytayullavar bhagayvanmar ; avar bhoomiye avakashmakyum .
niitikyu vishannu dahikyunnavar bhagayvanmar ; avakyru trapati varum .
karunnayullavar bhagayvanmar ; avakyru karunnlabhikyum .
hradayashuddhiyullavar bhagayvanmar ; avar daivatte kannum .
samadhanam undakyunnavar bhagayvanmar ; avar daivattinte putrnmar enu villikyppedum .
niiti nimittm upadrvikyppedunnavar bhagayvanmar ; srggrajaym avakyrullatu .
ente nimittm ningalle pajhyikyyum upadrvikyyum ningallekyondu elltinmayum kallavayi parrakayum cheyauboll ningall bhagayvanmar .
srggttill ningallude prtiphalam valutakakondu santokshichaullasippin ; ningallkyu mubeyundayirunnprvachakanmareyum avar anganetanne upadrvichauvalela .
ningallbhoomiyude uppakunu ; uppu karamillatepoyall atinu entonu kondu rasam varuttam ? purrattukallanjidtu manukshayr chavidtuvan allate mattonninum pinne kollunnatallal .
ningall lokattinte vellichaam aakunu ; malamell irikyunnpadtnnam marranjirippan padillal .
villakyu kattichau parrayin kiijhyalltandinmelaretvekyunnatu : appoll atu viidtilullellavakyrum prkashikyunu .
angane tanne manukshayr ningallude nallprvrattikalle kandu , srggsthnayningallude pitavine mahatppeduttendatinu ningallude vellichaam avarude mumbill prkashikydte .
njan nayayaprmannatteyo prvachakanmareyo niikyendatinu vanu enu niroopikyrutu ; niikyuvanallnivattrippanaretnjan vannatu .
sataymayidtu njan ningallodu parrayunu : aakashavum bhoomiyum ojhyinjupokumvare sakalavum nivrattiyakuvollam nayayaprmannattillninu oru valli ekkilum pulli ekkilum orunallum ojhyinjupekayillal .
aakayall i eettvum cherriykalpanakallill onu ajhyikyyum manukshayre angane patthippikyyum cheyaunnavan srggrajayttill eettvum cherriyavan enu villikyppedum ; avaye aacharikyyum patthippikyyum cheyaunnavanno srggrajayttill valiyavan enu villikyppedum .
ningallude niiti shasrtimarudeyum pariishanmarudeyum niitiye kaviyunnilelkkill ningall srggrajayttill kadakyyillenu njan ningallodu parrayunu .
kulcheyaarutu enum aarekkilum kulcheyatall nayayavidhikyu yogaynakum enum poovarrnmarodu arullicheeyattu ningall kedtidtundalela .
njano ningallodu parrayunnatu : sahodaranodu kopikyunnavan ellam nayayavidhikyu yogaynakum ; sahodaranodu nissarenu parranjalo nayayadhipasabhayude mumbill nillkyendivarum ; mooddhenu parranjalo inarakattinu yogaynakum .
aakayall ninte vajhyipadu yagapiitthattikkll kenduvaruboll sahodaranu ninte nere vallatum undenu avidevechau oammrvannall
ninte vajhyipadu avide yagapiitthattinte mumbill vecheechau , onnamatu chenu sahodaranodu niranu kollka ; pinne vanu ninte vajhyipadu kajhyiky .
ninte prtiyogiyodukoode vajhyiyill ullappoll tanne vegattill avanodu innangikyollka ; allanjall prtiyogi ninne nayayadhipanum nayayadhipan chevakanum eelpichaidtu nii tadavill aayepakum .
oduvilatte kashupolum koduttu tiiruvollam nii avide ninu purrattu varikayillenu njan sataymayidtu ninnodu parrayunu .
vaybhicharam cheyaarutu enu arullicheeyattu ningall kedtidtundalela .
njano ningallodu parrayunnatu : srtiiye mohikyendatinu avalle nokyunnavan ellam hradayam kondu avallodu vaybhicharam cheyatupoyi .
ennall valakknnu ninakyu idachaarvaruttunu ekkill atine choonneduttu errinjukallaka ; ninte shariiram mujhyuvanum narakattill viijhyunnatinekyall ninte avayavangallill onu nashikyunnatu ninakyu pryojanamareta .
valakkai ninakyu idachaar varuttunu ekkill atinevedtierrinju kallaka ; ninte shariiram mujhyuvanum narakattill pekunnatine kyall avayavangallill onu nashikyunnatu ninakyu pryojanamareta .
aarekkilum bharayye upekshichaall avallkyu upekshannapatrm kodukydte enum arullicheeyatidtundalela .
njano ningallodu parrayunnatu : parasamgam hetuvayidtllate bhayaarye upekshikyunnavanellam avallekyondu vaybhicharam cheyaikyunu ; upekshichaavalle aarekkilum vivaham kajhyichaall vaybhicharam cheyaunu .
kallsataym cheyaarutu enum sataym cheyattu kattravinu nivattrikyennam enum poovaarnmarodu arullicheeyattu ningall kedtidtundalela .
njano ningallodu parrayunnatu : asheksham sataym cheyaarutu ; srggttekyondu arutu , atu daivattinte simhasanam ;
bhoomiyekyondu arutu atu avantepadapiittham ; yerooshaleminekyondu arutu , atu maharajavinte nagaram .
ninte talayekyondum sataym cheyaarutu ; oru romavum velluppippano karruppippano ninakyu kajhyikayillalela .
ningallude vakyu uvau , uvau enum illa , illenum aayirikydte ; itill adhikamayatu dushtanill ninu varunu .
kanninu pakaram kannum pallinu pakaram pallum enu arullicheeyattu ningall kedtidtundalela .
njano ningallodu parrayunnatu : dushtanodu etikyrrutu ; ninne valatte chekidtttu adikyunnavanu mattetum tirichau kanniky .
ninnodu vayvaharichau ninte vasrtm eduppan ichchikyunnvanu ninte putappum vidtukoduky .
oruttn ninne oru najhyikvajhyipekuvan nibaarndichaall randu avanodu koode poka .
ninnodu yachikyunnavanu koduky ; vayipp vanguvan ichchikyunnavane ojhyinjukallayarutu .
koodtukarane senhiky enum shatruvine pakeky enum arullicheeyattu ningall kedtidtundalela .
njano ningallodu parrayunnatu : ningallude shatrukylle senhippin ; ningalle upadrvikyunnavakyru vendi pratthrippin ;
sggrsthnayningallude pitavinu putrnmarayi tiirendatinu tanne ; avan dushtanmarude melum nallavarudemelum tante sooyaarne udippikyyum niitimanmarudemelum niitikedtvarude melum majhypeyaikyyum cheyaunuvalela .
ningalle senhikyunnavare senhichaall ningallkyu entu prtiphalam ? chukkkyarum angane tanne cheyaunnillayo ?
sahodaranmare matrm vandnam cheyatall ningall entu visheksham cheyaunu ? jatikallum angane tanne cheyaunnillayo ?
aakayall ningallude sggriiypitavu sallgunnapoonnrn aayirikyunnatupole ningallum sallgunnpoonnrrakuvin .
manukshayr kannendatinu ningallude niitiye avarude mumbill cheyaatirippan sookshippin ; allanjall sggr ttilullningallude pitavinte pakyll ningallkyu prtiphalamillal .
aakayall bhikshkodukyuboll manukshayrall manam labhippan pallikallilum viithikallilum kapadabhtikyar cheyaunnatu pole ninte mumbill kahallam utikyrutu ; avarkyu prtiphalam kidtippoyi enu njan sataymayidtu ningallodu parrayunu .
niiyo bhikshkodukyuboll ninte bhikshrahasayttilayirikyendatinu valakkai cheyaunnatu entu enu idakkai arriyarutu .
rahasayttill kannunnninte pitavu ninakyu prtiphalam tarum .
ningall pratthrikyuboll kapadabhtikyareppole aakarutu ; avar manukshaykyur villangendatinu pallikallilum terukyonnukallilum ninu kondu pratthrippan ishtappedunu ; avakyur prtiphalam kidtippoyi enu njan sataymayidtu ningallodu parrayunu .
niiyo pratthrikyuboll arrayill kadanu vatill adechau rahasayttilullninte pitavinodu pratthriky ; rahasayttill kannunnninte pitavu ninakyu prtiphalam tarum .
pratthrikyyill ningall jatikalleppole jalpanam cheyaarutu ; atibhakshannattall uttram kidtum ennalelavarkyu tonunnatu .
avarodu tulayrakarutu ; ningallkyu aavashaymullatu innatenu ningall yachikyummube ningallude pitavu arriyunuvalela .
ningall ivaannm pratthrippin ; sggrsthnaynjangallude pitave , nante namam vishuddhiikarikyppedenname ;
ninte rajaym varenname ; ninteishtam sggrttile ppole bhoomiyilum aakenname ;
njangallkyu aavashaymullaaharam inu tarenname ;
njangallude kadakyarodu njangall kshamichairikyunnatupole njangallude kadangalle njangallodum kshamikyenname ;
njangalle pariikshayill kadattate dushtakkll ninu njangalle viduvikyenname . rajayvum shtiyum mahatvum ennekyum ninakyullatalela .
ningall manukshayrodu avarude pijhyakalle kshamichaall , sggrsthnayningallude pitavu ningallodum kshamikyum .
ningall manukshayrodu pijhyakalle kshamikyanjalo ningallude pitavu ningallude pijhyakalleyum kshamikyyillal .
upavasikyuboll ningall kapadabhtikyareppole vadiymukham kannikyrutu ; avar upavasikyunnatu manakshayrkyu villangendatinu mukham viroopamakyunu ; avakyrru prtiphalam kidtippoyi enu njan sataymayidtu ningallodu parrayunu .
niiyo upavasikyuboll ninte upavasam manukshaykyrllrahasayttilullninte pitavinu villangendatinu talayill enn techau mukham kajhyukuka .
rahasayttill kannunnninte pitavu ninakyu prtiphalam nalkum .
pujhyuvum turumbum kedukyyum kallanmar turanu moshtikyyum cheyaunni bhoomiyill ningall nikshepam sroopikyrutu .
pujhyuvum turumbum kedukyateyum kallanmar turanu moshtikyateyumirikyunnsggrttill nikshepam sroopichau kollvin .
ninte nikshepam ulledattu ninte hradayavum irikyum .

alla , entu kanman poyi ? madtrvavasrtm dharichamanukshayneyo ? madtrvavasrtm dharikyunnavar rajagrahangalli lalela .
allentinu poyi ? oru prvachakane kanmano ? ate , prvachakanilum mikechaavane tanne enu njan ningallodu parrayunu .
" njan ente dootane ninakyu mumbayi ayakyunu ; avan ninte mumbill ninakyu vajhyi orukyum " enu ejhyutiyirikyunnavan avan tanne .
srtiikallill ninu janichaavarill yohannan sapakanekyall valiyavan aarum ejhyunnettidtilla ; sggrrajayttill eettvum cherriyavano avanilum valiyavan enu njan sataymayidtu ningallodu parrayunu .
yohannan sapakante nallukallmutall innevare sggrrajaytte balalkyaram cheyaunu ; balalkyarikall atine pidichaadakyunu .
sakalprvachakanmarum nayayaprmannavum yohannan vare prvachichau .
ningallkyu parigrhippan manassundekkill varuvanulleeliiyavu avan tanne .
kellppan cheviyullavar kellkydte .
ennall i talamurraye eetinodu upamikyendu ? chantasthlangallill irunu changatikallodu :
njangall ningallkyayi kujhyalooti , ningall nrattm cheytilla ; njangall vilapam padi , ningall marrattdichailla ; enu villichauparrayunnkudtikallodu atu tulaym .
yohannan tinukayum kudikyyum cheyaattvanayi vanu ; avanu bhootamundenu avar parrayunu .
manukshayputrn tinum kudichaum kondu vanu ; tinniyum kudiyanumaymanukshayn ; chukkkyarudeyum papikalludeyum senhitan enu avar parrayunu ; njanamo tante prvrattikallall niitiikarikyppedtirikyunu .
pinne avan tante viiyaaarprvrattikall mikytum nadannpadtnnangall manasantarappedaykayall avaye shasichautudangi ;
korasiine , ninakyu hkashtam ; betsayide , ninakyu hkashtam ; ningallill nadannviiyaarprvrattikall sorilum siidonilum nadannirunu ekkill avar pandu tanne radtilum venniirrilum manasantarappedumayirunu .
ennall nayayavidhidivasattill ningallekyall sorinum siidonum sahikyavatakum enu njan ningallodu parrayunu .
niiyo kaphannarhoome , sggrttollam uyannaririkyumo ? nii patallamvare tannupokum ; ninnill nadannviiyaar prvrattikall sodomill nadannirunu ekkill atu inuvare nilkyumayirunu .
ennall nayayavidhidivasattill ninnekyall sodomayrude nadtinu sahikyavatakum enu njan ningallodu parrayunu .
asamayattu tanne yeshu parranjtu : pitave , sggrttinum bhoomikyum kattravayullove , nii itu njanikallkyum vivekikallkyum marrechau shishukyllkyu vellippeduttiyatukondu njan ninne vajhyttunu .
ate , pitave , inganeyalelninakyu prsadam tonniyatu :
ente pitavu sakalavum ekkll bharamelpichairikyunu ; pitavallate aarum putrne arriyunnilla ; putrnum putrn vellippeduttikyoduppan ichchikyunnavanum allate aarum pitavine arriyunnatumillal .
addhvanikyunnavarum bharam chumakyunnavarum aayullore , ellavarum ente adukyll varuvin ; njan ningalle aashsippikyum .
njan semaytayum tyum ullavan aakayall ente nukam eettukondu ennodu patthippin ; ennall ningallude aatmakyllkyu aashasam kandettum .
ente nukam mraduvum ente chumadu laghuvum aakunu .
akalattu yeshu shabaattill villabhoomiyill koodi kadanupoyi ; avante shikshaynmar vishannidtu katir parrichau tinutudangi .
pariishar atu kandidtu : ita , shabaattill vihitamallatttu ninte shikshaynmar cheyaunu enu avanodu parranju .
avan avarodu parranjtu :
daviid tanikyum koodeyullavakyrum vishannappoll cheyattu entu ? avan daivalayattill chenu , purohitanmakyur matrmallate tanikyum koodeyullavakyrum tinman vihitamallatt kyappm tinu enu ningall vayichaidtillayo ?
alla , shabaattill purohitanmar daivalayattill vechau shabaattine lamghikyunu ekkilum kuttmillate irikyunu enu nayayaprmannattill vayichaidtillayo ?
ennall daivalayattekyall valiyavan ivide undu enu njan ningallodu parrayunu .
yagattilalla , karunnayill areta , njan prsadikyunu ennullatu entu enu ningall arrinjirunu ekkill kuttmillattvare kuttm vidhikyyillayirunu .
manukshay putrno shabaattinu kattravakunu .
avan avidam vidtu avarude palliyill chennappoll , kai varandoru manukshayne kandu .
avar avanill kuttm chumattendatinu shabaattill sekhaymakyunnatu vihitamo enu avanodu chodichau .
avan avarodu : ningallill oruttnu oru aadundu ennirikydte ; atu shabaattill kujhyiyill viinnall avan atine pidichau kayattukayillayo ?
ennall manukshayn aadinekyall etr vishekshatayullavan . aakayall shabaattill nanmcheyaunnatu vihitam tanne enu parranju .
pinne amanukshaynodu : kai niidtukenu parranju ; avan niidti , atu mattetupole sekhaymayi .
pariishanmaro purrappedtu avane nashippippan vendi avanu virodhamayi tammill aalochichau .
yeshu atu arrinjidtu avidam vidtupoyi , vallare per avantepinnale chenu ; avan avare okyeyum sekhaymakyi ,
tanne prsiddhmakyrutu enu avarodu apichau .
" ita , njan tiranjedutt ente dasan , ente ullam prsadikyunnente priyan ; njan ente aatmavine avante mell vekyum ; avan jatikallkyu nayayavidhi arriyikyum .
avan kalahikyyilla , nilavillikyyilla ; aarum terukyllill avante shabdam kellkyyumillal .
chatanj oadavan odichaukallakayilla ; pukayunntiri keduttukallakayilla ; avan nayayavidhi jayattollam nadattum .
avante namattill jatikall prtayashavekyum "
enningane yeshayaaprvachakanmukhantaram arullicheeytatu nivrattiaakuvan samgativanu .
anantaram chilar kurudanum umanumayoru bhootagrsatne avante adukyll konduvanu ; uman samsarikyyum kannkkyum cheyvan takyvannm avan avane sekhaymakyi .
puruksharam okyeyum visyichau : ivan daviidputrn tanneyo enu parranju .
atu kedtidtu pariishanmar : ivan bhootangallude talavanaybeyeeboolinekyondallate bhootangalle purrattakyunnillenu parranju .
avan avarude niroopannam arrinju avarodu parranjtu : oru rajaym tannill tanne chidrichau ekkill shoonaymakum ;
oru padtnnamo grahamo tannill tanne chidrichau ekkill nilanilkyyilla . sattan sattane purrattakyunuvekkill avan tannill tanne chidrichau poyalela ; pinne avante rajaym engane nilanilkyum ?
njan beyeeboolinekyondu bhootangalle purrattakyunu ekkill , ningallude makyll aarekyondu purrattakyunu ? atukondu avar ningallkyu nayayadhipanmar aakum .
daivatmavinall njan bhootangalle purrattakyunu ekkilo daivarajaym ningallude adukyll vannettiyirikyunu spashtam .
balavane pidichau kedtiidtllate balavante viidtill kadanu avante koppu kavanurkallavan engane kajhyiyum ? pidichau kedtiyall pinne avante viidu kavachaar cheyaam .
enikyu anukoolamallattvan enikyu prtikoolam aakunu ; ennodukoode chekyrattvan chitarrikyunu .
atukondu njan ningallodu parrayunnatu : sakalapapavum dookshannavum manukshayrodu kshamikyum ; aatmavinu nereyulldookshannamo kshamikyyillal .
aarekkilum manukshayputrnu nere oru vakyu parranjall atu avanodu kshamikyum ; parishuddhatmvinu nere parranjalo i lokattilum varuvanullatilum avanodu kshamikyyillal .
onnukill vraksham nallatu , phalavum nallatu enu veppin ; allaykill vraksham chiitt , phalavum chiitt enu veppin ; phalam kondalelvraksham arriyunnatu .
sappr santatikalle , ningall dushtarayirikye nallatu samsarippan engane kajhyiyum ? hradayam nirranju kaviyunnatill ninnalelvay samsarikyunnatu .
nallmanukshayn tante nallnikshepattillninu nallatu purrappeduvikyunu ; dushtamanukshayn dunnarikshepattillninu tiiyatu purrappeduvikyunu ;
ennall manukshayr parrayunneetu nissaravakyinum nayayavidhidivasattill kannakyu bodhippikyendivarum enu njan ningallodu parrayunu .
ninte vakyukallall niitikarikyppedukayum ninte vakyukallall kuttm vidhikyppedukayum cheyaum .
appoll shasrtimarilum pariishanmarilum chilar avanodu : guro , nii oru adayallam cheyatukanman njangall ichchikyunu enu parranju . avan avarodu uttram parranjtu :
dokshavum vaybhicharavumulltalamurradayallam tirayunu ; yonaprvachakante adayallamallate atinu adayallam labhikyyillal .
yonkadalanayude vayattill moonu ravum moonu pakalum irunnatupole manukshayputrn moonu ravum moonu pakalum bhoomiyude ullill irikyum .
niinevekyar nayayavidhiyill i talamurrayodu onnichau ejhyunnettu atine kuttm vidhikyum ; avar yonayude prsamgam kedtu manasantarappedtu valela ; ita , ivide yonayilum valiyavan .
tekye ri nayayavidhiyill i talamurrayodu onnichau uyitterjhyunnettu atine kuttm vidhikyum ; avall shalomonte njanam kellppan bhoomiyude arrutikallill ninnu vannuvalela ; ivide ita , shalomonilum valiyavan .
ashuddhatmavu oru manukshayne vidtu purrappedtsheksham niirillatt sthlangallillkoodi tannuppu anevkshichaukondu sanchrikyunu ; kandettunnillatanum .
njan purrappedtuponnente viidtilekyu madangicheellum enu avan parrayunu ; udane vanu atu ojhyinjtum adichauvari alakkrichaatumayi kannunu .
pinne avan purrappedtu , tannilum dushtatayerriyverre eejhyu aatmakylle koodtikyonduvarunu ; amanukshaynte pinnatte sthiti mumbilatte tilum vallate aakum ; i dushtatalamurrekyum angane bhavikyum .
avan puruksharattodu samsarichaukondirikyyill avante ammyum sahodaranmarum avanodu samsarippan aagrhichau purrattu ninu .
oruttn avanodu : ninte ammyum sahodaranmarum ninnodu samsarippan aagrhichau purrattu nilkyunu enu parranju .
atuparranjvanodu avan : ente amm aar ente sahodaranmar aar enu chodichau .
shikshaynmarude nere kai niidti : ita , ente ammyum ente sahodaranmarum .
sggrsthnayente pitavinte ishtam cheyaunnavan ente sahodaranum sahodariyum ammyum akunu enu parranju .
anu yeshu viidtillninu purrappedtu kadalarike irunu .
vallare puruksharam avante adukyn vanu koodukakondu avan padakill kayarri irunu ; puruksharam ellam karayill irunu .
avan avarodu palatum upamakallayi prsatavichaatentennall ; vitekyunnavan viteppan purrappedtu .
vitekyuboll chilatu vajhyiyarike viinnu ; parravakall vanu atu tinu kallanju .
chilatu parrasthlattu eerre mannillatt idattu viinnu ; manninu tyillaykayall kshannattill mullechauvanu .
sooyaarn udichaarre choodutadti , ver illaykayall atu unnangippoyi .
mattuchilatu mullinnidayill viinnu ; mullu mullechau vallanur atine njerukyikyllanju .
mattuchilatu nallnilattu viinnu , noorrum arrupatum mupptum meniyayi villanju .
cheviyullavan kellkydte .
pinne shikshaynmar adukye vanu : avarodu upamakallayi samsarikyunnatu entu enu avanodu chodichau .
avan avarodu uttram parranjtu : sggrrajayttinte mammrngalle arrivan ningallkyu varam labhichairikyunu ; avakyerlabhichaidtillal .
ullavanu kodukyum ; avanu samraddhiyundakum ; illattvnodo avanullatum koode eduttukallayum .
atukondu avar kandidtu kannateyum kedtidtu kellkyateyum grhikyateyum irikyyall njan upamakallayi avarodu samsarikyunu .
" ningall cheviyall kellkyum grhikyyilltanum ; kannall kannum dasharikyyilltanum . i janattinte hradayam tadichairikyunu ; avar chevikondu mandmayi kellkyunu ; kannu adechairikyunu ; avar kannu kannateyum chevi kellkyateyum hradayamkondu grhikyateyum tirinju kollateyum njan avare sekhaymakyateyum irikyendatinu tanne . "
enu yeshayaavu parranj prvachakattinu avarill nivratti varunu .
ennall ningallude kannu kannunnatu kondum ningallude chevi kellkyunnatu kondum bhagaymullava .
eerriyprvachakanmarum niitimanmarum ningall kannunnatu kanman aagrhichaidtum kandill ningall kellkyunnatu kellppan aagrhichaidtum kedtillenu njan sataymayidtu ningallodu parrayunu .
ennall vitekyunnavante upamkedtukollvin .
oruttn rajayttinte vachanam kedtidtu grhikyanjall dushtan vanu avante hradayattill vitekyppedttu eduttukallayunu ; itaretvajhyiyarike vitekyppedttu .
parrsthlattu vitekyppedtto , oruttn vachanam kedtidtu udane santokshattode kaikyollunnatu aakunu . ekkilum verillatirikyyall avan kshannikanareta .
vachanam timittm njerukymo upadrvamo neridtall avan kshannattill idarrippokunu .
mullinnidayill vitekyppedtto , oruttn vachanam kellkyunu ekkilum ilokattinte chintayum dhanattinte vanchnayum vachanatte njerukyiidtu nikshphalanayi tiirunnatakunu .
nallanilattu vitekyppedtto oruttn vachanam kedtu grhikyunnatu aakunnu ; atu villanju noorrum arrupatum mupptum meni nalkunnu .
avan mattoru upamavakyru parranju koduttu : sggrrajaym oru manukshayn tante nilattu nallvittu vitechaatinodu sadrashamakunu .
manukshayr urranguboll avante shatru vanu , kotambinte idayill kallvitechau poykyllanju .
njarru vallanur katirayappoll kallayum kannayvanu .
viidtudayavante dasanmar avante adukyll chenu : yajamanane , vayalill nallvittllayo vitechaatu ? pinne kallevideninu vanu enu chodichau .
itu shatru cheyattakunu enu avan avarodu parranju . njangall poyi atu parrichaukoodtuvan sammtamundo enu dasanmar avanodu chodichau .
itinu avan : illa , pakshe kallparrikyuboll kotambum koode pijhyutu pokum randum koode koyttollam vallaradte ;
koyttu kalattu njan koyaunnavarodu mube kallparrichau koodti chudtukallayendatinu kedtukallayi kedtuvanum kotambu ente kallappurayill koodtiveppanum kalpikyum enu parranju .
mattoru upamavan avakyru parranju koduttu : sggrrajaym kadukumanniyodu sadrasham ; atu oru manukshayn eduttu tante vayalill idtu .
atu ellvittilum cherriyatekkilum vallanur sasayngallill eettvum valutayi , aakashattile parravakall vanu atinte kombukallill vasippan takyvannm vrakshamayi tiirunu .
avan mattoru upamavarodu parranju : sggrrajaym pullichamavinodu sadrasham ; atu oru satii eduttu moonu parrmavill ellam pullichauvaruvollam adakyivechau .
itu okyeyum yeshu puruksharattodu upamakallayi parranju ; upamkoodate avarodu onum parranjillal .
" njan upamprsatavippan vay turrakyum ; lokasthapanam mutall gooddhamayatu uchaarikyum " enu prvachakan parranjtu nivrattiyakuvan samgativanu .
anantaram yeshu puruksharatte parranjyachaidtu viidtill vanu , shikshaynmar avante adukyll chenu : vayalile kallayude upamtelliyichau tarennam enu apekshichau .
atinu avan uttram parranjtu : nallvittu vitekyunnavan manukshay putrn ; vayall lokam ;
nallvittu rajayttinte putrnmar ; kalldushtante putrnmar ;
atu vitechashatru pishachu ; koyttu lokavasanam ; koyaunnavar dootanmar .
kallkoodti tiiyill idtu chudumpole lokavasanattill sambhavikyum .
manukshayputrn tante dootanmare ayakyum ;
avar avante rajayttill ninu ellidachaarkalleyum adhammrrrrm prvattrikyunnavareyum koodticheettru tiichaoollayill idtukallakayum , avide karachaalum pallu kadiyum undakum .
anu niitimanmar tangallude pitavinte rajayttill sooyaarne ppole prkashikyum . cheviyullavan kellkydte .
sggrrajaym vayalill ollichauvechanidhiyodu sadrasham . atu oru manukshayn kandu marrechaidtu , tante santokshattall chenu tanikyullatokyeyum vittu avayall vangi .
pinneyum sggrrajaym nallmuttu anevkshikyunnoru vayapariyodu sadrasham .
avan vilayerriyoru muttu kandettiyarre chenu tanikyullatokyeyum vittu atu vangi .
pinneyum sggrrajaym kadalill idunnatum ellavakmiinum pidikyunnatumayoru valayodu sadrasham .
nirranjppoll avar atu valichau karekyu kayatti , , irunukondu nallatu patrngallill koodtivechau , chiitt errinju kallanju .
angane tanne lokavasanattill sambhavikyum : dootanmar purrappedtu niitimanmarude idayill ninu dushtanmare vertirichau tiichaoollayill idtu kallayum ;
avide karachaalum pallukadiyum undakum .
itellam grhichauvo ? ennatinu avar uvau enu parranju .
avan avarodu : atukondu sggrrajayttinu shikshaynayi ttiinnar eetu shasrtiyum tante nikshepattill ninu putiyatum pajhyayatum eduttu kodukyunnoru viidtudayavanodu sadrashanakunu enu parranju .
i upamakalle parranju tiinnarsheksham yeshu avidam vidtu tante pitranagarattill vanu , avarude palliyill avakyru upadeshichau .
avar visyichau : ivanu i njanavum viiyaarprvrattikallum evideninu ?
ivan tachaante makan allayo ? ivante amm marriyennavallallayo ? ivante sahodaranmar yakyob , yose , shimon , yoodennavar allayo ?
ivante sahodarikallum ellam nammodu koode illayo ? ivanu itu okyeyum evide ninu enu parranju avakkll idarrippoyi .
yeshu avarodu : oru prvachakan tante pitranagarattilum sntabhavanattilum allate bahumanmillattvan allenu parranju .
avarude avishasam nimittm avide vallare viiyaar prvrattikalle cheyatilla .
akalattu idaprbhuvayherodavu yeshuvinte shruti kedtidtu :
avan yohannan sapakan ; avan marichaavarude idayill ninu uyittru ; atukondakunu i shtikall avanill vayaparikunnatu enu tante bhrataynmarodu parranju .
herodavu tante sahodaranayphiilipposinte bhayaar heroday nimittm , avall ninakyu bhayaaryayirikyunnatu vihitamallenu yohannan avanodu parranjtukondu tanne ,
avane pidichau kedti tadavill aakyiyirunu .

ennall herodavinte janandivasam aayappoll herodayyude makall sabhamaddhey nrattm cheyatu herodavine prsadippichau .

avall ammyude upadeshprkaram : yohannan sapakante taloru talattill tarennam enu parranju .
rajavu du : khichau ekkilum cheyat sataytteyum virunukareyum vicharichau atu koduppan kalpichau ;
aallayachau tadavill yohannane shirachedam cheyaichau .

atu kedtidtu yeshu avidam vidtu padakill kayarri nijjarnamayoru sthlattekyu verridtu vangippoyi ; puruksharam atu kedtu padtnnangallill ninu kallnadayayi avante pinnale chenu .
avan vanu valiypuruksharatte kandu avarill manasslinju avarude rogikalle sekhaymakyi .
vaikunneramayappoll shikshaynmar avante adukyll chennu : i sthlam marubhoomiyalela , neravum vaiki ; puruksharam gramangallill poyi bhakshannasadhanangall kollendatinu avare parranjyakyennam enu parranju .
yeshu avarodu : avar pokuvan aavashaymilla ; ningall avarkyu bhakshippan koduppin enu parranju .
avar avanodu : anchu appvum randu miinum allate njangallkyu ivide onum illenu parranju .
atu ingu kondu varuvin enu avan parranju .
pinne puruksharam pullin mell irippan kalpichau ; anchu appvum randu miinum eduttu , sggrttekyu nokyi vajhytti , appm nurrukyi , shikshaynmarude pakylum shikshaynmar puruksharattinum koduttu .
ellavarum tinu trapatrayi ; shekshichakakshannam pantrndu kodt nirracheeduttu .
tinnavaro srtiikalleyum paitangalleyum koodate eekadesham ayaayiram purukshanmar aayirunu .
udane yeshu tan puruksharatte parranjyakyunnatinnidayill shikshaynmar padakill kayarri , tanikyu mumbayi akyrekyu pokuvan avare nibaarndichau .
avan puruksharatte parranjyachaidtu pratthrippan taniye malayill kayarrippoyi ; vaikunneram aayappoll eekanayi avide irunu .
padako karavidtu palnajhyikdoorattayi , kattu prtikoolamakakondu tirakallall valanjirunu .
ratriyile nalam yamattill avan kadalinmell nadanu avarude adukyll vanu .
avan kadalinmell nadakyunnatu kandidtu shikshaynmar bhrmichau : atu oru bhootam enu parranju pedichau nilavillichau .
udane yeshu avarodu : dhaiyaarppeduvin ; njan aakunu ; pedikyendenu parranju . " njan idayane vedtum aadukall chitarrippokum " enu ejhyutiyirikyunuvalela .
atinu paretas : kattrave , nii aakunu ekkill njan vellattinmell ninte adukye varendatinu kalpikyennam enu parranju .
varikenu avan parranju . paretas padakill ninu irrangi , yeshuvinte adukyll chelluvan vellattinmell nadanu .
ennall avan kattu kandu pedichau mungittudangukayall ; kattrave , enne rakshikyenname enu nilavillichau .

avar padakill kayarriyappoll kattu amanur .
padakilullavar : nii daivaputrn sataym enu parranju avane namaskarichau . vayakulappeduvanum tudangi :
avar akyreyetti , gennesaret deshattu chenu .

ninte shikshaynmar poovaarnmarude sabrdayam lamghikyunnatu entu ? avar bhakshikyuboll kai kajhyukunnillalelenu parranju .
avan avarodu uttram parranjtu : ningallude sabrdayam kondu ningall daivkalpanlamghikyunnatu entu ?
appneyum ammyeyum bahumaniky enum appneyo ammyeyo dookshikyunnavan marikyennam enum daivam kalpichauvalela .
ningallo oruttn appnodu ekkilum ammyodu ekkilum : ninakyu ennall upakaramayi varendatu vajhyipadu enu parranjall avan appne bahumanikyendenu parrayunu ;
ingane ningallude sabrdayattall ningall daivvachanatte dubaaarlamakyiyirikyunu .
kapadbhtikyare , ningallekyurrichau yeshayaavu :
" i janam adharam kondu enne bahumanikyunu ; ekkilum avarude hradayam enne vidtu akannirikyunu .
manukshkalpanakallayupadeshangalle avar patthippikyunnatu kondu enne vaytthrmayi bhajikyunu . " enningane prvachichaatu ottirikyunu .
pinne avan puruksharatte arike villichau avarodu parranjtu : kedtu grhichau kollvin ,
manukshaynu ashuddhi varuttunnatu vayikykattu chellunnatalla , vayill ninu purrappedunnatareta ; atu manukshayne ashuddhmakyunu .
appoll shikshaynmar adukye vanu : pariishanmar i vakyu kedtu idarrippoyi enu arriyunnuvo enu chodichau .
atinu avan : sggrsthnayente pitavu nadtidtillatt tai okyeyum verode parrinju pokum .
avare viduvin ; avar kurudanmarayvajhyikadtikall areta ; kurudan kurudane vajhyi nadattiyall iruvarum kujhyiyill viijhyum enu uttram parranju .
paretas avanodu : upamnjangallkyu telliyichau tarennam enu parranju .
atinu avan parranjtu : ningallum inuvare bodhamillattvaro ?
vayikykattu kadakyunnatellam vayattill chennidtu marrappurayill pokunu enu grhikyunnillayo ?
vayill ninu purrappedunnato hradayattill ninu varunu ; atu manukshayne ashuddhmakyunu .
enganeyennall duschinta , kulapatakam , vaybhicharam , parasamgam , mokshannam , kallssakshaym , dookshannam innivhradayattill ninu purrappedtu varunu .
manukshayne ashuddhmakyunnatu itareta ; kajhyukatt kai kondu bhakshikyunnato manukshayne ashuddhmakyunnillal .
yeshu avidam vidtu , sor siidon ennprdeshangallilekyu vangi ppoyi .
adeshattu ninu oru kananaysrtii vanu , avanodu : kattrave , daviiduputra , ennodu karunntonnenname ; ente makallkyu bhootopadrvam katthinamayirikyunu enu nilvillichau parranju .
avan avallodu oru vakyum uttram parranjilla ; avante shikshaynmar adukye vanu : avall nammude pinnale nilvillichau kondu varunu ; avalle parranjyakyenname enu avanodu apekshichau .
atinu avan : yisrayell grahattile kannate poyaadukallude adukylekyllate enne ayachaidtillenu uttram parranju .
ennall avall vanu : kattrave , enne sahayikyenname enu parranju avane namaskyrichau .
avano : makyllude appm eduttu naykyudtikallkyu idtu kodukyunnatu nannallenu uttram parranju .
atinu avall : ate , kattrave , naykyudtikallum udayavarude meshayill ninu viijhyunnnurrukyukall tinunundalellenu parranju .
srtiiye , ninte vishasam valiyatu ; ninte ishtam pole ninakyu bhavikydte enu parranju . anajhyikmutall avallude makallkyu sekhaym vanu .
yeshu avide ninu yatryayi galiilakydalarike chenu malayill kayarri avide irunu .
vallare puruksharam mudantar , kurudar , umar , koonar mutalaypalareyum avante adukyll konduvanu avante kalkyll vechau ; avan avare sekhaymakyi ;
umar samsarikyunnatum koonar sekhaymakunnatum mudantar nadakyunnatum kurudar kannunnatum puruksharam kandidtu arayppedtu , yisrayelinte daivatte mahat ppedutti .
ennall yeshu tante shikshaynmare adukye villichau : i puruksharam ippoll moonu nallayi ennodu koode pakyrunu ; avakyru bhakshippan onum illaykkondu avare kyurrichau enikyu manasslivu tonunu ; avare padtinniyayi vidtyappan manassumilla ; avar vajhyiyill vechau tallanurpoyekyum enu parranju .
shikshaynmar avanodu : itr valiypuruksharattinu trapati varuttuvan matiyayappm i kadtill namukyu evide ninu enu parranju .
ningallude pakyll etr appm undu enu yeshu chodichau ; eejhyu ; kurre cherrumiinum undu enu avar parranju .
avan puruksharattodu nilattu irippan kalpichau ,
aeejhyu appvum miinum eduttu vajhytti nurrukyi shikshaynmarude pakylum shikshaynmar paruksharattinum koduttu .
ellavarum tinu trapatrayi ; shekshichakakshannam avar eejhyu vadti nirrecheeduttu .
tinnavaro srtiikalleyum paitangalleyum koodate nalayiram purukshanmar aayirunu .
panne avan puraksharatte parranjyachaidtu padakill kayarri magadadeshattu etti .

aakashattinte bhavam vivechippan ningall arriyunu ; ennall kallakshannangalle vivechippan kajhyikayillayo ?

shikshaynmar akyre pokuboll appm eduppan marranu poyi .
ennall yeshu avarodu : nokyuvin ; pariishanmarudeyum sadookayrudeyum pullichamavu sookshichaukollvin enu parranju .
appm konduporaykayall aayirikyum enu avar tammill tammill parranju .
atu arrinjidtu yeshu parranjtu : alpavishasikalle , appm kondu varaykayall tammill tammill parrayunnatu entu ?

angane appttinte pullichamavalla , pariishanmarudeyum sadookayrudeyum upadeshamaretsookshichau kollvan avan parranju enu avar grhichau .

ningallo enne aar enu parrayunu enu avan chodichaatinu shimon paretas :
nii jiivanulldaivattinte putrnaykrisatu enu uttram parranju .

nii paretas aakunu ; i parrmell njan ente sabhaye panniyum , patallagopurangall atine jayiky yillenu njan ninnodu parrayunu .
sggrrajayttinte takyoll njan ninakyu tarunu ; nii bhoomiyill kedtunnatu okyeyum sggrttill kedtppedtirikyum ; nii bhoomiyill ajhyikyunnatu okyeyum sggrttill ajhyinjirikyum enu uttram parranju .
pinne tan krisatu aakunu enu aarodum parrayarutu enu kalpichau .
anu mutall yeshu tan yerooshalemill chennidtu , mooppnmar , mahapurohitanmar , shasrtimar ennivarall palatum sahichau kollappedukayum moonnamnall uyitterjhyunnelkyyum vendatu enu shikshaynmarodu prsatavichau tudangi .

aarekkilum tante jiivane rakshippan ichchichaall atine kallayum ; ente nimittm aarekkilum tante jiivane kallanjall atine kandettum .
oru manukshayn savaarlokavum nediidtum tante jiivane nashtappeduttiyall avanu entu pryojanam ? alla , tante jiivane viindu kollvan manukshayn entu marru vilkodukyum ?

arentayas , philippos batteralomayi , mattayi , tomas , alphayiyude makanayyakyob , tadtayi , kananaynayshimon ,

avan avare adukye villichau upamakallall avarodu parranjtu : sattanu sattane engane purrattakyuvan kajhyiyum ?
oru rajaym tannilltanne chidrichau ekkill arajayttinu nilanilpan kajhyikayilla .
oru viidu tannilltanne chidrichau ekkill aviidtinu nilanilppan kajhyikayilla .
sattan tannodutanne etittru chidrichau ekkill avanu nilanilppan kajhyivilla ; avante avasanam vanu .
balavane pidichau kedtiidtllate avante viidtillkadanu avante koppu kavanurkallavan aakyrum kajhyikayilla ; pidichau kedtiyall pinne avante viidu kavachaarcheyaam .

avanu oru ashuddhatmavu undu enu avar parranjirunu .
anantaram avante ammyum sahodaranmarum vanu purrattu ninu avane villippan aallayachau .
puruksharam avante chuttum irunnirunu ; avar avanodu : ninte ammyum sahodaranmarum purrattuninu ninne anevkshikyunu enu parranju .
avan avarodu : ente ammyum sahodaranmarum aar enu parranjidtu
chuttilum irikyunnavare nokyikyondu : ente ammyum sahodaranmarum ita .
daivattinte ishtam cheyaunnavan tanne ente sahodaranum sahodariyum ammyum aakunu enu parranju .
avan pinneyum kadallkyrevechau upadeshippan tudangi . appoll eettvum valiypuruksharam avante adukyll vanu koodukakondu avan padakill kshayarri kadalill irunu ; puruksharam okyeyum kadalarike karayill aayirunu .
avan upamakallall avare palatum upadeshichau , upadeshattill avarodu parranjtu : kellppin ;
vitekyunnavan viteppan purrappedtu .
vitekyuboll chilatu vajhyiyarike viinnu ; parravakall vanu atu tinu kallanju .
mattuchilatu parrasthlattu eerre mannillattedattu viinnu ; manninu t illaykayall kshannattill mullechau vanu .
sooyaarn udichaarre choodutadti , verillaykakondu unnangippoyi :
mattu chilatu mullallinidayill viinnu ; mullallu mullechau vallanur atine njerukyikyllanju ; atu villanjtumilla .
mattu chilatu nallamannill viinnidtu mullechau vallanur phalam koduttu ; mupptum arrupatum noorrum meni villanju .
kellppan chevi ullallavan kellkydte enum avan parranju .
anantaram avan tanichairikyuboll avanodukoodeyullallvar pantiruvarumayi upamakallekyurrichau chodichau .
avan avarodu parranjtu : daivarajayttinte mammrm ningallkyu nalkappedtirikyunu ; purrattullallavakyersakalavum upamakallall labhikyunu .
avar manam tiriyateyum avarodu kshamikyateyum irikyttkyvannm avar kandidtum arriyatirippanum kedtidtum grhikyatirippanum samgati varum .
pinne avan avarodu parranjtu : i upamgrhikyunnillayo ? pinne matte upamakall okyeyum engane grhikyum .
vitekyunnavan vachanam vitekyunu .
vachanam vitechaidtu vajhyiyarike viinnatu , kedt udane sattan vanu hradayangallill vitekyppedt vachanam eduttukallayunnatakunu .
angane tanne parrasthlattu vitechaatu vachanam kedt udane santokshattode kaikyollallunnavar ;
ekkilum avar ullallill verillate kshannikanmar aakunu ; vachanam nimittm upadrvamo piiddhayo undakayall kshannattill idarrippokunu .
mullallinnidayill vitekyppedtto vachanam kedtidtu
ihalokattinte chintakallum dhanattinte vanchnayum mattu vikshaymohangallum akattu kadanu , vachanatte njerukyi nikshphalamakyi tiikyrunnatakunu .
nallamannill vitekyppedtto vachanam kellkyyum amgiikarikyyum cheyaunnavar tanne ; avar mupptum arrupatum noorrum meni villayunu .

ningall kellkyunnatu entu enu sookshichaukollvin ; ningall allakyunnallavukondu ningallkyum allanukidtum ; adhikamayum kidtum .
ullallavanu kodukyum ; illattvanodo ullallatumkoode eduttukallayum enu avan avarodu parranju .
pinne avan parranjtu : daivarajaym oru manukshayn mannill vittu errinjsheksham
ravum pakalum urrangiyum ejhyunnettum irikye avan arriyate vittu mullechau vallarunnatupole aakunu .
bhoomi syamayi mube njarrum pinne katirum pinne katirill nirranj manniyum ingane villayunu .

atu kadukumanniyodu sadrasham ; atine mannill vitekyu boll bhoomiyile ellavittilum cherriyatu .

avar vallare bhayappedtu : kattum kadalum koode ivane anusarikyunuvalela ; ivan aar enu tammill parranju .
avar kadalinte akyre gadaradeshattu etti .
padakillninu irrangiyudane ashuddhatmavullalloru manukshayn kallarrakallill ninu vanu avane etirettu .
avante pappru kallarrakallill aayirunu ; aakyrrum avane changalakondupolum bandichaukoodanju .

avan yeshuvine doorattuninu kandidtu oadicheenu avane namaskyrichau .

ashuddhatmave , i manukshayne vidtu purrappedtupokenu yeshu kalpichairunu .
ninte perentu enu avanodu chodichaatinu : ente per legeyan ; njangall palar aakunu enu avan uttram parranju ;
nadtillninu tangalle ayachaukallayatirippan eerriyonu apekshichau .
avide malayarike oru valiypannikyoodtm menjukondirunu .
apannikallill kadakyendatinu njangalle ayakyennam enu avar avanodu apekshichau :
avan anuvadam koduttu ; ashuddhatmakyll purrappedtu pannikallill kadannidtu koodtm kaduntookyttoode kadalilekyu panju viippru mudti chattu . aveekadesham randayiram aayirunu .
pannikalle meykyunnavar oadicheenu padtnnattilum nadtilum arriyichau : sambhavichaatu kanman palarum purrappedtu ,
yeshuvinte adukyll vanu , legeyan undayirunnbhootagrsatn vasrtm dharichaum subodham poondum irikyunnatu kandu bhayappedtu .

appoll avar avanodu tangallude atirvidtu pokuvan apekshichautudangi .

avan poyi yeshu tanikyu cheyattokyeyum dekyeppolinadtill ghokshichau tudangi ; ellavarum ayaarppedukayum cheyatu .
yeshu viindum padakukayarri ikyre kadanu kadalarike irikyuboll valiypuruksharam avante adukyll vanu koodi .

ente kunjumakall atayasanattill irikyunu ; avall rakshappedtu jiivikyendatinu nii vanu avallude mell kai vekyenname enu vallare apekshichau .

avano atu cheyatvalle kanman chuttum nokyi .

avan ellavareyum purrattakyi kudtiyude appneyum ammyeyum tannodukoodeyullallavareyum koodtikondu kudti kidakyunnidattuchenu

avan eeliyavakunu enu mattuchilar parranju , verre chilar : avan prvachakanmarill oruttneppole oru prvachakan enu parranju .
atu herodavu kedtarre : njan talavedtichayohannan aakunu avan : avan uyitterjhyunnettirikyunu enu parranju .
herodtante sahodaranayphiilipposinte bhayaaar herodayye parigrhichaatukondu avallnimittm aallayachau , yohannane pidichau tadavilakyiyirunu .
sahodarante bhayaarye parigrhikyunnatu ninakyu vihitamallenu yohannan herodavodu parranjirunu .
herodayyo avante nere pakavechau avane kolluvanum ichchichau ; sadhichaillatanum .
yohannan niitiyum vishuddhiyumullallpurukshan enu herodavu arrinju avane bhayappedukayum avane kattukollkayum cheyatu ; avante vachanam kedtidtu vallare kalangiyekkilum santokshattode kedtuponu .
ennall herodavu tante jananotsavattill tante mahattukyllkyum sahasradhipanmakyrum galiilayile prmannikallkyum virunu kajhyichaappoll oru taram vanu .
herodayyude makall akattu chenu nrattmcheyatu herodavineyum virunukareyum prsadippichasamayam : manassullallatu entekkilum ennodu chodichaukollka ; ninakyu taram enu rajavu balayodu parranju .

udane rajavu oru akambadiye ayachau , avante talkonduvaruvan kalpichau .

vaikunneram aayappoll padaku kadalinte naduvilum tan eekanayi karayilum aayirunu .

pariishanmarum yehoodanmar okyeyum poovaarnmarude sabrdayam prmannichau kai nannayi kajhyukiidtllate bhakshannam kajhyikyyilla .
chantayillninu varubojhyum kullichaidtllate bhakshannam kajhyikyyilla . panapatrm , bharanni chembu ennivkajhyukukmutalayi palatum prmannikyunnatu avakyru chadtmayirikyunu .
angane pariishanmarum shasrtimarum : ninte shikshaynmar poovaaarnmarude sabrdayam anusarichau nadakyate shuddhiyillatt kaikondu bhakshannam kajhyikyunnatu entu enu avanodu chodichau .
avan avarodu uttram parranjtu : kapadabhtikyarayningallekyurrichau yeshayaavu prvachichaatu shari : " i janam adharamkondu enne bahumanikyunu ; ekkilum avarude hradayam ekkllninu doorattu akannirikyunu .
manukshakalpanakallayupadeshangalle avar upadeshikyunnatu kondu enne vaytthrmayi bhajikyunu . " enu ejhyutiyirikyunnatupole tanne .
ningall daivakalpanvidtumkallanju manukshayrude sabrdayam prmannikyunu ;
pinne avarodu parranjtu : ningallude sabrdayam prmannippan vendi ningall daivakalpantallallikyllayunnatu nannayi .
ninte appneyum ammyeyum bahumaniky enum appneyo ammyeyo prakunnavan marikyennam enum moshe parranjuvalela .
ningallo oru manukshayn : appnodo ammyodo : ninakyu ennall upakaramayi varendatu vajhyipadu ennatthrmullallkobaaran enu parranjall mati enu parrayunu ;
tante appnno ammkyo melall onum cheyvan avane sammtikyunnatumillal .
ingane ningall upadeshikyunnsabrdayattall daivkalpandubaarlamakyunu ; i vakpalatum ningall cheyaunu .
pinne avan puruksharatte arike villichau avarodu : ellavarum kedtu grhichaukollvin .

( kellppan chevi ullallavan kellkydte ) enu parranju .
avan puruksharattevidtu viidtillchennasheksham shikshaynmar upamayekyurrichau avanodu chodichau .
avan avarodu : ingane ningallum bodhamillattvaro ? purrattuninu manukshaynte akattuchellunnyatonninum avane ashuddhmakyuvan kajhyikayillenu tirichaarriyunni llayo ?
atu avante hradayattill allvayattilaretchellunnatu ; pinne marrappurayilekyu pokunu ; ingane sakalabhojayngallkyum shuddhivaruttunu enu parranju .
manukshaynillninu purrappedunnataretmanukshayne ashuddhnkyunnatu ;
akattuninu , manukshayrude hradayattill ninu tanne , duschinta , vaybhicharam , parasamgam , kulapatakam ,
mokshannam , atayagrham , dushtata , chati , dukshkammrm , vidakyu kannu , dookshannam , ahakkaram , mooddhatennivpurrappedunu .
i dokshangall ellam akattuninu purrappedtu manukshayne ashuddhnakyunu enum avan parranju .
avan avideninu purrappedtu siidonteyum sorinteyum atirnadtill chenu oru viidtill kadanu ; aarum arriyarutu enu ichchichau ekkilum marranjirippan sadhichailla .
ashuddhatmavu badhichacherriymakall ullellaru srtii avante vasatutakedtidtu vanu avante kalkyll viinnu .
avall surrophoyiikayjatiyilullalloru yavanasrtii aayirunu ; tante makallillninu bhootattepurrattakyuvan avall avanodu apekshichau .
yeshu avallodu : mube makyllkyu trapativaradte ; makyllude appm eduttu cherrunaykyllkyu idtukodukyunnatu nannallenu parranju .
avall avanodu : ate , kattrave , cherrunaykyllum meshekyu kiijhye kudtikallude appnurrukyukalle tinunuvalelenu uttram parranju .
avan avallodu : i vakyunimittm poykyollk bhootam ninte makalle vidtu poyirikyunu enu parranju .
avall viidtill vannarre , makall kidakymell kidakyunnatum bhootam vidtupoyatum kandu .
avan viindum sorinte atirvidtu siidonvajhyiyayi dekyppolideshattinte naduvillkoodi galiilakydalpurrattu vanu .
avide avar vikynayoru chekidane avante adukyll konduvanu , avante mell kai vekyennam enu apekshichau .
avan avane puruksharattillninu verridtu koodtikyondu poyi avante cheviyill virall idtu , tuppi avante navine todtu ,
sggrttekyu nokyi neduviippridtu avanodu : turranu varikenu atthrmullallephathenu parranju .
udane avante chevi turranu navinte kedtum ajhyinjidtu avan shariyayi samsarichau .
itu aarodum parrayarutu enu avarodu kalpichau ekkilum avan etr kalpichauvo atryum avar prsiddhmakyi :
avan sakalavum nannayi cheyatu ; chekidare kellkyumarrakyunu ; umare samsarikyumarrakyunu enu parranju atayntam visyichau .
adivasangallill eettvum valiypuruksharam undayirikye avakyru bhakshippan onum illaykakondu yeshu shikshaynmare adukyll villichau avarodu :
i puruksharam ippoll moonunallayi ennodukoode pakyrunu ; avakyru bhakshippan onum illaykakondu enikyu avarodu alivu tonunu ;
njan avare padtinniyayi viidtilekyu ayachaall avar vajhyiyillvechau tallanurpokum ; avarill chilar doorattuninnu vannavaralelenu parranju .
atinu avante shikshaynmar : ivakyru ivide marubhoomiyill appm koduttu trapativaruttuvan engane kajhyiyum enu uttram parranju .
avan avarodu : ningallude pakyll etr appm undu enu chodichau . eejhyu enu avar parranju .
avan puruksharattodu nilattu irippan kalpichau ; pinne aeejhyappm eduttu setatrm cheyatu nurrukyi , shikshaynmarude pakyll villambuvan koduttu ; avar puruksharattinu villambi .
cherriyamiinum kurre undayirunu ; atum avan anugrhichaidtu , villambuvan parranju .
avar tinu trapatrayi ; shekshichakakshannangall eejhyuvadti nirracheeduttu .
avar eekadesham nalayiramper aayirunu .
avan avare parranjyachudane shikshaynmarodukoode padakill kayarri dalnoothamshangallill etti .
anantaram pariishanmar vanu avane pariikshichaukondu aakashattuninu oru adayallam anevkshichau avanumayi takyrichau tudangi .
avan aatmavill njarangi : i talamurradayallam anevkshikyunnatu entu ? i talamurrekyu adayallam labhikyyillenu njan sataymayidtu ningallodu parrayunu enu parranju .
avare vidtu pinneyum padaku kayarri akyrekyu kadanu .
avar appm kondupokuvan marranu poyirunu ; padakill avarude pakyll oru appm matrme undayirunnullallu .
avan avarodu : nokyuvin , pariisharude pullichaamavum herodavinte pullichaamavum sookshichau kollvin enu kalpichau .
namukyu appm illaykayall enu avar tammill tammill parranju .
atu yeshu arrinju avarodu parranjtu : appm illaykayall ningall tammill parrayunnatu entu ? ippojhyum tirichaarriyunnillayo ? grhikyunnillayo ? ningallude hradayam kaduttirikyunuvo ?
kannu undayidtum kannunnillayo ? chevi undayidtum kellkyunnillayo ? oakyrunnatumillayo ?
ayaayirampekyru njan anchppm nurrukyiyappoll kakshannangall etrkodt nirracheeduttu ? pantrndu enu avar avanodu parranju .
nalayiram pekyru eejhyu nurrukyiyappoll kakshannangall etr vadti nirracheeduttu ? eejhyu enu avar avanodu parranju .
pinne avan avarodu : ippojhyum ningall grhikyunnillayo enu parranju .
avar betsayidayill ettiyappoll oru kurudane avante adukyll konduvanu avane todennamenu apekshichau .
avan kurudante kaikyu pidichau avane urinu purrattu kondupoyi avante kannill tuppi avante mell kaivechau : nii vallatum kannunundo enu chodichau .
avan melepadtunokyi : njan manukshayre kannunu ; avar nadakyunnatu marangallpoleyaretkannunnatu enu parranju .
pinneyum avante kanninmell kaivechaarre avan sekhaym prapichau mijhyichaunokyi ellam spashtamayi kandu .
nii urill kadakypolum arutu enu avan parranju avane viidtilekyu ayachau .
anantaram yeshu shikshaynmarumayi philipposinte kaisayaarkyu adutt urukallilekyu poyi ; vajhyiyill vechau shikshaynmarodu : janangall enne aar enu parrayunu enu chodichau .
yohannan sapakanenu chilar , eeliiyavenu chilar , prvachakanmarill oruttn enu mattu chilar enu avar uttram parranju .
avan avarodu : ennall ningall enne aar enu parrayunu enu chodichaatinu : nii krisatu aakunu enu paretas uttram parranju .
pinne tannekyurrichau aarodum parrayarutenu avan avarodu khanditamayi parranju .
manukshayputrn palatum sahikyyum mooppnmarum mahapuro hitanmarum shasrtimarum avane tallallikyllanju kollukayum moonunall kajhyinjidtu avan uyitterjhyunne lkyyum vennam enu avare upadeshichautudangi .
avan i vakyu turranu parranju . appoll paretas avane verridtukondupoyi shasichautudangi ;
avano tirinjunokyi shikshaynmare kandidtu paretasine shasichau : sattane , enne vidtupo ; nii daivattintetallmanukshayrudetaretkarutunnatu enu parranju .
pinne avan puruksharatteyum tante shikshaynmareyum arike villichau avarodu parranjtu : oruvan enne anugamippan ichchichaall avan tannettan tayjichau tante kroosh eduttukondu enne anugamikydte .
aarekkilum tante jiivane rakshippan ichchichaall atine kallayum ; aarekkilum enteyum suvishekshattinteyum nimittm tante jiivane kallanjall atine rakshikyum .
oru manukshayn savaarlokavum nedukayum tantejiivane kallakayum cheyatall avanu entu pryojanam ?
alla , tante jiivanuvendi manukshayn entoru marruvilkodukyum ?
vaybhicharavum papavum ullalli talamurrayill aarekkilum enneyum ente vachanatteyumkurrichau nannichaall avane kyurrichau manukshayputrnum tante pitavinte tejassill vishaddhdootanmarumayi varuboll nannikyum ;
pinne avan avarodu : daivarajaym shtiyode varunnatu kannuvollam marannam aasdikyattvar chilar i nilkyunnavarill undu enu njan sataymayidtu ningallodu parrayunu enu parranju .
aarrudivasam kajhyinjsheksham yeshu paretasineyum yakyobineyum yohannaneyum koodti oru uyannar malayilekyu tanichau kondupoyi avarude mumbake roopantarappedtu .
bhoomiyill oru alakyukaranum velluppippan kajhyiyatvannm avante vasrtm atayntamvelluppayi tillangi .
appoll eeliiyavum mosheyum avakyru prtaykshamayi yeshuvinodu sambhakshichaukondirunu .

tan entu parrayendu enu avan arrinjilla ; avar bhayaparavasharayirunu .
pinne oru meghamvanu avarudemell nijhyalidtu : ivan ente priyaputrn ; ivanu chevikoduppin enu meghttillninu oru shabdavum undayi .
pedtenu avar chuttum nokyiyarre tangallodukoode yeshuvine matrm allate aareyum kandilla .
avar malayillninu irranguboll : manukshayputrn marichavarillninu ejhyunnettidtllate i kandatu aarodum arriyikyrutu enu avan avarodu kalpichau .

rreeliiyavu mube varendatu enu shasrtimar vadikyunnatu entu enu avar chodichau .
atinu yeshu : eeliiyavu mube vanu sakalavum yathasthanattakyunu sataym ; ennall manukshayputrne kyurrichau : avan vallare kashtappedukayum dhikyriky ppedukayum cheyeendivarum enu ejhyutiyirikyunnatu engane ?
eeliiyavu vanu ; avanekyurrichau ejhyutiyirikyunnatu pole avar tangallkyu tonniyatu ellam avanodu cheyatu enu njan ningallodu parrayunu enu uttram parranju .

avan avarodu : ningall avarumayi takyrikyunnatu entu enu chodichau .
atinu puruksharattill oruttn : guro , umanayaatmavullallente makane njan ninte adukyll konduvanu .

avan avarodu : avishasamullalltalamurraye , etrttollam njan ningallodukoode irikyum ? etrttollam ningalle porrukyum ? avane ente adukyll konduvaruvin enu uttram parranju .
avar avane avante adukyll konduvanu . avane kandudane aatmavu avane ijhyechau ; avan nilattu viinnu nurechaurundu .
itu avanu sambhavichaidtu etr kalamayi enu avante appnodu chodichaatinu avan : cherruppm mutall tanne .

balante appn udane nilavillichau : kattrave , njan vishsikyunu ente avishasattinu sahayikyenname enu parranju .

yeshu avanodu : njan ninakyu entu cheyatutarennamenu nii ichchikyunu enu chodichaatinu : rrabooni , enikyu k prapikyennamenu kurudan avanodu parranju .
yeshu avanodu : poka ; ninte vishasam ninne rakshichairikyunu enu parranju . udane avan k prapichau yatryill avane anugamichau .
avar yerooshaleminodu samiipichau oliiv malayarike betphagayilum bethanayyilum ettiyappoll avan shikshaynmarill randupere ayachau avarodu :
ningallkyu etireyullallgramattill chelluvin ; atill kadannall udane aarum orikylum kayarriidtillatt oru kajhyutkyudtiye kedtiyirikyunnatu kannum ; atine ajhyichau konduvaruvin .
itu cheyaunnatu entu enu aarekkilum ningallodu chodichaall kattravinu itinekyondu aavashaym undu enu parravin ; avan kshannattill atine ingodtu ayakyum enu parranju .
avar poyi teruvill purrattu vatilkyll kajhyutakyudtiye kedtiyirikyunnatu kandu atine ajhyichau .
avide ninnavarill chilar avarodu : ningall kajhyutakyudtiye ajhyikyunnatu entu enu chodichau .
yeshu kalpichaatupole avar avaroduparranju ; avar avare vidtyachau .
avar kajhyutakyudtiye yeshuvinte adukyll konduvanu tangallude vasrtm atinmell idtu ; avan atinmell kayarri irunu .
anekar tangallude vasrtm vajhyiyill virichau ; mattu chilar parrambukallillninu chillikyombuvedti vajhyiyill vitarri .
mumbum pimbum nadakyunnavar : hoshanna , kattravinte namattill varunnavan vajhyttppedtvan :
varunnatayrajaym , nammude pitavaydaviidinte rajaym vajhyttppedumarrakadte ; atayunnatangallill hoshannenu aattrukondirunu .
avan yerooshalemill daivalayattilekyu chenu sakalavum chuttum nokyiyasheksham neram vaikiyatukondu pantiruvarodumkoode bethanayyi lekyu poyi .
pittennall avar bethanayvidtu poruboll avanu vishanu ;
avan ilayullellaru attivraksham doorattuninu kandu , atill vallatum kidtumo enu vechau chenu , atinnarike ettiyappoll ilallate onum kandilla ; atu attippjhyattinte kalamallanju .
avan atinodu : ini nikkllninu ennekyum aarum phalam tinnatirikydte enu parranju ; atu shikshaynmar kedtu .
avar yerooshalemill ettiyappoll avan daivalayttill kadanu , daivalayattill vilkyunnavareyum vangunnavareyum purrattakyittudangi ; ponvannibhakyrude meshakalleyum prakylle vilkyunnavarude piitthangalleyum marrichaidtukallanju ;
aarum daivalayattill koodi oru vasatuvum kondupoku van sammtichailla .
pinne avare upadeshichau : ente aalayam pratthrnalayam enu villikyppedum enu ejhyutiyirikyunnillayo ? ningallo atine kallallanmarude guhayakyi tiittru enu parranju .
atu kedtidtu mahapurohitanmarum shasrtimarum avane nashippikyendatu engane enu anevkshichau . puruksharam ellam avante upadeshattill atishayikyyall avar avane bhayappedtirunu .
sandyyakuboll avan nagaram vidtupokum .
ravile avar kadanu pokuboll attivraksham verode unnangippoyatu kandu ,
appoll paretasinu oammrvanu : rrabai , nii shapichatti unnangippoyalelenu avanodu parranju .
yeshu avarodu uttram parranjtu : daivattill vishasamullallavar aayirippin .
aarekkilum tante hradayattill samshayikyate tan parrayunnatu sambhavikyum enu vashsichaumkondu i malayodu : nii niingi kadalill chadippokenu parranjall avan parranjtupole sambhavikyum enu njan sataymayidtu ningallodu parrayunu .
atukondu ningall pratthrikyuboll yachikyunnato kyeyum labhichau enu vishsippin ; ennall atu ningallkyu undakum enu njan ningallodu parrayunu .
ningall pratthrikyan nilkyuboll sggrsthnayningallude pitavu ningallude pijhyakalle kshamikyendatinu ningallkyu aarodekkilum vallatum undekkill avanodu kshamippin .
ningall kshamikyanjalo sggrsthnayningallude pitavu ningallude pijhyakalleyum kshamikyyilla .
avar pinneyum yerooshalemill chenu . avan daivalayattill chuttinadakyuboll mahapurohitanmarum shasrtimarum mooppnmarum avante adukyll vanu ;
nii entu adhikaramkondu itu cheyaunu enum itu cheyvanullalladhikaram ninakyu tannatu aar enum avanodu chodichau .
yeshu avarodu : njan ningallodu oru vakyu chodikyum ; atinu uttram parravin ; ennall innadhikaramkondu itu cheyaunu enu njanum ningallodu parrayum .
yohannante sanam sggrttill ninno manukshayrill ninno undayatu ? ennodu uttram parravin enu parranju .
avar tammill aalochichau : sggrttill ninu enu parranjall , pinne ningall avane vishsikyanjtu entu enu avan parrayum .
manukshayrillninu enu parranjalo-ellavarum yohannane sakshall prvachakan enu ennukakondu avar janatte bhayappedtu .
angane avar yeshuvinodu : njangallkyu arrinjukoodenu uttram parranju . ennall njanum innadhikaram kondu cheyaunu enu ningallodu parrayunnillenu yeshu avarodu parranju .
pinne avan upamakallall avarodu parranjutudangiyatu : oru manukshayn oru muntirittodtm nadtundakyi chuttum velikedti chakyum kujhyichau nadti gopuravum pannitu kudiyanmare eelpichaidtu paradeshattu poyi .
kalam aayappoll kudiyanmarodu todtttinte anubhavam vangendatinu avan oru dasane kudiyanmarude adukyll parranjyachau .
avar avane pidichau talli verrute ayachau kallanju .
pinne mattoru dasane avarude adukyll parranjyachau ; avane avar talayill murrivelpikyukayum avamanikyyum cheyatu .
avan mattoruvane parranjyachau ; avane avar konu ; mattu palareyum chilare adikyyum chilare kollukayum cheyatu .
avanu ini oruttn , oru priyamakan , undayirunu . ente makane avar shakkikyum enu parranju odukym avane avarude adukyll parranjyachau .
akudiyanmaro : ivan avakashi aakunu ; varuvin ; nam ivane kolluka ; ennall avakasham namukyakum enu tammill parranju .
avar avane pidichau konu todtttill ninu errinju kallanju .
ennall todtttinte udayavan entu cheyaum ? avan vanu akudiyanmare nigrhichau todtm mattullallavare eelpikyum .
" viidu panniyunnavar tallallikyllanj kallu moolakyllayatiinnariri kyunu .
itu kattravinall sambhavichau . nammude drashtiyill ayaarvumayirikyunu " enntiruvejhyuttu ningall vayichaidtillayo ?
i upamtangallekyurrichau aakunu parranjtu enu grhichaidtu avar avane pidippan anekshichau : ennall puruksharatte bhayappedtu avane vidtupoyi .
anantaram avane vakyill kudukyuvan vendi avar pariishanmarilum herodayrilum chilare avante adukyll ayachau .
avar vanu : guro , nii manukshayrude mukham nokyate daivattinte vajhyi nerayi patthippikyunnatukondu nii satayvanum aareyum gannaymakyattvanum enu njangall arriyunu ; kaisakyru karam kodukyunnatu vihitamo allayo ? njangall kodukyyo kodukyatirikyyo vendatu enu avanodu chodichau .
avan avarude kapadam arrinju : ningall enne pariikshikyunnatu entu ? oru vellallikyashu konduvaruvin ; njan kannadte enu parranju .
avar konduvanu . i sroopavum melejhyuttum aarudetu enu avarodu chodichaatinu : kaisarudetu enu avar parranju .
yeshu avarodu : kaisakyurllallatu kaisakyrum daivattinullallatu daivattinum koduppin enu parranju ; avar avakkll vallare ayaaarppedtu .
punarutthanam illenu parrayunnsadookayr avante adukyll vanu chodichaatentennall :
guro , oruttnte sahodaran makyllillate marichau bhayaaar shekshichaall abhayaarye avante sahodaran parigrhichau tante sahodaranu santatiye janippikyennam enu moshe ejhyutiyirikyunu .
ennall eejhyu sahodaranmar undayirunu ; avarill moottvan oru srtiiye vivaham kajhyichau santatiyillate marichau poyi .
randamattvan avalle parigrhichau santatiyillate marichau ; moonnamattvanum angane tanne .
eejhyuvarum santatiyillate marichau ; ellavakyrum oduvill srtiiyum marichau .
punarutthanattill avall avarill eevanu bhayaaaryakum ? eejhyuvakyrum bhayaaar aayirunuvalela .
yeshu avarodu parranjtu : ningall tiruvejhyuttukalleyum daivashtiyeyum arriyaykakondallayo tettippokunnatu ?
marichaavarillninu uyitterjhyunnelkyuboll vivaham kajhyikyyillvivahattinu kodukyppedukayumilla ; sggrttile dootanmareppole aakum .
ennall marichaavar uyitterjhyunnelkyunnatinekyurrichau mosheyude pusatkattill mullpadapprubhagattu daivam avanodu : njan abrahaminte daivavum yishakyi nte daivavum yakyobinte daivavum enu arullicheeyat prkaram vayichaidtillayo ?
avan marichaavarude daivamalla , jiivanullallavarude daivamareta ; ningall vallare tettippokunu .
shasrtimarill oruvan aduttuvanu avar tammill takyrikyu nnatukedtu avan avarodu nallavannm uttram parranj prkaram bodhichaidtu : ellattilum mukhaykalpaneetu enu avanodu chodichau .
atinu yeshu : ellattilum mukhaykalpanayo : ' yisrayele , kellky ; nammude daivamaykattravu eekkattravu .
ninte daivamaykattravine nii poonnrhradayattodum poonnratmavodum poonnrmanassodum poonnrshtiyodum koode senhikyennam ' enu aakunu .
randamatteto : ' koodtukarane ninneppole tanne senhikyennam ' ennareta ; ivayill valutayidtu mattoru kalpanayum illenu uttram parranju .
shasrti avanodu : nanu guro nii parranjtu sataym tanne ; eekaneyullallu ; avanallate mattoruttnumilla .
avane poonnrhradayattodum poonnrmanassodum poonnrshti yodumkoode senhikyunnatum tanneppole koodtukarane senhikyunnatum sakalsavaaramgahomangallekyallum yagngallekyallum saramerriyatu tanne enu parranju .
avan buddhiyode uttram parranju enu yeshu kandidtu : nii daivarajayttodu akannavanallenu parranju . atinte sheksham avanodu aarum onum chodippan tuninjilla .
yeshu daivalayattill upadeshichaukondu parranjutudngiyatu : krisatu daviidinte putrn enu shasrtimar parrayunnatu engane ?
" kattravu ente kattravinodu : njan ninte shatrukylle ninte padapiittham aakyuvollam ente valattubhagattiriky enu arullicheyatu " enu daviid tan parishuddhatmavilayi parrayunu .
daviid tanne avane kattravu enu parrayunuvalela ; pinne avante putrn aakunnatu engane ? ennall valiypuruksharam avante vakyu santokshattode kedtuponu .
avan tante upadeshattill avarodu : akkikallode nadakyunnatum angadiyill vandnavum
pallalliyill mukhayasanavum attajhyattill prdhanasthlavum ichchikyunnshasrtimare sookshichaukollvin .
avar vidhavamarude viidukalle vijhyungukayum upayattall niindprtthrnakajhyikyyum cheyaunu ; avakyru eettvum valiyshikshavidhi varum enu parranju .
pinne yeshu shriibhandarattinu nere irikyuboll puruksharam bhandarattill pannam idunnatu nokyikyondi runu ; dhanavanmar palarum vallare idtu .

pinne avan olivmalayill daivalayattinu nere irikyuboll paretasum yakyobum yohannanum arentayasum skayaaarmayi avanodu : atu eppoll sambhavikyum ?
atinu nivratti varunnkalattinte lakshannam entuenu njangallodu parranjalum enu chodichau .

njan aakunu enu parranjukondu anekar ente pereduttu vanu palareyum tettikyum .
ennall ningall yuddhngalleyum yuddh shrutikalleyum kurrichau kellkyuboll bhrmichaupokarutu . atu sambhavikyendatu tanne ; ennall atu avasanamalla .
jatijatiyodum rajaym rajayttodum etikyrum ; avidavide bhookambavum kshamavum undakum ; itu ittu novinte aarambhamareta .
ennall ningallettnne sookshichaukollvin ; avar ningalle nayayadhipasamghangallill eelpikyyum pallallikallill vechau tallukayum ente nimittm naduvajhyikallkyum rajakynmakyrum mumbake avakyru sakshayttinnayi nirruttukayum cheyaum .
ennall suvisheksham mube sakalajatikallodum prsamgikyendatakunu .
avar ningalle kondupoyi eelpikyuboll entu parrayendu enu munkoodti vicharappedarutu . anajhyikayill ningallkyu labhikyunnatutanne parravin ; parrayunnatu ningall alla , parishuddhatmavareta .
sahodaran sahodaraneyum appn makaneyum marannattinu eelpikyum ; makyllum ammyappnmarude nere ejhyunnettu avare kollikyum .
ente namam nimittm ellavarum ningalle pakekyum ; ennall avasanattollam sahichau nilkyunnavan rakshikyppedum .
ennall shoonaymakunnmelchchatnilkyrutatt sthlattu nilkyunnatu ningall kannuboll - vayikyunnavan chintichaukollalladte-anu yehoodaydeshattu ullallavar malakallilekyu oadippokadte .

vayalill irikyunnavan vasrtm eduppan madangippokarutu .
akalattu gabharinnikallkyum mulakudippikyunnavakyrum ayeekashtam !
ennall atu shiitakalattu sambhavikyatirippan pratthrippin .
anallukall daivam srashtichasrashtiyude aarambham mutall inuvare sambhavichaidtillatttum inimell sambhavikyatttum aaykashtakalam aakum .

anu aarekkilum ningallodu : ita , krisatu ivide enno atavide enno parranjall vishsikyrutu .

aakashattuninu nakshatrngall viinnukondirikyyum aakashattile shtikall illakippokayum cheyaum .
appoll manukshayputrn valiyshtiyodum tejassodum koode meghangallill varunnatu avar kannum .
anu avan tante dootanmare ayachau , tante vratanmare bhoomiyude arrutimutall aakashattinte arrutivareyum naludikyillninum koodticheekyrum .

yajamanan sandeykyo addhrratrikyo kojhyikookunnneratto ravileyo eppoll varum enu arriyay kakondu ,
avan pedtenu vanu ningalle urrangunnavarayi kande ttatirikyendatinu unnannaririppin .
njan ningallodu parrayunnato ellavarodum parrayunu . unnannaririppin .
randudivasam kajhyinjidtu pesahayudeyum pullippillatt appttinteyum utsavam aayirunu . appoll mahapurohitanmarum shasrtimarum avane upayattall pidichau kolelndatu engane enu anevkshichau :
janattill kalaham undakatirippan utsavattill arutu enu avar parranju .

avide chilar : tailattinte i verrum chelavu entinu ?
itu munnoorrill adhikam vellallikyashinu vittu daridrkyru koduppan kajhyiyumayirunuvalelenningane ullallill niirasappedtu avalle bhrichau .

avall tannall aavatu cheyatu : kallarrayile adakyttinnayi ente dehattinu mumbukoodti tailam techau .

avar atukedtu santokshichau avanu pannam kodukyam enu vagdattm cheyat ; avanum avane engane kannichaukodukyam enu takym anevkshichauponu .
