shikshaynmar purrappedtu nagarattill chenu avan tangallodu parranjtupole kandu pesahorukyi .
sandyyayappoll avan pantiruvarodumkoode vanu .
avar irunu bhakshikyuboll yeshu : ningallill oruvan , ennodukoode bhakshikyunnavan tanne , enne kannichau kodukyum enu njan sataymayidtu ningallodu parrayunu enu parranju .
avar du : khichau , ororuttn : njano njano enu avanodu chodichau tudangi .
avan avarodu : pantiruvarill oruvan , ennodukoode talattill kai mukyunnavan tanne .
manukshayputrn pokunnatu tannekyurrichau ejhyutiyirikyunntupole tanne sataym ; manukshayputrne kannichaukodu kyunnmanukshaynno ayeekashtam ; amanukshayn janikytirunu ekkill avanu kollallayirunu enu parranju .
avar bhakshikyuboll avan appm eduttu vajhytti nurrukyi avakyru koduttu : vanguvin ; itu ente shariiram enu parranju .
pinne panapatrm eduttu setatrmcholli avakyru koduttu ; ellavarum atillninu kudichau ;
itu anekakyurvendi choriyunnatayi niyamattinullallente rtam .
muntirivallalliyude anubhavam pututayi anubhavikyumnall vare njan atu ini anubhavikyyillenu njan sataymayidtu ningallodu parrayunu enu avarodu parranju .
pinne avar setatrm padiyasheksham olivmalekyu poyi .
yeshu avarodu : ningall ellavarum idarrippokum ;
ennall njan uyitterjhyunnettsheksham ningallkyu mube galiilekyu pokum enu parranju .
paretas avanodu : ellavarum idarriyalum njan idarrukayillenu parranju .
yeshu avanodu : inu , i ratriyill tanne , kojhyi randuvadtm kookummube nii moonuvadtm enne tallallipprrayum enu njan sataymayidtu ninnodu parrayunu enu parranju .
avano : ninnodukoode marikyendivannalum njan ninne tallallipprrakayillenu adhikamayi parranju ; angane tanne ellavarum parranju .
avar getshemanennperullalltodtttill vannarre avan shikshaynmarodu : njan pratthrichautiiruvollam ivide irippin enu parranju .
pinne avan paretasineyum yakyobineyum yohannaneyum koodtikyondu bhrmippanum
ente ullallam marannavedanapole atidu : khitamayirikyunu ; ivide pattru unnannaririppin enu avarodu parranju .
pinne alpam mubodtu chenu nilattu viinnu , kajhyiyum ekkill anajhyikniingippokennam enu pratthrrichau :
abaa , pitave , ninakyu ellam kajhyiyum ; i panapatrm ekkllninu niikyenname ; ekkilum njan ichchikyunnatallnii ichchikyunnataretaakadte enu parranju .
pinne avan vanu avar urrangunnatukandu paretasi nodu : shiimone , nii urrangunuvo ? oru najhyikunnannari rippan ninakyu kajhyinjillayo ?
pariikshayill akappedayvan unnannarirunu pratthrippin ; aatmavu orukymullallatu , jaddamo balahiinamaretenu parranju .
avan pinneyum poyi avachanam tanne cholli pratthrichau .
madangivannarre avarude kannukallkyu bharamerriyirunnatu kondu avar urrangunnatu kandu ; avar avanodu entu uttram parrayennam enu arrinjill ;
avan moonnamatu vanu avarodu : ini urrangi aashsichau kollvin ; mati , najhyikvanu ; ita , manukshayputrn papikallude kayaill eelpikyppedunu .
ejhyunnelpin ; nam poka ; ita , enne kannichaukodu kyunnavan aduttirikyunu enu parranju .
udane avan samsarichaukondirikyuboll tanne , pantiruvarill oruttnayyoodayum avanodukoode mahapu rohitanmar , shasrtimar , mooppnmar ennavar ayachoru puruksharavum vallum vadiyumayi vanu .
avane kannichaukodukyunnavan njan eevane chumbikyu mo avan tanne aakunu ; avane pidichau sookshtayode kondupokuvin enu avakyru oru adayallam parranjukoduttirunu .
avan vanu udane aduttu chennu : rrabai , enu parranju avane chumbichau .
avar avante mell kaivechau avane pidichau .
arike nilkyunnavarill oruvan vall uri mahapuro hitante dasane vedti katu arruttu .
yeshu avarodu : oru kallallante nere ennapole ningall enne pidippan vallum vadiyumayi purrappedtu vanuvo ?
njan divasendaivalayattill upadeshichaukondu ningallodukoode irunu ; ningall enne pidichailla ; ekkilum tiruvejhyuttukallkyu nivratti varendatinu ingane sambhavikyunu enu parranju .
shikshaynmar ellavarum avane vidtu oadippoyi .
oru balaykyaran verrum shariirattinmell putappu putechaumkondu avane anugamichau ; avar avane pidichau .
avano putappu vidtu nnayi oadippoyi .
avar yeshuvine mahapurohitante adukyll kondu poyi . avante adukyll mahapurohitanmarum mooppnmarum shasrtimarum ellam vanu koodiyirunu .
paretas mahapurohitante aramanakykattollavum avane doorave anugamichau , bhrataynmarodu chenur tii kanjukondirunu .
mahapurohitanmarum nayayadhipasamgham okyeyum yeshuvine kolelndatinu avante nere sakshaym anevkshichau kandillatanum .
anekar avante nere kallallassakshaym parranjidtum sakshaym ottuvannilla .
chilar ejhyunnettu avante nere :
kaippnniyayi mandiram pollichau moonudivasamkondu kaippnniyallatt mattonu panniyum enu ivan parranjtu njan kedtu enu kallallassakshaym parranju .
ennidtum avarude sakshaym ottuvannilla .
mahapurohitan naduvill ninukondu yeshuvinodu : nii onum uttram parrayunnillayo ? ivar ninte nere sakshaym parrayunnatu entu enu chodichau .
avano mindateyum uttram parrayateyum irunu . mahapurohitan pinneyum avanodu : nii vandynayvante putrnaykrisatuvo enu chodichau .
njan aakunu ; manukshayputrn savaaarshtante valattu bhagattu irikyunnatum aakashameghangallode varunnatum ningall kannum enu yeshu parranju .
appoll mahapurohitan vasrtmkiirri : ini sakshikalle kyondu namukyu entu aavashaym ?
daivadookshannam ningall kedtuvalel ; ningallkyu entu tonunu enu chodichau . avan marannayogayn enu ellavarum vidhichau .
chilar avane tuppukayum avante mukham moodi avane mushtichurudti kuttukayum prvachiky enu avanodu parrakayum cheyatutudangi ; chevakar avane adichaumkondu kayeettu .
paretas tajhye nadumuttttu irikyuboll mahapurohitante balaykyarattikallill orutti vanu .
paretas tii kayunnatu kandu avane nokyi : niiyum nasarrayanayyeshuvinodukoode aayirunu enu parranju .
nii parrayunnatu tiriyunnilla , boddhymakunnatumillenningane avan tallallipprranju ; padippurayilekyu purrappedtppoll kojhyi kooki .
abalaykyaratti avane pinneyum kandu samiipattu nilkyunnavarodu : ivan aakoodtrill ullallavan tanne enu parranju tudangi .
kurrayaneram kajhyinjidtu arike ninnavar paretasinodu : nii aakoodtrill ullallavan sataym ; galiilakyaranallayo enu parranju .
ningall parrayunnmanukshayne njan arriyunnillenu avan prakuvanum aannayiduvanum tudangi .
udane kojhyi randamatum kooki ; kojhyi randuvadtm kookum mube nii moonuvadtm enne tallallipprrayum enu yeshu tannodu parranj vakyu paretas oattru atine kyurrichau vicharichau karanju .
udane atikalattu tanne mahapurohitanmarum mooppnmarum shasrtimarumayi nayayadhipasamgham okyeyum koodi aalochichau yeshuvine kedtikondu poyi piilattosine eelpichau .
piilattos avanodu : nii yehoodanmarude rajavo enu chodichaatinu : njan aakunu enu avan uttram parranju .
mahapurohitanmar avane eerriyonu kuttm chumatti .
piilattos pinneyum avanodu chodichau : nii oruttravum parrayunnillayo ? ita , avar ninne entellam kuttm chumattunu enu parranju .
yeshu pinneyum uttram onum parrayaykayall piilattos ayaarppedtu .
avan utsavamtorrum avar chodikyunnoru tadavukarane avakyru vidtukoduky pativayirunu .
ennall oru kalahattill kulcheyatvaraykalahakyarodu koode bandichairunnbarrabaas enu perullalloruttn undayirunu .
puruksharam kayarrivanu , avan pativupole cheyeennam enu apekshichau tudangi .
mahapurohitanmar asooyakondu avane eelpichau enu piilattos arrinjtukondu avarodu :
yehoodanmarude rajavine ningallkyu vidtutarennam enu ichchikyunnuvo enu chodichau .
ennall avan barrabaasine vidtukodukyendatinu chodippan mahapurohitanmar puruksharatte utsahippichau kondirunu .
piilattos pinneyum avarodu : ennall yehoodanmrude rajavu enu ningall parrayunnavane njan entu cheyeennam enu chodichau .
avane krooshiky enu avar viindum nilavillichau .
piilattos avarodu : avan entu doksham cheyatu enu parranjarre , avane krooshiky enu avar adhikamayi nilavillichau .
piilattos puruksharatte trapativaruttuvan ichchichau barrabaasine avakyru viidtukoduttu yeshuvine chammdtikondu adippichau krooshippan eelpichau .
padayallikall avane aasthanamaymandpattinakattu kondupoyi padtallatte ellam villichau koodti .
avane rtambaram dharippichau , mullallukondu oru kiriidam medanju avane choodichau :
yehoodanmarude rajave , jayajayenu parranju vandichau ;
kollkondu avante talayill adichau , avane tuppi , mudtukutti avane namaskyrichau .
angane avane parihasichaasheksham avar rtambaram niikyi sntvasrtm dharippichau avane krooshippan kondupoyi .
alaksantarinteyum roophasinteyum appnayi vayalill ninu varunnkarrenakyaranayshiimone avante kroosh chumappan avar nibaarndichau .
talayodidam ennatthrmullallgolgothennsthlattekyu avane kondupoyi ;
kandivenn kalattriyviinju avanu koduttu ; avano vangiyilla .
avane krooshichaasheksham avante vasrtm innavanu innatu kidtennam enu pakuticheyatu .
moonnam mannineramayappoll avane krooshichau .
yehoodanmarude rajavu enningane avante kuttm miite ejhyutiyirunu .
avar randu kallallanmare oruttne valattum oruttne idattumayi avanodu koode krooshichau .
( adhammrikallude koodtttill avane enni enullalltiruvejhyuttu nivrattiyayi . )
kadanu pokunnavar talakulukyikyondu : ha , ha , mandiram pollichau moonu nallukondu panniyunnavane ,
ninnettnne rakshichau krooshillninu irrangivenu parranju avane dukshichau .
angane tanne mahapurohitanmarum mooppnmarum avane parihasichau : ivan mattullallavare rakshichau tannettan rakshippan vahiya .
nam kandu vishsikyendatinu krisatu ennyisrayell rajavu ippoll krooshillninu irrangivaradte enu tammill parranju ; avanodukoode krooshikyppedtvarum avane pajhyichau parranju .
aarram mannineramayappoll ombatam manninerattollam deshattuellam irudtu undayi .
ombatam manninerattu yeshu : ente daivame , ente daivame , nii enne kaividttu entu enu atthrmullallelohi , elohi , lammshabatani enu atayuchattill nilavillichau .
arike ninnavarill chilar kedtidtu : avan eeliiyave villikyunu enu parranju .
oruttn oadi oru sepangill pullichaviinju nirrechau oru oadakyolinmelakyi : nilpin ; eeliiyavu avane irrakyuvan varumo enu namukyu kannam enu parranju avanu kudippan koduttu .
yeshu urrakye villichau prannane vidtu .
udane mandirattile tirashiilmelltodtu adiyollavum randayi chiintippoyi .
avanu etire ninnirunnshatadhipan avan ingane prannane vidttu kandidtu : i manukshayn daivaputrn aayirunu sataym enu parranju .
srtiikallum doorattuninu nokyikyondirunu ; avarill magdalakyaratti marriyayum cherriyyakyobinteyum yoseyudeyum amm marriyayum shalomayum undayirunu .
avan galiilayill irikyuboll avar avane anugamichaum shushrookshichaum ponu ; avanodukoode yerooshalemilekyu vannmattu srtiikallum undayirunu .
vaikunneramayappoll shabaattinte talanallayorukynall aakakondu reshakshtthamantriyum
daivarajaytte kattirunnavanumayarimatthyyile yoseph vanu dhaiyaarttode piilattosinte adukyll chenu yeshuvinte shariiram chodichau .
avan marichaukajhyinjuvo enu piilattos ayaaarppedtu shatadhipane villichau : avan marichaidtu odtuneramayo enu
shatadhipanodu vasatutchodichaarrinjidtu udall yosephinu nalki .
avan oru shiilvangi avane irrakyi shiilayill chutti ppotinju , parrayill vedtiidtullallkallarrayill vechau , kallarravatilkyll oru kallu urudti vechau .
avane vechidam magdalakyaratti marriyayum yoseyude amm marriyayum nokyikyndu .
shabaat kajhyinjsheksham magdalakyaratti marriyayum yakyobinte amm marriyayum shalomayum chenu avane pooshendatinu sugandvaggrm vangi .
avadtttinte onnamnall atikalattu sooyaarn udichappoll avar kallarrekyll chenu :
kallarrayude vatilkyllninu namukyuvendi aar kallu urudtikyllayum enu tammill parranju .
avar nokyiyarre kallu urudtikyllanjtayi kandu ; atu eettvum valutayirunu .
avar kallarrekykattu kadannappoll vellallanilayakki dharichoru balaykyaran valattu bhagattu irikyunnatu kandu bhrmichau .
avan avarodu : bhrmikyenda ; krooshikyppedt nasarrayanayyeshuvine ningall anevkshikyunu ; avan uyitterrrjhyunnettu ; avan ivide illa ; avane vechasthlam ita ,
ningall poyi avante shikshaynmarodum paretasinodum : avan ningallkyu mube galiilekyu pokunu enu parravin ; avan ningallodu parranjtupole avide avane kannum enu parravin enu parranju .
avakyru virrayalum paribhrmavum pidichau avar kallarravidtu oadippoyi ; avar bhayappedukayall aarodum onum parranjilla .
( avan avadtttinte onnam nall ravile uyitterjhyu nnettidtu tan eejhyubhootangalle purrattakyiyirunnmagdalakyratti marriyekyu aadaym prtaykshanayi .
avall chenu avanodukoode irunnavarayi du : khichaum karanjumkondirunnavarodu arriyichau .
avan jiivanodirikyunu enum avall avane kandu enum avar kedtarre vishsichailla .
pinne avarill randuper nadtilekyu pokuboll avan mattoru roopattill avakyru prtaykshanayi .
avar poyi shekshamullallavarodu arriyichau ; avarude vakyum avar vishsichailla .
pinnettetill patinoruvar bhakshannattinirikyuboll avan avakyrru prtaykshanayi , tanne uyitterjhyunnettvnayi kandavarude vakyu vishsikyaykayall avarude avishasatteyum hradayakatthinaytteyum shasichau .
pinne avan avarodu : ningall bhoolokattill okyeyum poyi sakalsrashtiyodum suvisheksham prsamgippin .
vishsikyyum sanam eelkyyum cheyaunnavan rakshappedum ; vishsikyattvan shikshavidhiyill akappedum .
vishsikyunnavarall i adayallangall nadakyum : ente namattill avar bhootangalle purrattakyum ; putubhakshakallill samsarikyum ;
sapprngalle pidicheedukyum ; marannakaramayyatonu kadichaalum avakyru hani varikayilla ; rogikallude mell kai vechaall avakyru sekhaym varum enu parranju .
ingane kattravayyeshu avarodu arullicheeyatsheksham sggrttilekyu edukyppedtu . daivattinte valattu bhagattu irunu .

shriimanayteyophilose , aadimutall kandsakshikallum vachanattinte shushrookshakanmarumayavar namme bharamelpichaatupole ,
nammude idayill poonnrmayi prmannichau varunnkayaarngalle vivarikyunnoru charitrm chameppan palarum tuninjiriky kondu ,
ninakyu upadesham labhichairikyunnvattryude nischayam nii arriyendatinu atu krmamayi ejhyutunnatu
nannenu aadimutall sakalavum sookshmayi parishodhichaidtu enikyum tonniyirikyunu .
yehoodayrajavayherodavinte kalattu abiyakyoorrill sekhayaaravu enu perullallpurohitan undayirunu ; avante bhayaar aharonte putrimarill orutti aayirunu ; avallkyu eliishabet enu per .
iruvarum daivasannidhayill niitiyullallavarum kattravinte sakalakalpanakallilum nayayangallilum kuttmillattvarayi nadakyunnavarum aayirunu .
eliishabet machaiyakakondu avakyru santati illanju ; iruvarum vayassuchennavarum aayirunu .
avan koorrinte krmaprkaram daivasannidhiyill purohi tanayi shushrookshcheyatuvaruboll :
perohitaymayaaradaprkaram kattravinte mandirattill chenu dhoopam kadtuvan avanu narrukyu vanu .
dhoopam kadtunnnajhyikayill janasamooham okyeyum purrattu pratthrichaukondirunu .
appoll kattravinte dootan dhoopapiitthattinte valattu bhagattu nilkyunnavanayidtu avanu prtaykshanayi .
sekhayaaaravu avane kandu bhrmichau bhayaparavashanayi .
dootan avanodu parranjtu : sekhayaarave , bhayappedenda ; ninte pratthrnekyu uttramayi : ninte bhayaaar eliishabet ninakyu oru makane prsavikyum ; avanu yohannan enu per idennam .
ninakyu santokshavum ullasavum undakum ; avante jananttikkll palarum santokshikyum .
avan kattravinte sannidhiyill valiyavan aakum ; viinjum madayvum kudikyyilla ; ammyude gabharttill vechau tanne parishuddhatmavu kondu nirrayum .
avan yisrayell makyllill palareyum avarude daivamaykattravikklekyu tirichauvaruttum .
avan appnmarude hradayangalle makyllilekyum vajhyangattvare niitimanmarude bodhattilekyum tirichaum kondu orukymullellaru janatte kattravinu vendi orukyuvan avanu mumbayi eeliiyavinte aatmavodum shtiyodumkoode nadakyum .
sekhayaaravu dootanodu ; itu njan entonninall arriyum ? njan vraddhnum ente bhayaar vayassuchennavallu malelenu parranju .
dootan avanodu : njan daivasannidhiyill nilkyunngabriiyell aakunu ; ninnodu samsarippanum i sadttrmanam ninnodu arriyippanum enne ayachairikyunu .
takysamayattu nivrattivaruvanullallente vakyu vishsi kyaykakondu atu sambhavikyum vare nii samsarippan kajhyiyate menamayirikyum enu parranju .
janam sekhayaaravinnayi kattirunu , avan mandirattill tamasichaatinall ayarrrppedtu .
avan purrattu vannarre avarodu samsarippan kajhyinjilla ; atinall avan mandirattill oru dasharnam kandu enu avar arrinju ; avan avakyru aagaymkadti umanayi pattru .
avante shushrookshakalam tikanjsheksham avan viidtlekyu poyi .
anallukall kajhyinjidtu avante bhayaaar eliishabet gabharm dharichau :
manukshayrude idayill enikyundayirunnnind niikyuvan kattravu enne kadakshichaanallill ingane enikyu cheyatu tannirikyunu enu parranju anchu masam ollichau pattru .
aarram masattill daivam gabriiyelldootane nasarret enngaliilapadtnnattill ,
daviidgrahattilullallyoseph ennoru purukshanu vivaham nischayichairunnkanaykayude adukyll ayachau ; akanaykayude per marriyenu aayirunu .
dootan avallude adukyll akattu chenu : krapalabhichaavalle , ninakyu vandnam ; kattravu ninnodukoode undu enu parranju .
avall avakyu kedtu bhrmichau : itu entoru vandnam enu vicharichau .
dootan avallodu : marriyaye bhayappedenda ; ninakyu daivattinte kraplabhichau .
nii gabharm dharichau oru makane prsavikyum ; avanu yeshu enu per villikyennam .
avan valiyavan aakum ; atayunnatante putrn enu villikyppedum ; kattravaydaivam avante pitavaydaviidinte simhasanam avanu kodukyum .
avan yakyob grahattinu ennekyum rajavayirikyum ; avante rajayttinu avasanam undakayillenu parranju .
marriydootanodu : njan purukshane arriyaykayall itu engane sambhavikyum enu parranju .
atinu dootan : parishuddhatmavu ninte mell varum ; atayunnatante shti ninte mell nijhyalidum ; aakayall utdvikyunnvishuddhprjdaivaputrn enu villikyppedum .
ninte chachaarkyaratti eliishabettum vaddhrkayttill oru makane gabharm dharichairikyunu ; machai enu parranjvallkyu itu aarram masam .
daivattinu orukayaarvum asaddhymallallelenu uttram parranju .
atinu marriy ita , njan kattravinte dasi ; ninte vakyupole enikyu bhavikydte enu parranju ; dootan avalle vidtupoyi .
anallukallill marriyejhyunnettu malanadtill oru yehooday padtnnattill baddhppedtu chenu ,
sekhayaaravinte viidtill etti eliishabettine vandichau .
marriyayude vandnam eliishabet kedtppoll pillallavallude gabharttill tullalli ; eliishabet parishuddhatmavu nirranjvallayi , uchaattill villichau parranjtu :
srtiikallill nii anugrhikyppedtvall ; ninte gabharphalavum anugrhikyppedttu :
ente kattravinte matavu ente adukyll varunnmanam enikyu evideninu undayi .
ninte vandnasram ente cheviyill viinnappoll pillallente gabharttill aanandmkondu tullalli .
kattravu tannodu arullicheyattinu nivrattiyundakum enu vishsichaavall bhagayvati .
appoll marriyparranjtu : " ente ullallam kattravine mahimappeduttunu ;
ente aatmavu ente rakshitavaydaivattill ullasikyunu .
avan tante dasiyude t kadakshichairikyunuvalela ; inumutall ellatalamurrakallum enne bhagayvati enu vajhyttum .
shtanayavan enikyu valiyavcheyatirikyunu ; avante namam parishuddhm tanne .
avane bhayappedunnavakyru avante karunntalamurratalamurryollam irikyunu .
tante bhujamkondu avan balam prvattrichau , hradayavichrattill ahakkrikyunnavare chitarrichairikyunu .
prbhukynmare simhasanangallillninu irrakyi tannavare uyattriyirikyunu .
vishannirikyunnavare nanmakallall nirrechau , sambannanmare verrute ayachau kallanjirikyunu .
nammude pitakynmarodu arullicheeyattupole abrahaminum avante santatikyum ennekyum karunnoakyerndatinu ,
tante dasanayyisrayeline tunnechairikyunu . "
marriyeekadesham moonumasam avallodukoode pattridtu viidtilekyu madangippoyi .
eliishabettinu prsavippanullallkalam tikanjppoll avall oru makane prsavichau ;
kattravu avallkyu valiykarunnakannichau enu ayalkyarum chachaarkyarum kedtidtu avallodukoode santokshichau .
edtam nallill avar paitaline pariedancheyvan vanu ; appnte perpole avanu sekhayaaravu enu pervillippan bhavichau .
avante ammyo : alla , avanu yohannan enu peridennam enu parranju .
avar avallodu : ninte chachaaaryill i perullallavar aarum illalelenu parranju .
pinne avanu entu per villippan vicharikyunu enu appnodu aamgaymkadti chodichau .
avan oru ejhyuttu palakchodichau : avante per yohannan enu ejhyuti ; ellavarum ayaarppedtu .
udane avante vayum navum turranu , avan samsarichau daivatte satutichau .
chuttum pakyrrunnavakyru ellam bhayam undayi ; yehooday malanadtill engum i vattr okyeyum paranu .
kedtvar ellavarum atu hradayattill nikshepichau : i paitall entu aakum enu parranju ; kattravinte kai avanodukoode undayirunu .
avante appnaysekhayaaravu parishuddhatmavu nirranjvanayi prvachichau parranjtu :
" yisrayelinte daivamaykattravu anugrhikyppedtvan . avan tante janatte sandsharichau uddharannam cheykayum
aadimutall tante prvachakanmar mukhantaram arullicheyat tupele
nammude shatrukyllude vashattuninum namme pakekyunn eevarudeyum kayaillninu namme rakshippan
tante dasanaydaviidinte grahattill nammukyu rakshayude kombu uyattrukayum cheyatirikyunnatu ,
nammude pitakynmarodu karunnprvattrikyendatinum
nammude shatrukyllude kayaillninu rakshikyppedtu
nam aayukshkyalam okyeyum bhayamkoodate tirumumbill vishuddhiyilum niitiyilum tanne aaradhippan namukyu krapnalkumenu
avan nammude pitavayabrahaminodu cheyat satayvum tante vishuddh niyamavum oattrtukondum aakunu .
niiyo paitale , atayunnatante prvachakan enu villikyppedum . kattravinte vajhyi orukyuvanum
nammude daivattinte aadrrkarunnayall avante janattinu papamochanattill rakshaparinjanam koduppanumayi nii avanu mube nadakyum .
irullilum marannanijhyalilum irikyunnavakyru prkashichau , nammude kalukalle samadhanamaggrttill nadattendatinu
aaadrrkarunnayall uyarattillninu udayam namme sandsharichairikyunu . "
paitall vallanur aatmavill balappedtu ; avan yisrayelinu tannettan kannikyum nallvare marubhoomiyill aayirunu .
akalattu lokam okyeyum pervajhyi chatternnam enu ogusetaskaisarude oru purrappedtu .
kurrenayas surriyanadu vajhyuboll i onnamatte chattrll undayi .
ellavarum chattrppedendatinu tantante padtnnattilekyu yatryayi .
angane yosephum daviidinte grahattilum kulattilum ullallavan aakakondu tanikyu vivaham nischayichairunnmarriyenngabharinniyaybhayaaryodumkoode chattrppedendatinu galiilayile nasarret ennpadtnnam vidtu ,
yehoodayyill betelhem enndaviidin padtnnattilekyu poyi .
avar avide irikyuboll avallkyu prsavippanullallkalam tikenju .
avall aadayjatanaymakane prsavichau , shiilakallchutti vajhyiyambalattill avakyru sthlam illaykayall pashuto dtiyill kidatti .
anu aprdeshattu idayanmar ratryill aadtinkoodttte kavallkattu velliyill pattrirunu .
appoll kattravinte oru dootan avarude arike ninu , kattravinte tejas avare chuttiminni , avar bhayaparavasharayatiinur .
dootan avarodu : bhayappedend ; savaarjanattinum undavanullellaru mahasantoksham njan ningallodu suvishekshikyunu .
kattravaykrisatu ennrakshitavu inu daviidinte padtnnattill ningallkyayi janichairikyunu .
ningallkyu adayallamo : shiilakallchutti pashuttodtiyill kidakyunnoru shishuvine ningall kannum enu parranju .
pedtenu sggriiyasainayttinte oru samgham dootanodu chenur daivatte pukajhytti .
" atayunnatangallill daivattinu mahatm ; bhoomiyill daivaprsadamullallmanukshaykyru samadhanam " enu parranju .
dootanmar avare vidtu sggrttill poyasheksham idayanmar : nam bettelhemollam chenu kattravu nammodu arriyichi sambhavam kannennam enu tammill parranju .
avar baddhppedtu chenu , marriyayeyum yosephineyum pashutodtiyill kidakyunnshishuvineyum kandu .
kandasheksham i paitalinekyurrichau tangallodu parranj vakyu arriyichau .
kedtvar ellavarum idayanmar parranjtinekyurrichau ayaarppedtu .
marriyi vattr okyeyum hradayattill samgrhichau dhayanichaukondirunu .
tangallodu arriyichaatupole idayanmar kedttum kandatu mayellattineyumkurrichau daivatte mahatppeduttiyum pukajhyttiyumkondu madangippoyi .
pariedankajhyippanullalledtudivasam tikenjppoll avan gabharttill ulpadikyummube dutan parranjtupole avanu yeshu enu per villichau .
mosheyude nayayaprmannaprkaram avallude shuddhiikarannkalam tikenjppoll
kadinjoolayaannokyeyum kattravinu vishuddhm aayirikyennam enu kattravinte nayayaprmannattill ejhyutiyirikyunnatupole
avane kattravinu apprippanum oru innkurrupravine yo randu prakyunjineyo kattravinte nayayaprmannttill kalpichaatupole yagam kajhyippanum avar avane yerooshalemilekyu kondupoyi .
yerooshalemill shimeyan enu perullellaru manukshayn undayirunu ; i manukshayn niitimanum yisrayelinte aashasattinnayi kattirikyunnavanum aayirunu ; parishuddhatmavum avante mell undayirunu .
kattravinte krisatuvine kannummube marannam kankayillennu parishuddhatmavinall avanu arullappadu undayirunu .
avan aatmniyogattall daivalayattill chenu . yeshu ennpaitalinuvendi nayayaprmannattinte chadtprkaram cheyvan ammyappnmar avane akattu konduchennappoll
avan avane kayaill eenti daivatte pukajhytti :
" ippoll nathtiruvachanampole nii adiyane samadhanattode vidtyakyunu .
jatikallkyu vellippeduvanullallprkashavum ninte janamayyisrayelinte mahatvumayi
nii sakaljatikalludeyum mumbill orukyiyirikyunnninte rakshaye
ente kannu kanduvalela " enu parranju .
ingane avanekyurrichau parranjtill avante appnum ammyum aryaappedtu .
pinne shimeyan avare anugrhichau avante ammyaymarriyayodu : anekahradayangallile vicharam vellippedendatinu ivane yisrayelill palarudeyum viekyum ejhyunnelpinum marruttu parrayunnadayallattinu mayi vechairikyunu .
ninte sntprannanillkoodiyum oruvall kadakyum enu parranju .
aasher gotrttill phanoovelinte makallayhannennoru prvachaki undayirunu ; avall kanayakal ttill pinne bhattrvinodukoode eejhyusamvram kajhyichau ennpattunalu samvram vidhavayum vallare vayassu chennavallumayi
daivalayam vidtu piriyate upavasattodum pratthrnyodumkoode ravum pakalum aaradhanacheyatu ponu .
anajhyikayill avallum aduttuninu daivatte satutichau , yerooshaleminte viindeduppine kattirunnellavarodum avanekyurrichau prsatavichau .
kattravinte nayayaprmannattill kalpichairikyunnato kyeyum nivattrichaasheksham avar galiilayill tangallude padtnnamaynasarrettilekyu madangippoyi .
paitall vallannaru njanam nirranju , aatmavill balappedtuponu ; daivakrapayum avanmell undayirunu .
avante ammyappnmar aandutorrum pesahaperunallinu yerooshalemilekyu pokum .
avanu pantrndu vayassayappoll avar pativupole perunallinu poyi .
perunall kajhyinju madangipporuboll balanayyeshu yerooshalemill tamasichau ; ammyappnmaro arrinjilla .
sahayatrkyarude koodtttill undayirikyum enu avar uhichaidtu oru divasatte vajhyiponu ; pinne avane bandukylludeyum parichayakyarudeyum idayill tiranju .
kannanjidtu avane anevkshichaukondu yerooshalemilekyu madangippoyi .
moonu nall kajhyinjsheksham avan daivalayattill upadeshtakynmarude naduvill irikyunnatum avarude upadesham kellkyyum avarodu chodikyyum cheyaunnatum kandu .
avante vakyu kedtvakyerllavakyrum avante vivekattilum uttrangallilum visyam tonni .
avane kandidtu avar atishayichau : amm avanodu : makane , njangallodu ingane cheyattu entu ? ninte appnum njanum vaysanichaukondu ninne tiranju enu parranju .
avan avarodu : enne tiranjtu entinu ? ente pitavinullallatill njan irikyendatu enu ningall arriyunnillayo enu parranju .
avan tangallodu parranj vakyu avar grhichaill .
pinne avan avarodukoode irrangi , nasarrettill vanu avakyru kiijhyadangiyirunu . i kayaaarngallellam avante amm hradayattill samgrhichau .
yeshuvo njanattilum vallachaaryilum daivattinteyum manukshayrudeyum krapayilum mutinurvanu .
tibeyeeraskaisarude vyude patinancham aandill pontiyos piilattos yehoodaynadu vajhyuboll , herodavu galiilayilum avante sahodaranayphiilippos ituyaartrkhonittideshangallilum lusanayas abilenayilum idaprbhukynmarayum
hannavum kayaaphavum mahapurohitanmarayum irikyum kalam sekhayaaravinte makanayyohannannu marubhoomiyill vechau daivattinte arullappadu undayi .
avan yodtrannarikeyullallnadtill okyeyum vannu papmochanattinnayullallmanasantarasanam prsamgichau .
" marubhoomiyill villichau parrayunnavante vakyavitu : kattravi nte vajhyi orukyuvin ; avante patnirappakyuvin .
ellatajhyvarayum nikannuvarum ; ellamalayum kunnum tajhyum ; vallanjtu chovaayum dughardamayatu nirannvajhyiyayum tiirum ;
sakaljaddavum daivattinte rakshaye kannum " enningane yeshayaaprvachakante pusatkattill ejhyutiyi rikyunnatupole tanne .
avanall sanam eelpan vannpuruksharattodu avan parranjtu : sapprsantatikalle , varuvanullallkopatte ojhyinju oadippokuvan ningallkyu upadeshichau tannatu aar ?
manasantarattinnu yogaymayphalam kayippin . abraham njangallkyu pitavayidtundu ; ennu ullallam kondu parravan tuniyarutu ; abrahaminnu i kallukallillninnu makylle ullavakyuvan daivattinnu kajhyiyum ennu njan ningallodu parrayunnu .
ippoll tanne vrakshangallude chuvadtinnu kodali vechairikyunnu ; nallaphalam kaykyatt vraksham ellam vedti tiiyill idtukallayunnu .
ennall njangall entu cheyeennam ennu puruksharam avanodu chodichau .
atinnu avan : randu vasrtmullallavan illattvannu kodukydte ; bhakshannasadhanangall ullallavanum anganetanne cheyaadte ennu uttram parranju .
chukkkyarum sanam eelpan vannu : guro , njangall entucheyeeennam ennu avanodu chodichau .
ningallodu kalpichaatill adhikam onnum pirikyrutu ennu avan parranju .
padnavum avanodu : njangall entu cheyeennam ennu chodichaatinnu : aareyum balalkyaram cheyaateyum chatiyayi onnum vangateyum ningallude shaballam mati ennuveppin ennu avarodu parranju .
janam kattuninnu ; avan krisatuvo ennu ellavarum hradayattill yohannanekyurrichau vicharichaukondirikyu boll
yohannan ellavarodum uttram parranjtu : njan ningalle vellallamkondu sanam kajhyippikyunnu ; ennall ennilum balavanayavan varunnu ; avante cherippinte varru ajhyippan njan yogaynalla ; avan ningalle parishuddhatmavukondum tiikondum sanam kajhyippikyum .
avannu viishumurram kayaill undu ; avan kallatte muttum vedippakyi kotambu kallappurayill koodtivekyyum patir kedatt tiiyill idtu chudtukallakayum cheyaum .
mattu palatum avan prbodhippichau kondu janattodu suvisheksham arriyichau .
ennall idaprbhuvayherodavu sahodarante bhayaar herodaynimittvum herodavum cheyat sakaladokshangall nimittvum yohannan avane aakshepikyyall
atellam cheyatu koodate avane tadavill aakyukayum cheyatu .
janam ellam sanam eelkyukayill yeshuvum sanam eettu pratthrikyuboll sggrm turrannu ,
parishuddhatmavu deharoopattill pravu ennapole avante mell irrangivannu . nii ente priyaputrn ; ninnill njan prsadichairikyunnu ennu sggrttill ninnu orushabdavum undayi .

yeshu parishuddhatmavu nirranjvanayi yodtran vidtu madangi ; aatmavu avane marubhoomiyilekyu nadatti ; pishachu avane nalpatu divasam pariikshichaukondirunnu .
adivasangallill avan onnum bhakshichailla ; avkajhyinjppoll avannu vishannu .
appoll pishachu avanodu : nii daivaputrn ekkill i kallinodu appmayittiiruvan kalpiky ennu parranju .
yeshu avanodu : manukshayn appmkondu matrmalljiivikyunnatu ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnu ennu uttram parranju .
pinne pishachu avane melodtu koodtikyondupoyi lokattile sakalarajayngalleyum kshannanerattill avannu kannichau :
i adhikaram okyeyum atinte mahatvum ninakyu taram ; atu ekkll eelpichairikyunnu ; enikyu manassullall vannu njan kodukyunnu .
nii enne namaskarichaall atellam nintetakum ennu avanodu parranju .
yeshu avanodu : ninte daivamaykattravine namaskarichau avane matrme aaradhikyavu ennu ejhyuti yirikyunnu ennu uttram parranju .
pinne avane yerushalemilekyu koodtikyondupoyi daivalayattinte agrttinmell nirrutti avanodu : nii daivaputrn ekkill ivide ninnu tajhyodtu chaduka .
" ninne kappan avan tante dootanmarodu ninnekyurrichau kalpikyyum
ninte kall kallinodu tadtatavannm avar ninne kayaill tangikyollallukayum cheyaum . " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnuvalelennu parranju .
yeshu avanodu : ninte daivamaykattravine pariikshi kyrutu ennu arullicheeyatirikyunnu ennu uttram parranju .
angane pishachu sakalapariikshayum tikechaasheksham kurre kalattekyu avane vidtumarri .
yeshu aatmavinte shakatiyode galiilekyu madangicheennu ; avante shruti chuttumullallnadtill okyeyum parannu .
avan avarude pallallikallill upadeshichau ; ellavarum avane prshamsichau .
avan vallannar nasarrettill vannu : shabaattill tante pativupole pallalliyill chennu vayippan ejhyunnettu ninnu .
yeshayaaprvachakante pusatkam avannu koduttu ; avan pusatkam vidattri :
" daridrnmarodu suvisheksham arriyippan kattravu enne abhikshekam cheykayall avante aatmavu ente mell undu ; baddhnmakyru vidutalum kurudanmakyru kyum prsamgippanum piidditanmare viduvichaayappanum
kattravinte prsadavaksharm prsamgippanum enne ayachairi kyunnu . " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnsthlam kandu .
pinne avan pusatkam madakyi shushrookshakyarannu tirike koduttidtu irunnu ; pallalliyilullallellavarudeyum kannu avakkll patinjirunnu .
avan avarodu : innu ningall ente vachanam kellkyyill i tiruvejhyuttinnu nivratti vannirikyunnu ennu parranjutudangi .
ellavarum avane pukajhytti , avante vayillninnu purrappedt lavannayvakyukallnimittm ayaarppedtu ; ivan yosephinte makan allayo ennu parranju .
avan avarodu : vaidaya , ninnettnne sekhaymakyukennullallpajhyanchollum kaphannarhoomill undayi kedttu ellam i ninte pitranagarattilum cheykennu ningall ennodu parrayum nischayam .
oru prvachakanum tante pitranagarattill sammtanallennu njan sataymayidtu ningallodu parrayunnu ennu parranju .
eeliiyavinte kalattu aakasham moovandum aarrumasavum adanjidtu deshattu engum mahkshamamundayappoll yisryelill palavidhavamar undayirunnu ennu njan yathatthrmayi ningallodu parrayunnu .
ennall siidonile sarepatyill oru vidhavayude adukylekyllate avarill aarudeyum adukylekyu eeliiyavine ayachailla .
avaannm elishaprvachakante kalattu yisrayelill palkukshttharogikall undayirunnu . surriyakyaranaynayaman allate avararum shuddhmayillennum avan parranju .
pallalliyilullallavar itukedtidtu ellavarum kopam nirranj varayi ejhyunnettu
avane padtnnattinnu purrattakyi avarude padtnnam pannitirunnmalayude vakyollam kondupoyi talakiijhyayi tallalliyiduvan bhavichau :
avano avarude naduvillkoodi kadannu poyi .
anantaram avan galiilayile oru padtnnamaykaphannarhoo mill chennu shabaattill avare upadeshichau ponnu .
avante vachanam adhikarattode aakayall avar avante upadeshattill visyichau .
avide pallalliyill ashuddhbhootam badhichoru manukshayn undayirunnu .
avan nasarrayanayyeshuve , vidu ; njangallkyum ninakyum tammill entu ? njangalle nashippippan vannirikyunnuvo ? nii aar ennu njan arriyunnu ; daivattinte parishuddhn tanne ennu urrakye nilavillichau .
mindarutu ; avane vidtupokennu yeshu shasichaappoll bhootam avane naduvill tallalliyidtu kedu onnum varuttate avane vidtupoyi .
ellavakyrum visyam undayi : i vachanam entu ? adhikarattodum shakatiyodumkoode avan ashuddhatmakyllodu kalpikyunnu ; avpurrappedtupokunnu ennu tammill parranjukondirunnu .
avante shruti chuttumullallnadengum parannu .
avan pallalliyillninnu irrangi shimonte viidtill chennu . shimonte ammaviyamm katthinajramkondu valanjiriky yall avar avallkyuvendi avanodu apekshichau .
avan avalle kuninju nokyi , jratte shasichau ; atu avalle vidtumarri ; avall udane ejhyunnettu avane shushrookshichau .
sooyaarn asatmikyuboll nanavaydhikall pidichdiinakyar ullallavar okyeyum avare avante adukyll konduvannu ; avan oaroruttnteyum mell kaivechaau avare sekhaymakyi .
palarillninnum bhootangall ; nii daivaputrnaykrisatu ennu nilavillichau parranjukondupurrappedtupoyi ; tan krisatu ennu avarrikakondu minduvan polum avan sammtikyate avaye shasichau .
neram velluttppoll avan purrappedtu oru nijjarnasthlttekyupoyi . puruksharam avane tiranju avante arikattuvannu tangalle vidtupokatirippan avane taduttu .
avan avarodu : njan mattullallpadtnnangallilum daivarajaym suvishekshikyendatakunnu ; itinnayidtlelenne ayachairikyunnatu ennu parranju .
angane avan galiilayile pallallikallill prsamgichau ponnu .
avan gannesaret tadakattinte karayill nilkyuboll puruksharam daivavachanam kellkyendatinnu avane tikyikyondirikyyill
randu padaku karekyu aduttu nilkyunnatu avan kandu ; avayillninnu miinpidikyar irrangi valkajhyukukayayirunnu .
apadakill shimonnullallatayonnill avan karrayi karayillninnu alpam nikyennam ennu avanodu apekshichau ; angane avan padakill irunnu puruksharatte upadeshichau .
samsarichau tiinnarppoll avan shimonodu : aajhyattilekyu niikyi miinpidittttinnu valirrakyuvin ennu parranju .
atinnu shimon : natha , njangall ratrimujhyuvanum addhvanichaidtum onnum kidtiyilla ; ekkilum ninte vakyinnu njan valirrakyam ennu uttram parranju .
avar angane cheyatppoll perutt miinkoodtm akappedtu valkiirrarrayi .
avar matte padakilullallkoodtallikall vannu sahayippan avare madi villichau . avar vannu padaku randum mungumrrakuvollam nirrechau .
shimon paretas atu kandidtu yeshuvinte kalkyll viinnu : kattrave , njan papiyaymanukshayn aakakondu enne vidtupokenname ennu parranju .
avakyru undayminpidittttill avannum avannodu koodeyullallavakyru ellavakyrum sambhrmam pidichairunnu .
shimonte koodtalliyayyakyob yohannan ennsebedimakyllkyum avaannmtanne . yeshu shimonodu : bhayappedenda , innu mutall nii manukshayre pidikyunnavan aakum ennu parranju .
pinne avar padakukalle karekyu aduppichaidtu sakalavum vidtu avane anugamichau .
avan oru padtnnattill irikyuboll kukshttham nirranjoru manukshayn yeshuvine kandu kavinnuviinnu : kattrave , ninakyu manassundekkill enne shuddhmakyuvan kajhyiyum ennu avanodu apekshichau .
yeshu kainiidti avane todtu : enikyu manassundu ; shuddhmakennu parranju . udane kukshttham avane vidtu marri .
avan avanodu : itu aarodum parrayarutu ; ennall poyi ninnettnne purohitannu kannichau , avakyru sakshayttinnayi moshe kalpichaatupole ninte shuddhii karannattinnullallvajhyipadu appriky ennu avanodukalpichau .
ennall avanekyurrichaullallvattrmanam adhikam parannu . vallare puruksharam vachanam kellkyendatinnum tangallude vayadhikallkyu sekhaym kidtendatinnum koodi vannu .
avano nijjarnadeshattu vangippoyi pratthrichaukondirunnu .
avan orudivasam upadeshikyuboll galiilayilum yehoodayyilumullallsakalagramattillninnum yerushalemill ninnum vannpariishanmarum nayayashasrtimarum avide irunnirunnu . sekhaymakyuvan kattravinte shakati avanodukoode undayirunnu .
appoll chilaallukall pakshavatam pidichoru manukshayne kidakyyill eduttukandu vannu ; avane akattu konduchennu avante mumbill veppan shrmichau .
puruksharam hetuvayi avane akattu konduchelluvan vajhyi kannanjidtu puramell kayarri oadu niikyi avane kidakyyode naduvill yeshuvinte mumbill irrakyivechau .
avarude vishasam kandidtu . avan : manukshaya , ninte papangall mochichautannirikyunnu ennu parranju .
shasrtimarum pariishanmarum daivadookshannam parrayunnivan aar ? daivam oruvan allate papangalle mochippan kajhyiyunnavan aar ennu chintichau tudangi .
yeshu avarude chintakalle arrinju avarodu : ningall hradayattill chintikyunnatu entu ?
ninte papangall mochichautannirikyunnu ennu parrayunnato ejhyunnettu nadaky ennu parrayunnato eetakunnu elluppm ennu chodichau .
ekkilum bhoomiyill papangalle mochippan manukshayputrnnu adhikaram undu ennu ningall arriyendatinnu - avan pakshavatakyaranodu : ejhyunnettu kidaky eduttu viidtilekyu pokennu njan ninnodu parrayunnu ennu parranju .
udane avar kankke avan ejhyannettu , tan kidannkidaky eduttu daivatte mahatiikarichaumkondu viidtilekyu poyi .
ellavarum visyampoondu daivatte mahatppedutti bhayam nirranjvarayi : innu nam apoovaarkayaarngalle kandu ennu parranju .
atintesheksham avan purrappedtu , levi ennu perullellaru chukkkkaran chukksthlattu irikyunnatu kandu ; enne anugamiky ennu avanodu parranju .
avan sakalavum vidtu ejhyunnettu avane anugamichau .
levi tante viidtill avannu oru valiyvirunnu orukyi ; chukkkyarum mattum valiyoru puruksharam avarodukoode pantiyill irunnu .
pariishanmarum avarude shasrtimarum avante shikshaynmarodu : ningall chukkkyarodum papikallodumkoode tinnu kudikyunnatu entu ennu parranju pirrupirruttu .
yeshu avarodu : diinakyakyrllate sekhaymullallavakyru vaidaynekyondu aavashaymill ;
njan niitimanmare allpapikalle aretmanasantarattinnu villippan vannirikyunnatu ennu uttram parranju .

yeshu avarodu : mannavallan toyjmakyarodukoode ullallappoll avare upavasam cheyaippan kajhyiyumo ?
mannavallan avare vidtupiriyendunnkalam varum ; annu , akalattu , avar upavasikyum ennu parranju .
oru upamayum avarodu parranju : aarum kodittunniky ndam kiirriyeduttu pajhyayavasrtttodu chettru tunnumarrilla . tunniyalo putiyatu kiirrukayum putiyakandam pajhyayatinodu cheratirikyyum cheyaum .

putuviinju putiyturuttiyill aretpakannaru vekyendatu .

avallude ammyappnmar visyichau . sambhavichaatu aarodum parrayarutu enu avan avarodu kalpichau .

vajhyikyu vadiyum pokynnavum appvum pannavum onum edukyrutu ; randu uduppum arutu .

aarekkilum ningalle kaikyollallatirunnall apadtnnam vidtu avarude nere sakshayttinnayi ningallude kalill ninu podi tadtikyllavin .

sambhavikyunnatu ellam idaprbhuvayherodavu kedtu .

yohannane tan shirachedam cheyatu ; ennall njan inganeyullallatu kellkyunnivan aar enu parranju avane kanman shrmichau .

pakall kajhyivarrayappoll pantiruvar aduttuvanu avanodu : ivide nam marubhoomiyill aayirikykondu puruksharam chuttumullallurukallilum kudikallilum poyi ratri pappranum aaharam vanguvanum vendi avare parranjyakyennam enu parranju .

oru manukshayn savaarlokavum nediidtu tannettan nashtamakyikyllakayo chetam varuttukayo cheyatall avanu entu pryojanam ?

pittennall avar malayillninu irrangivannappoll bahu puruksharam avane etirettu .
koodtttillninu orall nilavillichau : guro , ente makane kadakshikyennamenu njan ninnodu apekshikyunu ; avan enikyu eekajatan aakunu .

atine purrattakyuvan ninte shikshaynmarodu apekshichau ekkilum avakyru kajhyinjillenu parranju

avan varuboll tanne bhootam avane tallalliyidtu pideppichau . yeshu ashuddhatmavine shasichau balane sekhaymakyi , appne eelpichau .

yeshu avanodu : virodhikyrutu ; ningallkyu prtikoolmallattvan ningallkyu anukoolamalelenu parranju .
avante aarohannattinullallkalam tikayarrayappoll , avan yerooshalemilekyu yatryavan manassu urrappichau tanikyu mumbayi dootanmare ayachau .

apadtnnattekyall sodomaykyru anajhyikayill sahikyavatavum enu njan ningallodu parrayunu .

ente pitavu sakalavum ekkll bharamelpichairikyunu . putrn innavan enu pitavallate aarum arriyunnilla ; pitavu innavan enu putrnum putrn vellippedutti kyoduppan ichchikyunnavanum allate aarum arriyunnatumilla .

yonninevekyakyru adayallam aayatupole manukshay putrn i talamurrekyum aakum .

atinu yeshu : aamen , aamen njan ninnodu parrayunu : vellallattalum aatmavinalum janichaillekkill daivarajayttill kadappan aakyrum kajhyikayilla .
jaddattall janichaatu jaddam aakunu ; aatmavinall janichaatu aatmavu aakunu .

appoll avar avane errivan kallu eduttu , yeshuvo marranju daivalayam vidtupoyi .
avan kadanu pokuboll pirraviyile kurudanayoru manukshayne kandu .

ingane parranjidtu avan nilattu tuppi tuppll kondu cherrundakyi cherru avante kanninmell pooshi
nii chenu shiloham kullattill kajhyukukenu avanodu parranju ; shiloham ennatinu ayakyppedtvan ennatthrm . avan poyi kajhyuki , kannu kannunnavanayi madangivanu .
ayalkyarum avane mube irakyunnavanayi kandavarum : ivanallayo avide irunnu bhikshyachichaavan enu parranju .

avar avanodu : ninte kannu turrannatu engane
enu chodichaatinu avan : yeshu enu perullmanukshayn cherrundakyi ente kanninmell pooshi : shiloham kullattill chenu kajhyukukenu ennodu parranju ; njan poyi kajhyuki k prapichau enu uttram parranju .
avan evide enu avar avanodu chodichaatinu : njan arriyunnillenu avan parranju .
kurudanayirunnavane avar pariishanmarude adukyll kondupoyi .
yeshu cherrundakyi avante kannu turrannatu shabaat nallill aayirunnu .
avan k prapichaatu engane enu pariishanmarum avanodu chodichau . avan avarodu : avan ente kanninmell cherru techau njan kajhyuki ; k prapichairikyunu enu parranju .
pariishanmarill chilar : i manukshayn shabaat prmannikyykakondu daivattinte adukyll ninu vannavanallenu parranju . mattu chilar : papiyayoru manukshaynu inganeyulladayallangall cheyvan engane kajhyiyum enu parranju ; angane avarude idayill oru bhinnatundayi .

kprapichaavante ammyappnmare villichau chodikyuvollam avan kurudanayirunu enum k prapichau enum yehoodar vishsichaillal .
kurudanayi janichau enu ningall parrayunnningallude makan ivan tanneyo ? ennall avanu ippoll kannu kannunnatu engane enu avar avarodu chodichau .
avante ammyappnmar : ivan njangallude makan enum karudanayi janichaavan enum njangall arriyunnu .
ennall kannu kannunnatu engane enu arriyunnilla ; avante kannu aar tarrannu enum arriyunnilla ; avanodu chodippin ; avannu prayam undalela ; avan tanne parrayum enu uttram parranju .

aamen , aamen , njan ningallodu parrayunu , aadtin tojhyuttill vatiloode kadakyate verre vajhyiyayi kayarrunnavan kallanum kavachaarkyaranum aakunu .

atinnu yeshu : i shabdam ente nimittmalla , ningallude nimittm aretundayatu .
ippoll i lokattinte nayayavidhi aakunu ; ippoll i lokattinte prbhavine purrattu tallikyllayum .
njano bhoomiyill ninu uyattrppedtall ellavareyum ekklekyu aakaksharikyum enu uttram parranju .
itu tan marippanullmarannavidham soochippichau parranjtareta .
puruksharam avanodu : krisatu ennekyum irikyum enu njangall nayayaprmannattill vayichau kedtirikyunu ; pinne manukshayputrn uyattrppedendatenu nii parrayunnatu engane ? i manukshayputrn aar ennu chodichau .
atinu yeshu avarodu : ini kurrayakalam matrm vellichaam ningallude idayill irikyum ; irull ningalle pidakyatirippan ningallkyu vellichaam ulledattollam nadannukollvin . irullill nadakyunnavan tan evide pokunu enu arriyunnillalela .
ningall vellichaattinte makyll aakendatinu vellichaam ulledattollam vellichaattill vishsippin enu parranju .
itu samsarichaidtu yeshu vangippoyi avare vidtu marranju . avar kannke avan itr vallare adayallangalle cheyatidtum avar avanill vishsichaillal .
" kattrave , njangall kellppichaatu aar vishsichairikyunu ? kattavinte bhujam aakyru vellippedtirikyunu ? " enu yeshayaprvachakan parranj vachanam nivrattiyavan idavanu .
avakyru vishsippan kajhyinjilla ; atinte karannam yeshayaavu verre oredattuparrayunnatu :
" avar kannukondu kannukayo hradayam kondu grhikyyo manam tirikayo tan avare sekhaymakyukayo cheyaatirikyendatinu avarude kannu avan kurudakyi hradayam tadippichairikyunu . "
yeshayaavu avante tejassu kandu avanekyurrichau samsarichaatu kondakunu itu parranjtu .

avar daivattalullmanattekyall manukshayralullmanatte adhikam senhichau .
yeshu villichauparranjtu : ennill vishsikyunnavan ennilallenne ayachaavanill tanne vishsikyunu .
enne kannunnavan enne ayachaavane kannunu .
ennill vishsikyunnavan aarum irullill vasikyatirippan njan vellichaamayi lokattill vannirikyunu .
ente vachanam kedtu prmannikyattvane njan vidhikyunnilla ; lokatte vidhippanalla , lokatte rakshippanaretnjan vannirikyunnatu .
ente vachanam kaikyollate enne tallikyllayunnavane nayayam vidhikyunnavan undu ; njan samsarichavachanam tanne odukytte nallill avane nayayam vidhikyum .
njan syamayi samsarichaidtilla ; enne ayachapitavu tanne njan innatu parrayennam enum innatu samsarikyennam enum kalpantannirikyunu .
avante kalpannitayjiivan enu njan arriyunu ; aakayall njan samsarikyunnatu pitavu ennodu arullicheeyattu pole tanne samsarikyunu .

nii orunallum ente kall kajhyukukayillenu paretas parranju . atinu yeshu : njan ninne kajhyukanjall ninakyu ennodu koode pakkillenu uttram parranju . appoll shimon paretas :

itu ningall arriyunu ekkill cheyatall bhagayvanmar .

atu sambhavikyuboll njan tanne mashiihenu ningall vishsikyendatinu njan ippoll atu sambhavikyum mube ningallodu parrayunu .
aamen , aamen , njan ningallodu parrayunu : njan ayakyunnavane kaikyollunnavan enne kaikyollunu ; enne kaikyollunnavan enne ayachaavane kaikyollunu .
itu parranjidtu yeshu ullam kalangi : aamen , aamen , njan tingallodu parrayunu : ningallill oruttn enne kannichaukodukyum enu sakshiikarichauparranju .
itu aarekyurrichau parrayunu enu shikshaynmar samshayichau tammill tammill nokyi .

kunjungalle , njan ini kurranjonu matrm ningallodukoode irikyum ; ningall enne anevkshikyum ; njan pokunnidattu ningallkyu varuvan kajhyikayillenu njan yehoodanmarodu parranjtupole inu ningallodum parrayunu .
ningall tammill tammill senhikyennam enu putiyoru kalpannjan ningallkyu tarunu ; njan ningalle senhichaatupole ningallum tammill tammill senhikyennam enu tanne .
ningallkyu tammill tammill senham undekkill ningall ente shikshaynmar enu ellavarum arriyum .
shimon paretas avanodu : kattrave , nii evide pokunu enu chodichaatinu : njan pokunnidattekyu ninakyu ippoll enne anugamippan kajhyikayilla ; pinnattetill nii enne anugamikyum enu yeshu avanodu uttram parranju .
kattrave , ippoll enikyu ninne anugamippan kajhyiyatttu entu ? njan ente jiivane ninakyu vendi vechaukallayum enu parranju .
atinu yeshu : ninte jiivane enikyuvendi vechaukallayumo ? aamen , aamen , njan ninnodu parrayunu : nii moonu pravashaym enne tallipprrayuvollam kojhyi kookukayillenu uttram parranju .
ningallude hradayam kalangippokarutu ; daivattill vishsippin , ennilum vishsippin .

tomas avanodu : kattrave , nii evide pokunu enu njangall arriyunnilla ; pinne vajhyi engane arriyum enu parranju .

ningall enne arrinju ekkill ente pitavineyum arriyumayirunu ; inu mutall ningall avane arriyunu ; avane kandumirikyunu enu parranju .
philippos avanodu : kattrave , pitavine njangallkyu kannichau tarennam ; ennall njangallkyu mati enu parranju .

njan pitavilum pitavu ennilum aakunu enu nii vishsikyunnillayo ? njan ningallodu parrayunnvachanam syamayidtllsamsarikyunnatu ; pitavu ennill vasichau kondu tante prvratti cheyaunu .
njan pitavilum pitavu ennilum enu enne vishsippin ; alelkkill prvratti nimittm enne vishsippin .
aamen , aamen , njan ningallodu parrayunu ; njan cheyaunnprvratti ennill vishsikyunnavanum cheyaum ; njan pitavinte adukyll pokunnatu kondu atill valiyatum avan cheyaum .
ningall ente namattill apekshikyunnatu okyeyum pitavu putrnill mahatppedendatinu njan cheyatutarum .
ningall ente namattill ennodu apekshikyunnatu okyeyum njan cheyatutarum .
ningall enne senhikyunnu ekkill ente kalpanakalle kattukollum .

njan ningalle anatharayi vidukayilla ; njan ningallude adukyll varum .

yeshu avanodu enne senhikyunnavan ente vachanam prmannikyum ; ente pitavu avane senhikyum ; njangall avante adukyll vanu avanodukoode vasam cheyaum .
enne senhikyattvan ente vachanam prmannikyunnilla ; ningall kellkyunnvachanam entetallenne ayachapitavintetaretenu uttram parranju .

samadhanam njan ningallkyu tannechaupokunu ; ente samadhanam njan ningallkyu tarunu ; lokam tarunnatupole allnjan ningallkyu tarunnatu . ningallude hradayam kalangarutu , bhrmikyyum arutu .
njan pokayum ningallude adukyll madangi varikayum cheyaum enu njan ningallodu parranjtu kedtuvalela ; ningall enne senhikyunu ekkill njan pitavinte adukyll pokunnatinall ningall santokshikyumayi runu ; pitavu ennekyall valiyavanalela .
atu sambhavikyuboll ningall vishsikyendatinu njan ippoll atu sambhavikyum mube ningallodu parranjiri kyunu .
njan ini ningallodu vallare samsarikyyilla ; lokattinte prbhu varunu ; avanu ennodu oru kayarrvumillal .
ekkilum njan pitavine senhikyunu enum pitavu ennodu kalpichaatupole njan cheyaunu enum lokam arriyadte . ejhyunnelpin : nam poka .
njan sakshall muntirivalliyum ente pitavu todtkyaranum aakunu .
ennill kaykyatt kombu okyeyum avan niikyikyllayunu ; kaykyunnatu okyeyum adhikam phalam kaykyendatinu chettivedippakyunu .
njan ningallodu samsarichavachanam nimittm ningall ippoll shuddhiyullavarakunu .
ennill vasippin ; njan ningallilum vasikyum ; kombinu muntirivalliyill vasichaidtllate syamayi kaypan kajhyiyatttu pole ennill vasichaidtllate ningallkyu kajhyikayillal .
njan muntirivalliyum ningall kombukallum aakunu ; oruttn ennilum njan avanilum vasikyunu ekkill avan vallare phalam kaykyum ; enne pirinju ningallkyu onum cheyvan kajhyikayillal .
ennill vasikyattvane oru kombupole purrattu kallanjidtu avan unnangippokunu ; avakchettru tiiyill idunu ; atu ventu pokum .
ningall ennilum ente vachanam ningallilum vasichaall ningall ichchikyunnatu entekkilum apekshippin ; atu ningallkyu kidtum .
ningall vallare phalam kaykyunnatinall ente pitavu mahatppedunu ; angane ningall ente shikshaynmar aakum .
pitavu enne senhikyunnatu pole njanum ningalle senhikyunu ; ente senhattill vasippin .
njan ente pitavinte kalpanakall prmannichau avante senhattill vasikyunnatu pole ningall ente kalpanakall prmannichaall ente senhattill vasikyum .
ente santoksham ningallill irippanum ningallude santoksham poonnrmakuvanum njan itu ningallodu samsarichairikyunu .
njan tingalle senhichairikyunnatupole ningallum tammill tammill senhikyennam ennakunu ente kalpana .
senhitanmakyru vendi jiivane kodukyunnatilum adhikamullsenham aakyrum illa .
njan ningallodu kalpikyunnatu cheyatall ningall ente senhitanmar tanne .
yajamanan cheyaunnatu dasan arriyaykakondu njan ningalle dasanmar enu ini parrayunnilla ; njan ente pitavinodu kedttu ellam ningallodu arriyichaatu kondu ningalle senhitanmar enu parranjirikyunu .
ningall enne tiranjeduttu ennalla , njan ningalle tiranjeduttu ningall poyi phalam kaykyndatinu ningallude phalam nilanilkyendatinum ningalle aakyivechaumirikyunu ; ningall ente namattill pitavinodu apekshikyunnatokyeyum avan ningallkyu taruvanayidtu tanne .
ningall tammill tammill senhikyendatinu njan itu ningallodu kalpikyunu .
lokam ningalle pakekyunu ekkill atu ningallkyu mube enne pakechairikyunu enu arrivin .
ningall lokakyar aayirunu ekkill lokam tanikyu sntamayatine senhikyumayirunu ; ennall ningall lokakyarayirikyate njan ningalle lokattill ninu tiranjedutttu kondu lokam ningalle pakekyunu .
dasan yajamananekyall valiyavanallenu njan ningallodu parranj vakyu oapprin . avar enne upadrvichau ekkill ningalleyum upadrvikyum ; ente vachanam prmannichau ekkill ningalludetum prmannikyum .
ekkilum enne ayachaavane avar arriyaykakondu ente namam nimittm itu okyeyum ningallodu cheyaum .
njan vanu avarodu samsarikyatirunnekkill avakyur papam illayirunu ; ippojhyo avarude papattinu ojhyikajhyivillal .
enne pakekyunnavan ente pitavineyum pakekyunu .
mattarum cheyatidtillatt prvrattikalle njan avarude idayill cheyatirunnillekkill avakyru papam illayirunu ; ippojhyo avar enneyum ente pitavineyum kannkayum pakekyukayum cheyatirikyunu .
" avar verrute enne pakechau " enu avarude nayayprmannattill ejhyutiyirikyunnvachanam nivratti yakendatinu tanne .
njan pitavinte adukyll ninu ningallkyu ayappanullkayarrsthnayi pitavinte adukyll ninu purrappedunnsatayatmavu varuboll avan ennekyurrichau sakshaym parrayum .
ningallum aadimutall ennodukoode irikykondu sakshaym parravin .
ningall idarrippokatirippan njan itu ningallodu samsarichairikyunu .
avar ningalle pallibhrshtar aakyum ; atryumallningalle kolalunnavan ellam daivattinu vajhyipadu kajhyikyunu enu vicharikyunnnajhyikvarunu .
avar pitavineyum enneyum arriyaykakondu ingane cheyaum .
atinte najhyikvaruboll njan atu ningallodu parranjidtundenu ningall oakyerndatinu itu ningallodu samsarichairikyunu ; aadiyill itu ningallodu parrayanjtu njan ningallodu koode irikykondareta .
ippojhyo njan enne ayachaavante adukyll pokunu : nii evide pokunu enu ningall aarum ennodu chodikyunnillal .
ekkilum itu ningallodu samsarikykondu ningallude hradayattill du : kham nirranjirikyunu .
ennall njan ningallodu sataym parrayunu ; njan pokunnatu ningallkyu pryojanam ; njan pokanjall kayarrsthn ningallude adukyll varikayilla ; njan poyall avane ningallude adukyll ayakyum .
avan vanu papattekyurrichaum niitiyekyurrichaum nayayavidhiyekyurrichaum lokattinu bodham varuttum .
avar ennill vishsikyaykakondu papatte kyurrichaum
njan pitavinte adukyll pokayum ningall ini enne kannatirikyyum cheyaunnatu kondu niitiye kyurrichaum
i lokattinte prbhu vidhikyppedtirikykondu nayayvidhiye kyurrichaum tanne .
iniyum vallare ningallodu parravan undu ; ennan ningallkyu ippoll vahippan kajhyivillal .
satayttinte aatmavu varubojhyo avan ningalle sakalsatayttilum vajhyi nadattum ; avan syamayi samsarikyate tan kellkyunnatu samsarikyyum varuvanullatu ningallkyu arriyichau tarikayum cheyaum .
avan enikyullatill ninu eduttu ningallkyu arriyichau tarunnatu kondu enne mahatppeduttum .
pitavinnullatu okyeyum enikyullatu ; atukondaretavan enikyullatill ninu eduttu ningallkyu arriyichau tarum enu njan parranjtu .
kurranjonnu kajhyinjidtu ningall enne kannukayilla ; pinneyum kurranjonnu kajhyinjidtu ningall enne kannum .
avante shikshaynmarill chilar : kurranjonu kajhyinjidtu ningall enne kannukayilla ; pinneyum kurranjonu kajhyinjidtu enne kannum enum pitavinte adukyll pokunu enum avan nammodu i parrayunnatu entu enu tammill chodichau .
kurranjonu enu i parrayunnatu entakunu ? avan entu samsarikyunu enu nam arriyunnillenum avar parranju .
avar tannodu chodippan aagrhikyunu enu arrinju yeshu avarodu parranjtu : kurranjonu kajhyinjidtu enne kannukayilla ; pinneyum kurranjonu kajhyinjidtu enne kannum enu njan parrakayall ningall tammill tammill chodikyunuvo ?
aamen , aamen , njan ningallodu parrayunu : ningall karanju vilapikyum ; lokamo santokshikyum ; ningall du : khikyum ; ennall ningallude du : kham santokshamayittiirum .
srtii prsavikyuboll tante najhyikvannatu kondu avallkyu du : kham undu , kunjine prsavichaashekshamo oru manukshayn lokattilekyu pirrannirikyunnsantoksham nimittm avall tante kashtam pinne okyrunnillal .
angane ningallkyum ippoll du : kham undu ekkilum njan pinneyum ningalle kannum ; ningallude hradayam santokshikyum ; ningallude santoksham aarum ningallill ninu eduttukallakayillal .
anu ningall ennodu onum chodikyyilla . aamen , aamen , njan ningallodu parrayunu : ningall pitavinodu apekshikyunnatokyeyum avan ente namattill ningallkyu tarum .
inuvare ningall ente namattill onum apekshichai dtilla ; apekshippin ; ennall ningallude santoksham poonnrmakumvannm ningallkyu labhikyum .
itu njan sadrashamayi ningallodu samsarichairikyunu ; ekkilum njan ini sadrashamayi ningallodu samsari kyate pitavine sambandichau spashtamayi ningallodu arriyikyunnnajhyikvarunu .
anu ningall ente namattill apekshikyum ; njan ningallkyu vendi pitavinodu apekshikyum enu njan parrayunnillal .
ningall enne senhichau , njan pitavinte adukyll ninu vannirikyunu enu vishsichairikykondu pitavu tanum ningalle senhakyunu .
njan pitavinte adukyll ninu purrappedtu lokattill vannirikyunu ; pinneyum lokatte vidtu pitavinte adukyll pokunu .
atinu avante shikshaynmar : ippoll nii sadrasham onum parrayate spashtamayi samsarikyunu .
nii sakalavum arriyunu enum aarum ninnodu chodippan ninakyu aavashaym illenum njangall ippoll arriyunu ; itinall nii daivattinte adukyll ninnu vannirikyunu enu njangall vishsikyunu enu parranju .
yeshu avarodu : ippoll ningall vishsikyunuvo ?
ningall oaroruttn tantante sntattilekyu chitarrippokayum enne eekanayi vidukayum cheyaunnnajhyikvarunu ; vanumirikyunu ; pitavu ennodukoode ullatu kondu njan eekanalltanum .
ningallkyu ennill samadhanam undakendatinu itu ningallodu samsarichairikyunu ; lokattill ningallkyu kashtam undu ; ekkilum dhaiyaarppeduvin ; njan lokatte jayichairikyunu enu parranju .
itu samsarichaidtu yeshu sggrttekyu nokyi parranjte ntennall : pitave , najhyikvannirikyunu ; ninte putrn ninne mahatppeduttendatinu putrne mahatppedu ttenname .

nii enikyu tannatu ellam ninte pakyll ninu aakunu enu avar ippoll arrinjirikyunu .

njan avakyru vendi apekshikyunu ; lokattinu vendi alla ; nii enikyu tannidtullavar ninakyullavar aakkondu avakyru vendiyaretnjan apekshikyunnatu .
entetu ellam nintetum nintetu entetum aakunu ; njan avarill mahatppedtumirikyunu .
ini njan lokattill irikyunnillivaro lokattill irikyunu ; njan ninte adukyll varunu . parishuddh pitave , avar nammeppole onnakendatinu nii enikyu tannirikyunnninte namattill avare kattu kollenname .
avarodukoode irunnappoll njan avare nii enikyu tannirikyunnninte namattill kattukondirunu ; njan avare sookshichau ; tiruvejhyuttinu nivratti varendatinu anashayogaynallate avarill aarum nashichau poyi dtillal .
ippojhyo njan ninte adukyll varunu ; ente santoksham avakyru ullill poonnrmakendatinu itu lokattill vechau samsarikyunu .
njan avakyru ninte vachanam koduttirikyunu ; njan lekikanallatttu pole avarum lekikanmarllaykkondu lokam avare pakechau .
avare lokattill ninu edukyennam ennalla , dushtante kayaill akappedatavannm avare kattukollennam ennaretnjan apekshikyunnatu .
njan lekikanallatttupole avarum lekiknmarallal .
satayttall avare vishuddhiikarikyenname ; ninte vachanam sataym aakunu .
nii enne lokattilekyu ayachaatupole njan avareyum lokattilekyu ayachairikyunu .
avarum sakshall vishuddhiikarikyppedtvar aakendatinu njan avakyru vendi ennettnne vishuddhiikarikyunu .
ivakyru vendimatrmalla , ivarude vachanattall ennill vishsippanirikyunnavakyru vendiyum njan apekshi kyunu .
nii enne ayachairikyunu enu lokam vishsippan avar ellavarum onnakendatinu , pitave , nii ennilum njan ninnilum aakunnatupole avarum nammill aakendatinu tanne .
nii enikyu tannidtullmahatm njan avakyru koduttirikyunu :
nii enne ayachairikyunu enum nii enne senhikyunnatu pole avareyum senhikyunu enum lokam arrivan , nam onnayirikyunnatu pole avarum onnakendatinu njan avarilum nii ennilumayi avar eekayttill tikenjvarayirikyendatinu tanne .
pitave , nii lokasthapanattinu mube enne senhichairikykondu enikyu nalkiymahatm nii enikyu tannidtullavar kannendatinu njan irikyunnidattu avarum ennodu koode irikyennam enu njan ichchikyunu .
niitiyullpitave , lokam ninne arrinjidtilla ; njano ninne arrinjirikyunu ; nii enne ayachairikyunu enu ivarum arranjirikyunu .
nii enne senhikyunnsenham avarill aakuvanum njan avarill aakuvanum njan ninte namam avakyru vellippeduttiyirikyunu ; iniyum vellippeduttum .

mahapurohitan yeshuvinodu avante shikshaynmareyum upadeshatteyum kurrichau chodichau .

ente rajaym eehikamalla ; ente rajaym eehikam aayirunnu ekkill enne yehoodanmarude kayaill eelpikyatavannm ente chevakar poradumayirunu ; ennall ente rajaym eehikamallenu uttram parranju .

pinne tomasinodu : ninte virall ingodtu niidti ente kaikalle kannka ; ninte kai niidti ente vilppurrattu iduka ; avishasi aakate vishasiyayiriky enu parranju .

shimon paretasum didimos enntomasum galiilayilullkanayile nathanayelum sebedimakyllum avante shikshaynmarill verre randu perum orumichau koodiyirunu .

padakinte valattubhagattu valviishuvin ; ennall ningallkyu kidtum enu avan avarodu parranju ; avar viishi , miininte peruppm hetuvayi atu valippan kajhyinjillal .
yeshu senhichashikshayn paretasinodu : atu kattravu aakunu enu parranju ; kattruvu aakunu enu shimon paretas kedtidtu , tan nnakayall akki arayill chutti kadalill chadi .

randamatum avanodu : yohannante makanayshimone , nii enne senhikyunnuvo enu chodichau . atinu avan : uvau , kattrave , enikyu ninnodu priyamundu enu nii arriyunnuvalelenu parranju . ente aadukalle paliky enu avan avanodu parranju .
moonnamatum avanodu : yohannante makanayshimone , ninakyu ennodu priyamundo enu chodichau . ennodu priyamundo enu moonnamatum chodikyyall paretas du : khichau : kattrave , nii sakalavum arriyunu ; enikyu ninnodu priyamundu enum nii arriyunnu enu avanodu parranju . yeshu avanodu : ente aadukalle meyky .
aamen , aamen , njan ninnodu parrayunu ; nii yevanakyaran aayirunnappoll nii tanne arkedti ishtamulledattu nadanu ; vayassnayshekshamo nii kai niidtukayum mattoruttn ninte arkedti ninakyu ishtamillatt idattekyu ninne kondu pokayum cheyaum enu parranju .

paretas tirinju yeshu senhichashikshayn pin chellunnatu kandu ; attajhyattill avante nenchodu chanju kondu : kattrave , ninne kannichau kodukyunnavan aar enu chodichaatu ivan tanne .
avane paretas kandidtu : kattrave , ivanu entu bhavikyum enu yeshuvinodu chodichau .
yeshu avanodu : njan varuvollam ivan irikyennmenu enikyu ishtam undekkill atu ninakyu entu ? nii enne anugamiky enu parranju .
aakayall ashikshayn marikyyillennoru shruti sahodaranmarude idayill paranu . yeshuvo : avan marikyyillennalla , njan varuvollam ivan irikyennam enu enikyu ishtamundekkill atu ninakyu entu ennaretavanodu parranjtu .
i shikshayn itinekyurrichau sakshaym parrayunnavanum itu ejhyutiyavanum aakunu ; avante sakshaym sataym enu njangall arriyunu .

yisrayell purukshanmare , i vachanam kedtu kollvin . ningall tanne arriyumpole daivam avanekyondu ningallude naduvill cheyaichashtikallum atbhutangallum adayallangallum kondu daivam ningallkyu kannichautannpurukshanayi

atu kondu ente hradayam santokshichau , ente navu aanandichau , ente jaddavum prtayashayode vasikyum .

aprvachakante vakyu kellkyatt eevanum janattinte idayill ninu chedikyppedum . " enu meshe parranju valela .

avar janattodu samsarichau kondirikyuboll tanne purohitanmarum daivalayattile padanayakanum sadookayrum avarude nere vanu ,
avar janatte upadeshikyyalum marichaavarill ninullpunarutthanatte yeshuvinte drashtantattall arriyikyyalum niirasappedtu .

i balahiinmanukshaynu undayupakaram nimittm ivan entonninall sekhaymayi enu njangalle inu visatrikyunu ekkill

viidu panniyunnavarayningall tallikyllanjidtu konninte moolakyllayittiinnar kallu ivan tanne .
matteruttnilum rakshilla ; nam rakshikyppeduvan aakashattin kiijhyill manukshayrude idayill nalkappedt verroru namavum illal .

nayayadhipasamghattill ninu purrattu pokuvan kalpi chaaaidtu avar tammill aalochichau :
i manukshayre entu cheyeendu ? prtaykshamayoru adayallam avar cheyatirikyunu enu yerooshalemill pakyrunnellavakyrum prsiddhmalela ; nikshedhippan namukyu kajhyivillal .

pinne avare villichaidtu : yeshuvinte namattill asheksham samsarikyrutu , upadeshikyyum arutu enu kalpichau .
atinu paretasum yohannanum : daivattekyall adhikam ningalle anusarikyunnatu daivattinte mumbake nayayamo enu vidhippin .
njangallkyo njangall kandum kedtumirikyunnatu prsatavikytirippan kajhyiyunnatallenu uttram parranju .
