i atbhutattall sekhaym prapichamanukshaynu nalpatill adhikam vayassullavanayirunu .
vidtyachasheksham avar koodtallikallude adukyll chenu mahapurohitanmarum mooppnmarum tangallodu parranjtu ellam arriyichau .
atu kedtidtu avar orumanappedtu daivattodu nilavillichau parranjtu : aakashavum bhoomiyum samudrvum avayilullsakalavum undakyiynathane ,
" jatikall kalahikyunnatum vamshangall vaytthrmayatu niroopikyunnatum entu ?
bhoomiyile rajakynmar anninirakyukayum adhipatikall kattravinu virodhamayum avante abhikshiktanu virodhamayum onnichau koodukayum cheyatirikyunu " enu ninte dasanaydaviid mukhantaram parishuddhatmavinall arullicheeyatvane ,
ni abhikshekam cheyat yeshu ennninte parishuddhdasanu virodhamayi herodavum pontiyospiilattosum jatikallum yisrayell janavumayi i nagarattill onnichau koodi ,
sambhavikyennam enu ninte kayaum ninte aalochanayum munniyamichaatu okyeyum cheyatirikyunu sataym .
ippojhyo kattrave , avarude bhiikshannikalle nokyenname .
sekhaymakyuvan ninte kai niidtunnatinalum ninte parishuddhdasanayyeshuvinte namattall adayallangallum atbhutangallum undakunnatinalum ninte vachanam poonnr dhaiyarrttodum koode prsatavippan ninte dasanmakyru krapnalkenname .
ingane pratthrichaappoll avar koodiyirunnsthlam kulungi ; ellavarum parishuddhatmavu nirranjvarayi daivavachanam dhaiyarrttode prsatavichau .
vishsichaavarude koodtm eekahradayavum eekamanassum ullavarayirunu ; tanikyullatu onum sntam enu aarum parranjilla ; sakalavum avakyru potuvayirunu .
apposatlanmar mahashtiyode kattravayyeshu vinte punarutthanattinu sakshaym parranjuvanu ; ellavakyrum dharallam kraplabhichairunu .
mudtullavan aarum avarill undayirunnilla ; nilangalludeyo viidukalludeyo udamasthnmarayavar okyeyum avaye vittu vilkonduvanu
apposatlanmarude kalkyll vekyum ; pinne oaroru ttnu avanavante aavashaym pole vibhagichaukodukyum .
prbodhanaputrn ennu atthrmullbannarbas enu apposatlanmar marruper villichakuprdiipukaranayyoseph ennoru levayn
tanikyundayirunnnilam vittu pannam konduvanu apposatlanmarude kalkyll vechau .
ennall ananayas enu perulloru purukshan tante bhayarryaysaphiirayodu koode oru nilam vittu .
bhayarryude arrivode vilayill kurre eduttuvechau oramsham kondu vanu apposatlanmarude kalkyll vachau .
appoll paretas : ananayase , parishuddhatmavinodu vayajam kannippanum nilattinte vilayill kurre eduttu veppanum sattan ninte hradayam kaivashamakyiyatu entu ?
atu vilkyum mube nintetayirunnillayo ? vittshekshvum ninte kaivasham allanjuvo ? i kayaarttill nii manassu vechaatu entu ? manukshayrodalldaivattodaretnii vayajam kannichaatu enu parranju .
i vakyu kedtidtu ananayas viinnu prannane vidtu ; itu kedtvakyru ellavakyrum mahbhayam undayi .
balaykyar ejhyunnettu avane shiilapotinju purrattu kondu poyi kujhyichaidtu .
eekadesham moonnu mannineram kajhyinjppoll avante bhayarr i sambhavichaatu onum arriyate akattu vanu .
paretas avallodu : iretakyo ningall nilam vitttu ? parrakenu parranju ; ate , iretakyu tanne enu avall parranju .
paretas avallodu : kattravinte aatmavine pariikshippan ningall tammill otttu entu ? ita , ninte bhattravine kujhyichaidtvarude kall vatilkyll undu ; avar ninneyum purrattu kondupokum enu parranju .
udane avall avante kalkyll viinnu prannane vidtu ; balaykyar akattu vanu avall marichau enu kandu purrattu kondupoyi bhattravinte arike kujhyichaidtu .
savarr sabhekyum itu kedtvakyru ellavakyrum mahbhayam undayi .
apposatlanmarude kayaall janattinte idayill paladayallangallum atbhutangallum nadanu ; avar ellavarum eekmanassode shalomonte mandpattill koodivarikpativayirunu .
mattullavarill aarum avarodu cheruvan tuninjilla ; janamo avare pukajhyttipponu .
melkyumell anavadhi purukshanmarum srtikallum kattravill vishsichau chenur vanu .
rogikalle purrattu kondu vanu , paretas kadanu pokuboll avante nijhyall ekkilum avarill vallavarudeyum mell viijhyendatinu viithikallill virippinmelum kidakymelum kidattum .
atu koodate yerooshaleminu chuttumullpadtnnangallill ninum puruksharam vanukoodi rogikalleyum ashuddhatmakyll badhichaavareyum kondu varikayum avar ellavarum sekhaym prapikyyum cheyaum .
pinne mahapurohitanum sadookayrude matakyarayavante pakshakyarokyeyum
asooynirranju ejhyunnettu apposatlanmare pidichau potutadavill aakyi ,
ratriyilo kattravinte dootan karagrahvatill turranu avare purrattu kondu vanu :
ningall daivalayattill chenu i jiivante vachanam ellam janattodu prsatavippin enu parranju .
avar kedtu pulacheerkyu daivalayattill chenu upadeshichau kondirunu ; mahapurohitanum koodeyullavarum vanu nayyadhipsamghatteyum yisrayell makyllude mooppnmareyum ellam villichau koodti , avare konduvaruvan tadavilekyu aallayachau .
chevakar chennappoll avare karagrahattill kannate madangi vanu : karagraham nallsookshttode poodtiyirikyu nnatum kavalkyar vatilkyll nilkyunnatum njangall kandu ;
turrannappojhyo akattu aareyum kandillenu arriyichau .
i vakyu kedtidtu daivalayattile padanayakanum mahpurohitanmarum itu entayittiirum enu avarekyu rrichau chanchlichau .
appoll oruttn vanu : ningall tadavill aakyiypurukshanmar daivalayattill ninukondu janatte upadeshikyunu enu bodhippichau .
padanayakan chevakarumayi chenu , janam kalelrriyum enu bhayappedukayall balalkyaram cheyaate avare koodti kyondu vanu .
angane avare konduvanu nayayadhipasamghattinmu mbake nirrutti ; mahapurohatan avarodu :
i namattill upadeshikyrutu enu njangall ningallodu amachaaryayi kalpichauvalela ; ningallo yerooshalemine ningllude upadesham kondu nirrechairikyunu ; amanukshaynte rtam njangallude mell varuttuvan ichchikyunu enu parranju .
atinu paretasum sheksham apposatlanmarum : manukshayre kyall daivatte anusarikyendatakunu .
yisrayelinu manasantaravum papmochanavum nalku van daivam avane prbhuvayum rakshitavayum tante valakkyaall uyattriyirikyunu .
i vasatutekyu njangallum daivam tanne anusarikyunnavkyru nalkiyparishuddhatmavum sakshikall aakunu enu uttram parranju .
itu kedtppoll avar kopaparavasharayi avare odukyi kyllavan bhavichau .
appoll savarrjanattinum bahumanamulldhammerapadeshtvaygamaliiyell ennoru pariishan nayayadhipasamghttill ejhyunnettu , avare kurre neram purrattakyuvan kalpichau .
pinne avan avarodu : yisrayell purukshanmare , i manukshayrude kayarrttill ningall entu cheyvan poku nu enu sookshichau kollvin .
i nallukallkyu mube tayudas ennavan ejhyunnettu tan mahan enu nadichau ; eekadesham nanoorru purukshanmar avanodu chenurkoodi ; ekkilum avan nashikyyum avane anusarichaavar ellavarum chinni onumillatakayum cheyatu .
avante sheksham galiilakyaranayyoodchattrlinte kalattu ejhyunnettu janatte tante paksham cheruvan vashiikarichau ; avanum nashichau , avane anusarichaavar okyeyum chitarrippoyi .
aakayall i manukshayre vidtu ojhyinju kollvin enu njan ningallodu parrayunu ; i aalochanayo prvratti yo manuksham enu varikill atu nashichau pokum ;
daivikam ekkilo ningallkyu atu nashippippan kajhyikayilla ; ningall daivattodu poradunu enu vararutalelenu parranju .
avar avane anusarichau : apposatlanmare varutti adippichau , ini yeshuvinte namattill samsarikyrutu enu kalpichau avare vidtyachau .
tirunamattinu vendi apamanam sahippan yogayrayi ennppedukayall avar santokshichau kondu nayayadhipsamghattinte mumbill ninu purrappedtu poyi .
pinne avar dinabrti daivalayattilum viidu torrum vidate upadeshikyyum yeshuvine krisatu enusuvishe kshikyyum cheyatu kondirunu .
akalattu shikshaynmar peruki varuboll tangallude vidhavamare dinabrtiyullshushrookshayill upekshayayi vicharichau enu yavanabhakshakyar ebrayabhakshakyarude nere pirrupirruttu .
pantiruvar shikshaynmarude koodttte villichau varutti : njangall daivavachanam upekshichau meshakallill shushrookshcheyaunnatu yogaymallal .
aakayall sahodaranmare , aatmavum njanavum nirranju nallsakshaymulleejhyu purukshanmare ningallill tanne tiranju kollvin ; avare i velekyu aakyam .
njangallo pratthrnayilum vachanashushrookshayilum uttirikyum enu parranju .
i vakyu koodtttinu okyeyum boddhymayi ; vishasvum parishuddhatmavum nirranj purukshanaysetphano s , philippos , repakhoros , nikyanor , timo n , pammernas , yehoodmatanusariyayanteyakaykyran nikyolavos ennivare tiranjeduttu ,
apposatlanmarude mumbake nirrutti ; avar pratthrichau avarude mell kaivechau .
daivavachanam paranu , yerooshalemill shikshaynmarude ennm eettvum peruki , purohitanmarilum valiyoru koodtm vishasattinu adhiinarayittiinur .
anantaram setphanos krapayum shtiyum nirranjvanayi janattill valiyatbhutangallum adayallangallum cheyatu .
libattriinar enu perullpallikyarilum kurrenakyari lum aleksantriyakyarilum kilikyy aasay enndeshkyarilum chilar ejhyunnettu setphanosinodu takyrichau .
ennall avan samsarichanattodum aatmavodum etittru nilpan avakyru kajhyinjillal .
appoll avar chilpurukshanmare vashattakyi : ivan moshekyum daivattinum virodhamayi dookshannam parrayunnatu njangall kedtu enu parrayichau ,
janatteyum mooppnmareyum shasrtimareyum illakyi , avnte nere chenu avane pidichau nayayadhipasamghattill kondupoyi
kallasakshikalle nirrutti : i manukshayn vishuddhsthlatti num nayayaprmannattinum virodhamayi idavidate samsarichau varunu ;
anasarrayanayyeshu i sthlam nashippichau moshe namukyu eelpichamayarradakalle mattikyllayum enu avan parrayunnatu njangall kedtu enu parrayichau .
irunnavar ellavarum avane uttunokyi avante mukham oru daivdootante mukham pole kandu .
itu ullatu tanneyo enu mahapurohitan chodichatinu avan parranjtu :
sahodaranmarum pitakynmarumaypurukshanmare , kellppin , nammude pitavayabraham haranill vanu pakyrum mube mesoppottamayyill irikyubo ll , tanne tejomayanaydaivam avanu prtaykshanayi :
avante appn marichasheksham daivam avane avideni nu ningall ippoll pakyrunni deshattill konduvnu papprichau .
avanu atill oru kaladi nilam polum avakasham koduttilla ; avanu santatiyillatirikye avanum avante sheksham avante santatikyum atine kaivashamayi nalkumenu avanodu vagdattm cheyatu .
avante santati anaydeshattu chenu pakyrum ; adeshakyar avare adimayakyi nanoorru samvram piiddippikyum enu daivam kalpichau .
avar sevikyunnjatiye njan nayayam vidhikyum ; atinte sheksham avar purrappedtuvanu i sthlattu enne sevikyum enu daivam arullicheeyatu .
pinne avanu pariedanayennniyamam koduttu ; angane avan yisahakyine janippichau , edtam nall pariedancheyatu . yisahak yakyobineyum yakyob pantrndu gotrpitakynmareyum janippichau .
gotrpitakynmar yosephinodu asooyappedtu avane misryiimilekyu vittukallanju .
ennall daivam avanodukoode irunu sakalasakkdangllill ninum avane viduvichau misryiim rajavaypharrvonte mumbake avanu krapayum njanavum koduttu : avan avane misryiiminum tante savarrgrahattinnum adhipatiyakyivechau .
misryiim deshattilum kananilum ellam kshamavum mahakashtavum vannarre nammude pitakynmakyru aaharam kidtateyayi .
misryiimill dhanaym undu enu kedtidtu yakyob nammude pitakynmare onnam pravashaym ayachau .
randam pravashaym yoseph tante sahodaranmarodu tannettan arriyichaum yosephinte vamsham pharravonu vellivayvanu .
yoseph aallayachau tante pitavayyakyobineyum kudumbatte okyeyum varutti ; avar aake ejhyupatt nchu perayirunu .
yakyob misryiimilekyu poyi ; avanum nammude pitakynmarum marichau .
avare shekhemill kondu vanu shekhemill emmorinte makyllodu abrham vilakoduttu vangiykallarrayill adakym cheyatu .
daivam abrahaminodu arullicheeyat vagdatt kalam aduttppoll janam misryiimill vaddhrichau peruki .
oduvill yosephine arriyatt verreru rajavu misryiimill vannu .
avan nammude vamshattodu upayam pryogichau nammude pitakynmare piiddippichau , avarude shishukyll jiivanode irikyrutu enu vechau avare purrattiduvichau .
akalattu moshe janichau , divaysundranayirunu ; avane moonu masam appnte viidtill potti .
pinne avane purrattidtppoll pharravonte makall avane eduttu tante makanayi vallattri .
moshe misryiimayrude sakalnjanavum abhaysichau vakyilum prvrattiyilum samatthrnayi ttiinur .
avanu nalpatuvayassu tikayarrayappoll yisrayell makyllaytante sahodaranmare chenu kannennam enu manassill tonni .
avarill oruttn anayayam eelkyunnatu kandidtu avanu tunnninu , misryiimayne adichau konu , piidditanu vendi prtikriycheyatu .
daivam tanmukhantaram avakyru rakshnalkum enu sahodaranmar grhikyum enu avan niroopichau ; ekkilum avar grhichaillal .
pittennall avar kalahichau kondirikyuboll avan avarude adukyll vanu : purukshanmare , ningallsahodarnmaralela ; tammill anayayam cheyaunnatu entu enu parrnju avare samadhanappeduttuvan nokyi .
ennall koodtukaranodu anayayam cheyaunnavan avane untikyllanju : ninne njangallkyu adhikariyum nayayakattravum aakyiyatu aar ?
innale misryiimayne konnatu pole enneyum kolluvan bhavikyunnuvo enu parranju .
i vakyu kedtidtu moshe oadippoyi midayan deshattu chenu pattru , avide randu putrnmare janippichau .
nalpatandu kajhyinjppoll siinaylayude marubhoomiyill oru daivadootan mull padapprile ijalayill avanu prtaykshanayi .
njan ninte pitakynmarude daivamayi abrahaminte yum yisahakyinteyum yakyobinteyum daivam aaku nu enu kattravinte shabdam kedtu . moshe virrechaidtu nokyuvan tuninjillal .
kattravu avanodu : nii nilkyunnsthlam vishuddh bhoomiyakayall kalill ninu cherippu urikyllaka .
misryiimill ente janattinte piiddnjan kandu , avarude njarakyvum kedtu , avare viduvippan irrangivannirikyunu ; ippoll varika ; njan ninne misryiimilekyu ayakyum enu parranju .
ninne adhikariyumnayayakattravum aakyiyatar enningane avar tallipprranj i mosheye daivam mullpadapprill prtaykshanaydootan mukhantaram adhikariyum viindeduppukaranum aakyi ayachau .
avan misryiimilum chekkdalilum nalpatu samvram marubhoomiyilum atishayangallum adayallangallum cheyatu avare nadattikyondu vanu .
daivam ningallude sahodaranmarill ninu enneppole oru prvachakane ningallkyu ejhyunnelpichautarum enu yisrayell makyllodu parranj moshe avan tanne .
siinaylayill tannodu samsarichadootanodum nammude pitakynmarodum koode marubhoomiyile sabhayill irunnavanum namukyu taruvan jiivanullarullappadu labhichaavanum avan tanne .
nammude pitakynmar avanu kiijhyppeduvan manassillate avane tallikyllanju hradayam kondu misryiimilekyu pintirinju , aharonodu :
njangallkyu mumbayi nadappan daivangalle undakyittrika ; njangalle misryiimill ninu nadatti kyondu vannamoshekyu entu sambhavichau enu njangall arriyunnillalelenu parranju .
anneram avar oru kallakyudtiye undakyi , abimbattinu bali kajhyichau tangallude kaippnniyill ullasichau kondirunu .
daivavum pintirinju , aakashattile sainaytte aaradhippan avare kaividtu . " yisrayell grahame , ningall marubhoomiyill enikyu nalpatu samvram hananayagangallum bhojanayagangallum apprichauvo ?
ningall namaskyrippan undakyiysroopangallaymolokyinte koodaravum rephan devante nakshatrvum ningall eduttu nadanuvalela ; ennall njan ningalle babilonnappurram prvasippikyum " enu pavachakanmrude pusatkattill ejhyutiyirikyunuvalela .
nii kandamatirikyottvannm atine tiikyernnam enu moshayodu arullicheeyatvan kalpichaatu pole nammude pitakynmakyru marubhoomiyill sakshaykoodaram undayirunu .
nammude pitakynmar atu eettu vangi daivam nammude pitakynmarude mumbill ninu niikyikyllanj jatikallude avakashattilekyu yoshuvayumayi kondu vanu daviidinte kalam vare vechairunu .
avan daivattinte mumbake krapalabhichau , yakyobinte daivattinu oru vasasthlam undakyuvan anuvadam apekshichau .
shalomon avanu oru aalayam pannitu .
atayunnatan kaippnniyayatill vasikyunnilltanum .
" sggrm enikyu simhasanavum bhoomi ente padapiitthavum aakunu ; ningall enikyu panniyunnaalayam eetu vidham ?
ente vishrmasthlavum eetu ? itokyeyum ente kaiyllayo ungakyiyatu ennu kattravu arullicheeyaunu " enu prvachakan parrayunuvalela .
shatthaykyarum hradayattinum chevikyum pariedanillatt varumayullore , ningallude pitakynmareppole tanne ningallum ellayepajhyum parishuddhatmavinodu marruttu nilkyunu .
prvachakanmarill eevane ningallude pitakynmar uvadrvikyatirunnidtullu ? niitimanayavante varavine kyurrichau mun arriyichaavare avar konu kallanju .
avanu ningall ippoll redahikallum kulapatakarum aayittiinur ; ningall daivadootanmarude niyogangallayi nayayaprmannam prapichau ekkilum atu prmannichaidtillal .
itu kedtppoll avar kopaparavasharayi avante nere pallu kadichau .
avano parishuddhatmavu nirranjvanayi sggrttilekyu uttunokyi , daivamahatvum daivattinte valattubhagattu yeshu nilkyunnatum kandu :
ita , sggrm turrannirikyunnatum manukshayputrn daivatti nte valattubhagattu nilkyunnatum njan kannunu enu parranju .
avar urrakye nalavillichau , chevi pottikyondu onnichau avante nere panju chenu ,
avane nagarattill ninu talli purrattakyi kalelrrinju . sakshikall tangallude vasrtm shell enu perulloru balaykyarante kalkyll vechau .
kattravayyeshuve , ente aatmavine kaikyolle nname enu setphanos villichaapekshikyyill avar avane kalelrrinju .
avano mudtukutti : kattrave , avakyru i papam nirruttrute enu uchaattill nilavillichau . itu parranjidtu avan nidr prapichau .
avane kulacheyattu shelinu sammtamayirunu . anu yerooshalemile sabhekyu oru valiyupadrvam neridtu : pposatlanmar ojhyike ellavarum yehooday shamayarr deshangalli ll chitarrippoyi .
bhtiyullpurukshanmar setphanosine adakym cheyatu . avanekyurrichau valiyoru prlapam kajhyichau .
ennall shell viidutorrum chenu purukshanmareyum srtiikalleyum pidichaijhyachau tadavill eelpichau kondu sabhaye mudichau ponu .
chitarrippoyavar vachanam suvishekshichaum kondu avidavi de sanchrichau .
philippos shamayarrrrr padtnnattill chenu avarodu krisatvine prsamgichau .
philippos cheyat adayallangalle puruksharangall kellkyyum kankayum cheykayall avan parrayunnatu eekmanassode shrddhichau kondirunu .
ashuddhatmakyll badhichapalarill ninum avurrakye nilavillichau kondu purrappedtu ; anekam pakshavatakyarum mudantarum sekhaym prapichau .
angane apadtnnattill vallare santoksham undayi .
ennall shimon enu perulloru purukshan apadtnnattill aabhicharam cheyatu , tan mahan enu parranju shamayarr jatiye bhrmippichau ponu .
ivan mahati enndaivashti aakunu enum parranju aabalavraddhm ellavarum avane shrddhichau vanu .
ivan aabhicharam kondu eerriykalam avare bhrmippikyyall aretavar avane shrddhichaatu .
ennall daivarajaytteyum yeshukrisatuvinte namatteyum kurrichaullsuvisheksham arriyikyunnphilipposine avar vishsichaappoll purukshanmarum srtiikallum sanam eettu .
shimon tanum vishsichau sanam eettu philipposino du chenur ninu , valiyviiyarr prvrattikallum adayallangallum nadakyunnatu kandu bhrmichau .
anantaram yerooshalemilullapposatlanmar , shamayarrr daivavachanam kaikyondu enu kedtu paretasineyum yohannaneyum avarude adukyll ayachau .
avar chenu , avakyru parishuddhatmavu labhikyendatinu avakyrayi pratthrichau .
anuvare avarill aarudemelum aatmavu vannirunnilla ; avar kattravayyeshuvinte namattill sanam eettirunnateyullu
avar avarude mell kai vechaappoll avakyru parishuddhatmavu labhichau .
apposatlanmar kai vechaatinall parishuddhatmavu labhichaatu shimon kandarre avakyru drvaym konduvanu :
njan oruttnte mell kai vechaall avanu parishuddhtmavu labhippan takyvannm i adhikaram enikyum tare nnam enu parranju .
paretas avanodu : daivattinte danam pannattinu vangikyollam enu nii niroopikykondu ninte pannam ninnodukoode nashichau pokadte .
ninte hradayam daivasannidhiyill nerullatallaykakondu i kayarrttill ninakyu pakkum ohariyumillal .
nii i vakshallatm vidtu manasantarappedtu kattavinodu pratthriky ; pakshe ninte hradayattile niroopannam kshami chau kidtumayirikyum .
nii kaippullpakayilum aniitiyude bandnattilum akappedtirikyunu enu njan kannunu enu parranju .
atinu shimon : ningall parranjtu onum enikyu bhavikyatirippan kattravinodu enikyuvendi pratthrippin enu uttram parranju .
avar kattravinte vachanam sakshiikarichau prsamgichasheksham shamayarrkyarude anekgramangallill suvisheksham arriyichau kondu yerooshalemilekyu madangippoyi .
anantaram kattravinte dootan phalipposinodu : nii ejhyunnettu tekyodtu yerooshalemill ninu gasekyullnijjarnamayvajhyiyilekyu pokenu parranju .
avan purrappedtu chennappoll kandky enneeteyapay riyude oru kshandnum mahanum avallude sakalbhandarattinum mell vicharakanumayoru eeteyapayne kandu . avan yerooshalemill namaskyrippan vannidtu
madangippokayill terill irunu yeshayaprvachakante pusatkam vayikyyayirunu .
aatmavu philipposinodu : nii aduttu chenuteri nodu chenur nadaky enu parranju .
philippos oadicheelluboll yeshayaprvachakante pusatkam vayikyunnatu kedtu : nii vayikyunnatu grhikyunu vo enu chodichaatinu :
oruttn porull tirichautaranjall engane grhikyum enu avan parranju , philippos kayarri tannodukoode irikyennam enu apekshichau .

( atinu philippos : nii poonnr hradayattode vishsi kyunu ekkill aakam enu parranju . yeshukrisatu daivputrn enu njan vishsikyunu enu avan uttram parranju . )
angane avan ter nittruvan kalpichau ; philipposum kshandnum iruvarum vellattill irrangi , avan avane sanam kajhyippichau .
avar vellattill ninu kayarriyappoll kattravinte aatmavu philipposine eduttu kondupoyi ; kshandn avane pinne kandilla ; avan santokshichaum kondu tante vajhyikyu poyi .
philipposine pinne asetadill kandu ; avan sanchrichau ellapadtnnangallilum suvisheksham arriyichau kondu kaisayarryill etti .

neram velluttppoll paretas evideppoyi ennu padayallikallkyu alpamallatt paribhrmam undayi .
herodavu avane anevkshichaidtu kannaykayall kavalkyare visatrichau avare kolluvan kalpichau ; pinne avan yehooday vidtu kaisayarryilekyu poyi avide pattru .
avan soyarrrudeyum sidonayrudeyum nere kruddhichai rikyuboll rajavinte deshattu ninnu tangallude deshatti nnu aaharam kidtivarikayall avar eekamanassode avnte adukyll chennu , rajavinte palliyarrakyaranaylbasetasine vashattakyi sandikyayi apekshichau .
nischayichadivasattill herodavu rajavasrtm dharichau bhadrasanattill irunnu avarodu prsamgam kajhyichau .
itu manukshaynte shabdamalloru devante shabdam aretennu janam aattru .
avan daivattinnu mahatm kodukyaykayall kattrravinte dootan udane avane adichau , avan kramikyu irayayi prannane vidtu .
ennall daivavachanam melkyumell parannu kondirunnu .
bannarbasum shelum shushrookshnivattrichasheksham makyeras ennu marruperullyohannaneyum koodti kyondu yerooshalem vidtu madangipponnu .
anteyakyyyile sabhayill bannarbas , niigar ennu perullshimon , kurrenakyaranaylookeyas , idaprbhuvayherodavodukoode vallannar manayen , shell ennii prvachakanmarum upadeshtakynmarum undayirunnu .
avar kattravine aaradhichaum upavasichaum kondirikyu boll : njan bannarbasineyum shelineyum villichai rikyunnvelekyayidtu avare enikyu vertirippin ennu parishuddhatmavu parranju .
angane avar upavasichau pratthrichau avarude mell kaivechau avare parranjyachau .
parishuddhatmavu avare parranjyachaidtu avar selookayyi lekyu chennu ; avide ninnu kappll kayarri kurepas diipilekyu poyi ,
salamiisill chennu yehoodanmarude palliyill daivavachanam arriyichau . yohannan avakyru bhrataynayidtu undayirunnu .
avar diipillkoodi paphos vare chennappoll baryeshu ennu perullyehoodanayi kallaprvachaknayoru vidane kandu .
avan buddhimanayseggerys pelos enndeshadhipatiyodu koode aayirunnu ; avan bannarbasi neyum shelineyum varutti daivavachanam kellppan aagrhichau .
ennall eliimas ennvidan - itakunnu avante perinte atthrm - avarodu etittru ninnu deshadhipatiyude vishasam taduttukallavan shrmichau .
appoll pelos ennum perullshell parishuddhatm poonnrnayi avane uttunokyi :
he sakalkapadavum sakaldhoottrum nirranjvane , pishachinte makane , savarr niitiyudeyum shatruve , kattravinte nevarrjhyikalle marrichaukallayunnatu nii matiyakyukayillayo ?
ippoll kattravinte kai ninte mell viijhyum ; nii oru samayattekyu sooyarrne kannate kurudanayirikyum ennu parranju . udane oru timiravum irudtum avante mell viinnu ; kaipidichau nadattunnavare tiranju kondu avan tappi nadannu .
i undayatu deshadhipati kandidtu kattravinte upadeshattill visyichau vishsichau .
pelosum koodeyullavarum paphosill ninnu kappll niikyi , pamphulayadeshattile peggerkyu chennu . avide vechau yohannan avare vidtu pirinju yerooshalemi lekyu madangippoyi .
avaro peggryill ninnu purrappedtu pisidayadeshattile anteyakyyyill etti shabaat nallill palliyill chennu irunnu .
nayayaprmannavum prvachakangallum vayichau tiinnarppoll palli prmannikall avarude adukyll aallayachau : sahodaranmare , ningallkyu janattodu prbodhanam vallatum undakkill parravin ennu parrayichau .
pelos ejhyunnettu aamgaym kadti parranjtu : yisrayell purukshanmarum daivabhtanmarum aayullore , kellppin .
yisrayell janattinte daivam nammude pitakynmare tiranjeduttu , misryiim deshattile prvasakalattu janatte vaddhrippichau , bhujaviiyarrm kondu avide ninnu purrappeduvichau ,
marubhoomiyill nalpatu samvrakalattollam avarude sbhavam sahichau ,
kanan deshattile eejhyu jatikalle odukyi , avarude desham avakyru avakashamayi vibhagichau koduttu . angane eekadesham nanoottmbatu samvram kajhyinju .
atinte sheksham avan avakyru shamoovell prvachakan vare nayadhipatimare koduttu .
anantaram avar oru rajavine chodichau ; daivam avakyru benayamiin gotrkyaranaykiishinte makan sheline nalpatandekyu koduttu .
avane niikyiidtu daviidine avakyru rajavayi vajhyichau : njan yishshayiyude makanaydaviidine enikyu bodhichapurukshanayi kandu ; avan ente hitam ellam cheyaum ennu avanekyurrichau sakshaym parranju .
avante santatiyill ninnu daivam vagdattm cheyattu pole yisrayelinnu yeshu ennrakshitavine koduttu .
avante varavinnu mube yohannan yisrayell janattinnu okyeyum manasantarattinte sanam prsamgichau .
yohannan jiivakalam tikavarrayappoll : ningall enne aar ennu niroopikyunnu ? njan mashiihayalla ; avan ente pinnale varunnu ; avante kalile cherippu ajhyippan njan yogaynallennu parranju .
sahodaranmare , abraham vamshattile makyllum avarodu chennar daivabhtanmarumayullore , namukyakunnu i rakshavachanam ayachairikyunnatu .
yerooshalem nivasikallum avarude prmannikallum avaneyo shabaattutorrum vayichau varunnprvachakanmarude vachanangalleyo tirichaarriyate avane shikshekyu vidhikyyall avekyu nivrattivarutti .
marannattinnu oru hetuvum kannanjidtum avane kolelnnam ennu avar piilattosinodu apekshichau .
avanekyurrichau ejhyutiyirikyunnatu okyeyum tikechasheksham avar avane marattill ninnu irrakyi oru kallarrayill vechau .
daivamo avane marichaavarill ninnu uyitterjhyunnelpichau ;
avan tannodukoode galiilayill ninnu yerooshalemilekyu vannavakyru eerriydivasam prtaykshanayi ; avar ippoll janattinte mumbake avante sakshikall aakunnu .
daivam pitakynmarodu cheyat vagdattm yeshuvine uyatterjhyunnelpichaatinnall makyllkyu nivattrichairikyunnu ennu njangall ningallodu suvishekshikyunnu .
nii ente putrn ; innu njan tinne janippichau ennu randam sakkiittrnattill ejhyutiyirikyunnuvalela .
ini drvatttilekyu tiriyatavannm avan avane marichaavarill ninnu ejhyunnelpichaatinekyurrichau avan : daviidinte sthiramayullvishuddh krapakalle njan ningallkyu nalkum ennu parranjirikyunnu .
mattoru sakkiittrnattilum : ninte parishuddhne drvatm kanman nii vidtukodukyyillennu parrayunnu .
daviid tante talamurrayill daivattinte aalochanekyu shushrookshcheyat sheksham nidr prapichau tante pitakynmarodu chennaru drvatm kandu .
daivam uyitterjhyunnelpichaavano drvatm kandilla .
aakayall sahodaranmare , ivan moolam ningallodu papamochanam arriyikyunnu ennum
mosheyude nayayaprmannattall ningallkyu niitiikarannam varuvan kajhyiyatt sakalattill ninnum vishsikyunneevanum ivanall niitiikarikyppedunnu ennum ningall arrinju kollvin .
aakayall , " he nindkyare , nokyuvin ; ayarrppedtu nashichau pokuvin . ningallude kalattu njan oru prvratti cheyaunnu ; ningallodu vivarichaall ningall vishsikyatt prvratti tanne "
ennu prvachakapusatkangallill arullicheeyatirikyunnatu ningallkyu bhavikyatirippan sookshichau kollvin .
avar palli vidtu pokuboll pitte shabaattill i vachanam tangallodu parrayennam ennu avar apekshichau .
palli pirinjsheksham yehoodanmarilum bhtiyullyehoodmatanusarikallilum palar pelosineyum bannarbasineyum anugamichau : avar avarodu samsarichau daivakrapayill nilanilkyendatinnu avare utsahippichau .
pitte shabaattill eekadesham padtnnam mujhyuvanum daivvachanam kellppan vannu koodi .
yehoodanmaro puruksharatte kandu asooynirranjvarayi dukshichau kondu pelos samsarikyunnatinnu etir parranju .
appoll pelosum bannarbasum dhaiyarrm poondu : daivavachanam aadaym ningalloadu parrayunnatu aavashaymayirunnu ; ennall ningall atine talli ningalle ttnne nitayjiivannu ayogayr ennu vidhichau kallayunnatinall ita , njangall jatikallilekyu tiriyunnu .
" nii bhoomiyude attttollavum rakshaakendatinnu njan ninne jatikallude vellichaamakyi vechairikyunnu . " ennu kattravu njangallodu kalpichaidtundu ennu parranju .
jatikall itu kedtu santokshichau daivavachanatte mahatppedutti , nitayjiivannayi niyamikyppedtvar ellavarum vishsichau .
kattravinte vachanam anadtill engum vayapichau .
yehoodanmaro bhtiyullmanaysrtiikalleyum padtnnattile prdhanikalleyum illakyi pelosinteyum bannarbasinteyum nere uvadrvamundakyi avare tangallude atirukallill ninnu purrattakyikyllanju .
ennall avar tangallude kalile podi avarude nere tadtikyllanju ikyonayyilekyu poyi .
shikshaynmar santokshavum parishuddhatmavum nirranjvarayi ttiinnaru .
ikyonayyill avar orumichau yehoodanmarude palliyill chennu yehoodanmarilum yavananmarilum valiyoru puruksharam vishsippan takyvannm samsarichau .
vishsikyatt yehoodanmaro jatikallude manassu sahodaranmarude nere illakyi vakshallakyi .
ennall avar vallarekyalam avade pattru , kattravill aashryichau pragatdyttode prsamgichau kondirunnu ; avan tante krapayude vachanattinnu sakshininnu , avarude kayaall adayallangallum atdutangallum undakuvan varam nalki .
ennall padtnnattile janasamooham bhinnichau chilar yehoodanmarude pakshattilum chilar apposatlanmarude pakshattilum aayi .
avare avamanipparum kalelrrivanum jatikallum yehoodanmarum avidatte prmannikallodukoodi oru aakrmam bhavichaappoll
avar atu grhichau lusrt , debarr ennlukyvonay padtnnangallilekyum chuttumulldeshattilekyum oadippoyi
avide suvisheksham arriyichau ponnu .
lusrtyill ammyude gabharm mutall mudantanayi orikylum nadannidtillateyum kalinnu shtiyillateyum ulloru purukshan irunnirunnu .
avan pelos samsarikyunnatu kedtu ; avan avane uttu nokyi , sekhaym prapippan avannu vishasamundu ennu kandidtu :
nii ejhyunnettu kaloonni nivinnaru nilky ennu urrakye parranju ; avan kuticheejhyunnettu nadannu .
pelos cheyattu puruksharam kandidtu : devanmar manukshay roopattill nammude adukyll irrangi vannirikyunnu ennu lukyvonay bhakshayill nilavillichau parranju .
bannarbasinnu indrn ennum pelos mukhay prsamgiyakayall avannu budhan ennum per villichau .
padtnnattinte mumbilullindrkshetrttile purohitan kallakalleyum poomalakalleyum gopurattikkll kondu vannu puruksharattodukoode yagam kajhyippan bhavichau .
itu apposatlanmaraybannarbasum pelosum kedtidtu vasrtm kiirrikyondu puruksharattinte idayilekyu oadicheennu nilavillichau parranjtu :
purukshanmare , ningall i cheyaunnatu entu ? njangall ningallodu samas bhavamullmanukshayr aret ningall i vaytthr kayarrngalle vidtu , aakashavum bhoomiyum samudrvum avayilullsakalavum undakyiyjiivanulldaivatti kklekyu tiriyennam ennullsuvisheksham njangall ningallodu arriyikyunnu .
kajhyinj kalangallill avan sakaljatikalleyum sntavajhyikallill nadappan sammtichau .
ekkilum avan nanmcheykayum aakashattu ninnu majhyayum phalapushtiyullkalangallum ningallkyu tarikayum aaharavum santokshavum nalki ningalle trapatrakyukayum cheyatu ponnatinall tannekyurrichau sakshaym taratirunnidtillal .
avan ingane parranju tangallkyu yagam kajhyikyatavannm puruksharatte pryasattode taduttu .
ennall anteyakyyyill ninnum ikyonayyill ninnum yehoodanmar vannu koodi puruksharatte vashattakyi pelosine kalelrrinju ; avan marichau ennu vicharichaidtu avane padtnnattinnu purrattekyu ijhyechau kallanju .
ennall shikshaynmar avane chuttinilkyyill avan ejhyunnettu padtnnattill chennu ; pittennall bannarbasi nodu koode deberrkyu poyi .
apadtnnattilum suvisheksham arriyichau palareyum shikshayrakyiysheksham avar lusrt , ikyonay , anteyakay ennpadtnnangallilekyu madangicheennu ,
vishasattill nilanillkyennam ennum nam anekam kashtangallillkoodi daivarajayttill kadakyendatakunnu ennum prbodhippichau shikshaynmarude manassu urrappichau ponnu .
avar sabhatorrum avakyru mooppnmare niyamikyyum upavasichaum pratthrichaum kondu tangall vishsichakattravikkll avare bharamelpikyyum cheyatu .
avar pisidayyill koodi kadannu pamphulayyill etti ,
peggryill vachanam prsamgichasheksham attleykyu poyi
avide ninnu kappll kayarri anteyakyyyilekyu poyi ; tangall nivattrichavelakyayi daivakrapayill avare bharamelpichaayachaatu avide ninnu aayirunnuvalela .
avide ettiyasheksham sabhaye orumichau koodti , daivam tangallodukoode irunnu cheyattokyeyum jatikallkyu vishasattinte vatill turrannu kodutttum arriyichau .
pinne avan shikshaynmarodukoode kurrekyalam avide pattru .
yehoodayyill ninnu chilar vannu : ningall moshe kalpichaaacharam anusarichau pariedaneelkyanjall rakshprapippan kajhyikayillennu sahodaranmare upadeshichau .
pelosinnum bannarbasinnum avarodu alpamallatt vadavum takyrvum undayidtu pelosum bannarbasum avarill mattu chilarum i takyrsamgatiyepptti yerooshalemill apposatlanmarudeyum mooppnmarudeyum adukyll pokennam ennu nischayichau .
sabhavare yatr ayachaidtu avar phoyniikyyyilum shamayarryilum koodi kadannu jatikallude manasantaravivaram arriyichau sahodaranmakyru mahasantoksham varutti .
avar yerooshalemill ettiyarre sabhayum apposatlanmarum mooppnmarum avare kaikyendu ; daivam tangallodukoode irunnu cheyattokyeyum avar arriyichau .
ennall pariishapakshattill ninnu vishsichaavar chilar ejhyunnettu avare pariedankajhyippikyyum mosheyude nayayaprmannam aacharippan kalpikyyum vennam ennu parranju .
i samgatiyekyurrichau vicharippan apposatlanmarum mooppnmarum vannukoodi ,
vallare takyrm undayasheksham paretas ejhyunnettu avarodu parranjtu : sahodaranmare , kurre nall mube daivam ningallill vechau njan mukhantaram jatikall suvishekshavachanam kedtu vishsikyennam ennu nischayichaatu ningall arriyunnuvalela .
hradayangalle arriyunndaivam namukyu tannatupole avakyrum parishuddhatmvine koduttu kondu sakshi ninnu
vishasattall avarude hradayangalle shuddhiikarichaatinall namukyum avakyrum tammill oru vaytayasavum vechaidtillal .
aakayall nammude pitakynmakyrum namukyum chumappan kajhyinjidtillatt nukam shikshaynmarude kajhyuttill veppan ningall ippoll daivatte pariikshikyunnatu entu ?
kattravayyeshuvinte krapayall rakshprapikyum ennu nam vishsikyunnatu pole avarum vishsikyunnu .
janasamooham ellam mindate bannarbasum pelosum daivam tangalle kyondu jatikallude idayill cheyaichadayallangallum atdutangallum ellam vivarikyunnatu kedtu kondirunnu .
avar parranju nirruttiyasheksham yakyob uttram parranjtu : sahodaranmare , ente vakyu kedtukollvin ;
daivam tante namattinnayi jatikallill ninnu oru janatte eduttu kollvan aadaymayidtu kadakshichaatu shimon vivarichauvalela .
itinodu prvachakanmarude vakayngallum okyunnu .
" anantaram njan daviidinte viinnupoykoodaratte viindum panniyum ; atinte shoonayshishtangalle viindum pannitu atine nivittrum ;
manukshayrill sekshichaavarum ente namam villichairikyunnsakalajatikallum kattravine anevkshikyum
ennu itu poovarrkalam mutall arriyikyunnkattravu arullicheeyaunnu " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnuvalela .
aakayall jatikallill ninnu daivattikklekyu tiriyunnavare nam asahayppeduttate
avar vigrhamalinayngall , parasamgam , shsam mudtichaatttu , rtam ennivvrichairippan nam avakyru ejhyutennam ennu njan abhiprayappedunnu .
mosheyude nayayaprmannam shabaattutorrum pallikallill vayichau varunnatinall poovarrkalam mutall padtnnam torrum atu prsamgikyunnavar undalela .
appoll tangallill chilpurukshanmare tiranjeduttu pelosinodum bannarbasinodum koode anteyakyyyilekyu ayakyennam ennu apposatlanmarum ooeppnmarum savarrsabhayum ninnryichau , sahodaranmarill prmannappedt purukshanmaraybarshabas ennyoodayeyum shiilasineyum niyogichau .
avarude kaivasham ejhyuti ayachaatentennall : apposatlanmarum mooppnmaraysahodaranmarum anteyakyyyilum surriyayilum kilikyyyilum jatikallill ninnu chennar sahodaranmakyru vandnam .
njangall kalpankodukyate chilar njangallude idayill ninnu purrappedtu ningalle vakyukallall bhrmippichau ningallude hradayangalle kalakyikyllanju ennukellky kondu
njangall chilpurukshanmare tiranjeduttu nammude kattravayyeshukrisatuvinte namattinnu vendi prannatayagam cheyatvaraya
nammude priybannarbasodum pelosodum koode ningallude adukyll ayakyennam ennu njangall orumanppedtu nischayichau .
aakayall njangall yoodayeyum shiilasineyum ayachairikyunnu ; avar vamojhyiyayum itutanne arriyikyum .
vigrhappritam , rtam , shasam mudtichaatttu , parasamgam ennivvrikyunnatu aavashaym ennallate adhikamaybharam onnum ningallude mell chumattrutu ennu parishuddhatmavinnum njangallkyum tonniyirikyunnu .
ivvrichau sookshichau kondall nannu ; shubhamayirippin .
angane avar vidavangi anteyakyyyill chennu janasamoohatte koodti varutti lekhanam koduttu .
avar i aashasavachanam vayichau santokshichau .
yoodayum shiilasum prvachakanmar aakakondu palvachanangallalum sahodaranmare prbodhippichau urrappichau .
kurrenall tamasichasheksham sahodaranmar avare ayachaavarude adukylekyu samadhanattode parranjyachau .
ennall pelosum bannarbasum anteyakyyyill pattru mattu palarodum koodi kattravinte vachanam upadeshichaum suvishekshichaum kondirunnu .
kurre nall kajhyinjidtu pelos bannarbasinodu : nam kattravinte vachanam arriyichapadtnnam torrum pinneyum chennu sahodaranmar enganeyirikyunnu ennu nokyukennu parranju .
makyeras ennyohannaneyum koodtikyondu pokuvan bannarbas ichchichau .
peloso pamphulayyill ninnu tangalle vidtu prvrattikyu varate poyavane koodtikyondu pokunnatu yogaymallennu niroopichau .
angane avar tammill ugrvadamundayidtu ver pirinju , bannarbas makyerasine koodti kappll kayarri kurepas diipilekyu poyi .
peloso shiilasine tiranjeduttu sahodaranmarall kattravinte krapayill bharamelpiky ppedtidtu
yatr purrappedtu surriykilikaydeshangallill koodi sanchrichau sabhakalle urrappichau ponnu .

avan deberryilum lusrtyilum chennu . avide vishasamulloru yehoodasrtiiyude makanayi timotheyos ennu perulloru shikshayn undayirunnu . avante appn yavananayirunnu .
avan lusrtyilum ikyonayyilumullsahodaranmarall nallsakshaym kondavan aayirunnu .
avan tannodukoode porennam ennu pelos ichchichau ; avante appn yavayan ennu avidangallilullyehoodanmar ellavarum arrinjirunnatinall avare vicharichau avane pariedankajhyippichau .
avar padtnnam torrum chennu yerooshalemile apposatlnmarum mooppnmarum vidhichaninnryangall prmannikyendatinnu avakyru eelpichau koduttu .
angane sabhakall vishasattill urrekyyum ennttill divasenperukukayum cheyatu .
avar aasayyill vachanam prsamgikyrutennu parishuddhatmavu vilakyukayall phrugayyilum galatay deshattilum koodi sanchrichau ,
musayyill etti : bithuneykyu pokuvan shrmichau ; yeshuvinte aatmavo avare sammtichailla .
avar musay kadannu retavasill etti .
avide vechau pelos ratriyill makyedonay kyaranayoru purukshan arike ninnu : nii makyedoneykyu kadannu vannu njangalle sahayiky ennu tannodu apekshikyunnatayi oru dasharnam kandu .
i dasharnam kandidtu avarodu suvisheksham arriyippan daivam njangalle villichairikyunnu ennu nischayichau , njangall udane makyedoneykyu purrappeduvan shrmichau .
angane njangall retavasill ninnu kappll niikyi nere samotrakyeyilekyum pittennall navapolikyum avide ninnu phalippiyilekyum chennu .
itu makyedonayyude abhagatte oru prdhanapadtnnavum rromakyar kudiyerrippattrtum aakunnu . apadtnnattill njangall chiladivasam pattru .
shabaattu nallill njangall gopurattinnu purrattekyu poyi avide pratthrnasthlam undayirikyum ennu njangall vicharichau pujhyavakyttu irunnu ; avide koodi vannsrtiikallodu samsarichau .
tuyattairpadtnnakyarattiyum rtambaram vilkyunnvallumayi ludiyennu perulldaivabhtyayoru srtii kedtu kondirunnu . pelos samsarichaatu shrddhikyendatinnu kattravu avallude hradayam tarrannu .
avallum kudubavum sanam eettsheksham : ningall enne kattravill vishsat ennu enniyirikyunnu vekkill ente viidtill vannu papprin ennu apekshichau njangalle nibarrndichau .
njangall pratthrnasthlattekyu chelluboll vellichappadattiyayi lakshannam parranju yajamananmakyru vallare labham varuttunnoru balaykyaratti njangalle etirettu .
avall pelosinteyum njangalludeyum pinnale vannu : i manukshayr atayunnatanaydaivattinte dasanmar , rakshamaggrm ningallodu arriyikyunnavar ennu villichau parranju .
ingane avall palanall cheyatu vannu . pelo mukshinju tirinju nokyi avallilullbhootattodu : avalle vidtu pokuvan njan yeshukrisatu vinte namattill ninnodu kalpikyunnu ennu parranju . anajhyikayill tanne atu avalle vidtu poyi .
avallude yajamananmar tangallude labhattinte aashpoyepayatu kandidtu pelosineyum shiilasineyum pidichau , chantasthlattu prmannikallude adukylekyu valichau kondu poyi
adhipatikallude mumbill nirrutti : yehoodanmarayi manukshayr nammude padtnnatte kalakyi ,
rromakyaraynamukyu amgiikarippanum anusarippanum nayayamallatt aacharangalle prsamgikyunnu ennu parranju .
puruksharavum avarude nere illaki ; adhipatikall avarude vasrtm parrichaurinju koll kondu avare adippan kalpichau .
avare vallare adippichasheksham tadavill aakyi karagrahprmanniyodu avare sookshttode kappan kalpichau .
avan inganeyullkalpankidtukayall avare akatte tadavill aakyi avarude kall aamattill idtu poodti .
addhrratrikyu pelosum shiilasum pratthrichau daivatte padi satutichau : tadavukar shrddhichau kondirunnu .
pedtennu valiyoru bhookambam undayi , karagrahattinte adisthanam kulungi vatill okyeyum turrannu poyi , ellavarudeyum changalajhyinju viinnu .
karagrahaprmanni urrakyunnannaru karagrahattinte vatilukall tarrannirikyunnatu kandidtu changalakyar oadippoykyllanju ennu uhichau valloori tannettan kolluvan bhavichau .
appoll pelos : ninakyu oru dokshavum cheyaarutu ; njangall ellavarum ivide undalelennu urrakye villichau parranju .
avan vellichaam chodichau akattekyu chadi virrechaum kondu pelosinteyum shiilasinteyum mumbill viinnu .
avare purrattu kondu vannu : yajamananmare , rakshprapippan njan entu cheyeennam ennu chodichau .
kattravayyeshuvill vishsiky ; ennall niiyum ninte kudumbavum rakshaprapikyum ennu avar parranju .
pinne avar kattravinte vachanam avanodum avante viidtilullellavarodum prsamgichau .
avan ratriyill , anajhyikayill tanne , avare koodti kyondu poyi avarude murrivukalle kajhyuki ; tanum tanikyullavarellavarum tamasiyate sanam eettu .
pinne avare viidtill kaikyondu avakyru bhakshannam koduttu , daivattill vishsichaatill viidadakym aanandichau .
neram pulannarppoll adhipatikall kolkyare ayachau : amanukshayre vidtyakyennam ennu parrayichau .
karagrahprmanni i vakyu pelosinodu arriyichau : ningalle vidtyappan adhipatikall aallayachairikyunnu ; aakayall samadhanattode pokuvin ennu parranju .
pelos avarodu : rromaperanmaraynjangalle avar visataram koodute parasaymayi adippichau tadavilakyiyalela ; ippoll rahasaymayi njangalle purrattakyunnuvo ? angane alla ; avar tanne vannu njangalle purrattu kondu pokadte ennu parranju .
kolkyar avakyu adhipatikallodu bodhippichaarre avar rromperanmar ennu kedtu avar bhayappedtu chennu
avarodu nallvakyu parranju avare purrattu konduvannu padtnnam vidtu pokennam ennu apekshichau .
avar tadavu vidtu ludiyayude viidtill chennu sahodaranmare kandu aashsippichasheksham purrappedtu poyi .
avar amphipolisilum appolonayyilum koodi kadannu tesslonikyyill etti ; avide yehoodanmarude oru palli undayirunnu .
pelos pativu pole avarude adukyll chennu moonnu shabaattill tiruvejhyuttukalle aadharamakyi avarodu vadichau .
krisatu kashtam anubhavikyyum marichaavarill ninnu uyitterjhyu nnelkyyum cheyeendatu ennum njan ningallodu arriyikyunni yeshu tanne krisatu ennum telliyichau vivarichau kondirunnu .
avarill chilarum bhtiyullyavayanmarill oru valiykoodtvum manay srtiikallill anekarum vishsichau pelosinodum shiilasinodum chennaru .
yehoodanmaro asooyapoondu , minakyedtu nadakyunnachildushtanmare chettru puruksharatte illakyi padtnnattill kalaham undakyi yasonte viidu vallanju avare janasamoohattill kondu varuvan shrmichau .
avare kannanjidtu yasoneyum chilsahodaranmareyum nagaradhipanmarude adukylekyu ijhyechau kondu : bhoolokatte kalahippichaavar ivideyum etti ;
yason avare kaikyendum irikyunnu ; avar okyeyum yeshu ennmattoruvan rajavu ennu parranju kondu kaisarude niyamangallkyu prtikoolamayi prvattrikyunnu ennu nilavillichau .
itu kedtidtu puruksharavum nagaradhipanmarum bhrmichau
yason mutalayavarodu jamaym vangi avare vidtyachau .
sahodaranmar udane , ratriyill tanne , pelosi neyum shiilasineyum berovekyu parranjyachau . avide ettiyarre avar yehoodanmarude palliyill poyi .
avar tessloniiky yilullavarekyall uttmanmarayi runnu . avar vachanam poonnr jagrtayode kaikyondatllate atu angane tanneyo ennu dinabrti tiruvejhyuttukalle parishodhichau ponnu .
avarill palarum manayrayyavanasrtiikallilum purukshanmrilum anekarum vishsichau .
pelos berovayilum daivavachanam arriyichaatu tessloniikyyile yehoodanmar arrinju avideyum vannu puruksharatte illakyi bhrmippichau .
udane sahodaranmar pelosine samudr tiirattekyu parranjyachau ; shiilasum timotheyosum avide ttnne pattru .
pelosinodukoode vajhyittunnpoyavar avane athenyollam kondu poyi ; shiilasum timotheyosum kajhyiyunnvegattill tante adukyll varennam ennullkalpanvangi madangi pponnu .
athenayill pelos avakyrayi kattirikyuboll nagarattill bimbangall nirranjirikyunnatu kandu manassinnu choodu pidichau .
avan palliyill vechau yehoodanmarodum daivabhtnmarodum chantasthlattu divasenkandavarodum sambhakshichau ponnu .
eppikyooyarrrum setayikyrum aaytat njanikallill chilar avanodu vadichau . i viduvayan entu parravan pokunnu ennu chilarum avan yeshuvineyum punarutthanatteyum prsamgiky kondu : ivan anay devatakalle ghokshikyunnavan ennu tonnunnu ennu mattu chilarum parranju .
pinne avane pidichau arayopagakyunninmell kondu chennu : nii prsatavikyunni naviinopadesham innatu ennu njangallkyu arriyamo ?
nii chilapoovarrngalle njangallude cheviyill kadattunnu valela ; atu entu ennu arrivan njangall aagrhi kyunnu ennu parranju .
ennall athenar okyeyum avide vannu pakyrunnparadeshikallum vallputumayum parrakayo kellkyyo cheyvanallate mattonninnum avasaramullavarallal .
pelos arayopagamaddhey ninnu kondu parranjtu : athenapurukshanmare , ningall ellattilum atibhtanmar ennu njan kannunnu .
njan chuttinadannu ningallude poojasthanangalle nokyuboll " atdevannu " ennu ejhyuttulloru vedikyllu kandu ; ennall ningall arriyate poojikyunnatu tanne njan ningallodu arriyikyunnu .
lokavum atilullatu okyeyum undakyiydaivam sggrttinnum bhoomikyum nathanakakondu kaippnniyaykshetrngallill vasam cheyaunnilla .
tan ellavakyrum jiivanum shasavum sakalavum kodukyunnavan aakayall vallatinnum mudtullavan ennpole manukshakaikallall shushrookshaavashayppedunnilla .
bhootalattill engu kudiyirippan avan oruttnill ninnu manukshayjatiye okyeyum ullavakyi , avarude nivasattinnu atirukallum kalangallum nischayichau .
avar daivatte tappinokyi kandettumo ennu vechau avane anevkshikyendatinnu tanne . avan nammill aakyrum akannirikyunnavanallatanum .
avanilalelnam jiivikyyum charikyyum irikyyum cheyaunnatu . angane ningallude kavivaranmarilum chilar : " nam avante santanamalela " ennu parranjirikyunnu .
nam daivattinte santanam ennu varikayall daivam manukshaynte shilpavidayyum sakklpavum kondu kottittii kyrunnpon , velli , kallu ennivayodu sadrasham ennu niroopikyendatallal .
ennall arriyayyude kalangalle daivam lakshaymakyte ippoll ellayidattum ellavarum manasantarppedennamennu manukshayrodu kalpikyunnu .
tan niyamichapurukshan mukhantaram lokatte niitiyill nayayam vidhippan avan oru divasatte nischayichau ; avane marichaavarill ninnu uyitterjhyunnelpichaatinall ellavakyrum atinte urrappu nalkiyumirikyunnu .
marichaavarude punarutthanattekyurrichau kedtidtu chilar parihasichau ; mattu chilar : njangall itinepptti pinneyum ninte prsamgam kellkyum ennu parranju .
angane pelos avarude naduvill ninnu poyi .
chilpurukshanmar avanodu chennaru vishsichau ; avarill arayopagasthaniyaydiyonuseyasum damaris ennu perulloru srtiiyum mattu chilarum undayirunnu .
anantaram avan athenvidtu korintill chennu .
yehoodanmar ellavarum rromanagaram vidtu pokennam ennu keldeyas kalpichaatu kondu ittlayyill ninnu idekyu vannavanayi pontoskaran akilas ennu perulloru yehoodaneyum avante bhayarr priskyillayeyum kandu avarude adukyll chennu .
tojhyill onnakakondu avan avarodukoode pattru velcheyatu ponnu ; tojhyilo koodarappnniyayirunnu .
ennall shabaattorrum avan palliyill samvadichau yehoodanmareyum yavayanmareyum sammtippichau .
shiilasum timotheyosum makyedonayyill ninnu vannarre pelos vachanghokshannattill shukshkyanti poondu yeshu tanne krisatu ennu yehoodanmakyru sakshiikrichau .
avar etir parrakayum dukshikyyum cheykayall avan vasrtm kudanju : ningallude nashattinnu ningall tanne uttravadikall ; njan nimmrlan : inimell njan jatikallude adukyll pokum ennu avarodu parranju .
avan avidam vidtu tiittos yusetas ennoru daivabhtante viidtill chennu ; avante viidu palliyodu todtirunnu .
palliprmanniyaykrisepas tante sakalkudubatto dum koode kattravill vishsichau ; korintayrill anekar vachanam kedtu vishsichau sanam eettu .
ratriyill kattravu dasharnattill pelosinodu : nii bhayappedate prsamgiky ; mindatirikyrutu ;
njan ninnodu koode undu ; aarum ninne kayeettm cheyatu dokshppeduttukayilla ; i padtnnattill enikyu vallare janam undu ennu arullicheeyatu .
angane avan orandum aarru masavum avarude idayill daivavachanam upadeshichau kondu tamasichau .
galliyon akhayayill deshadhipati yayi vajhyuboll yehoodanmar pelosinte nere orumanppedtu ejhyunnettu , avane nayasanattinte mumbake kondu chennu :
ivan nayayaprmannattinnu virodhamayi daivatte bhajippan manukshayre sammtippikyunnu ennu parranju .
pelos vayaturrappan bhavikyuboll galliyon yehoodanmarodu : yehoodanmare : vallanayayamo vallatt patakamo aayirunnekkill njan kshamayode ningallude sakkdam kellkyumayirunnu .
vachanatteyum namangalleyum ningallude nayayaprmanntteyum sambandichaulltakyr samgatikall ekkilo ningall tanne nokyi kyollvin ; i vakekyu nayayadhipati aakuvan enikyu manassillennu parranju
avare nayyasanattikkll ninnu purrattakyi .
ellavarum palli prmanniyaysosthnesine pidichau nayayasanattinte mumbill vechau adichau ; itu onnum galliyon koodtakyiyillal .
pelos pinneyum kurrenall pattrsheksham sahodaranmarodu yatr parranjidtu , tanikyu oru nechaar undayirunnatinall kemkryayill vechau talksheram cheyaichaidtu priskyillayodum akilasinodum koode kappll kayarri surriyayilekyu purrappedtu
ephesosill etti avare avide vidtu , avan palliyill chennu yehoodanmarodu sambhakshichau .
kurrekyoode tamasikyennam ennu avar apekshichaidtu avan sammtikyate :
daivahitamundekkill njan ningallude adukyll madangi varum ennu parranju vidavangi ephesosill ninnu kappll niikyi ,
kaisayarryill vannirrangi , yerooshalemilekyu chennu , sabhaye vandnam cheyatidtu antokyyyilekyu poyi .
avide kurrenall tamasichasheksham purrappedtu , krmattale galataydeshattilum phrugayyilum sanchrichau shikshaynmare okyeyum urrappichau .
alaksantriyakyaranayi vagaivbhavavum tiruvejhyuttu kallill samatthryvumullappolelas ennu perulloru yehoodan ephesosill etti .
avan kattravinte maggrttill upadesham labhichaavan aayirunnu ; yohannante sanattekyurrichau matrm arrinjirunnu ekkilum aatmavill erivullavanakayall avan yeshuvinte vasatutsookshmayi prsatavikyyum upadeshikyyum cheyatu .
avan palliyill pragatdyttode prsamgichau tudangi ; akilasum priskyillayum avante prsamgam kedtarre avane chettrukondu daivattinte maggrm adhikam spashtamayi avannu telliyichau koduttu .
avan akhayayilekyu pokuvan ichchichaappoll sahodaranmar avane utsahippikyyum avane kaikyellendatinnu shikshaynmakyru ejhyutukayum cheyatu ; avide ettiyarre avan daivakrapayill vishsichaavakyru pallare pryojanamayittiinnur .
yeshu tanne krisatu ennu avan tiruvejhyuttukallall telliyichau balattode yehoodanmare parasaymayi khandichau kallanju .
appolelas korintill irikyuboll pelos ullprdeshangallill koodi sanchrichau ephesosill etti chilshikshaynmare kandu :
ningall vishsichaidtu parishuddhatmavine prapichauvo ennu avarodu chodichaatinnu : parishuddhatmavu undennu polum njangall kedtidtillennu avar parranju .
ennall eetayirunnu ningallude sanam ennu avan avarodu chodichaatinnu : yohannante sanam ennu avar parranju .
atinnu pelos : yohannan manasantarasanmaretkajhyippichau tante pinnale varunnavanayyeshuvill vishsikyennam ennu janattodu parranju ennu parranju .
itu kedtarre avar kattravayyeshuvinte namattill sanam eettu .
pelos avarude mell kaivechaappoll parishuddhatmavu avarude mell vannu avar anaybhakshakallill samsarikyyum prvachikyyum cheyatu .
apurukshanmar ellam koodi pantrndollam aayirunnu .
pinne avan palliyill chennu daivarajayttekyurrichau samvadichaum sammtippichaum kondu moonnu masattollam pragatdyttode prsamgichau .
ennall chilar katthinappedtu anusarikyate puruksharatti nte mumbake i maggrtte dukshichaappoll avan avare vidtu shikshaynmare vertirichau , turrannosinte patthashalyill dinabrti samvadichau ponnu .
atu randu samvrattollam nadakyyall aasayyill pakyrunnyehoodanmarum yavananmarum ellam kattravinte vachanam kellppan idayayi .
daivam pelos mukhantaram asadharannayayviiyarr prvrattikalle cheyaikyyall
avante meyemll ninnu rroomalum uttriiyavum rogikallude mell kondu vannidukayum vayadhikall avare vidtu marrukayum duratmakyll purrappedukayum cheyatu .
ennall deshantarikallayi nadakyunnmantrvadikallaychilyehoodanmar : pelos prsamgikyunnyeshuvinte namattill njan ningallodu aannayidunnu ennu parranju yeshuvinte namam cholluvan tuninju .
ingane cheyatvar mahapurohitanayskyevennoru yehoodante eejhyu putrnmar aayirunnu .
duratmavu avarodu : yeshuvine njan arriyunnu ; pelosineyum parichayamundu ; ennall ningall aar ennu chodichau .
pinne duratmavullmanukshayn avarude mell chadi avare iruvareyum kiijhyadakyi jayiky yall avar nrum murrivettvaru mayi aviidtill ninnu oadippoyi .
itu ephesosill pakyrunnsakalyehoodanmarum yavananmarum arrinju : avakyru okyeyum bhayam tadti , kattravayyeshuvinte namam mahimappedtu .
vishsichaavarill anekarum vannu tangallude prvrattikalle eettu parranju arriyichau .
kshudrpryogam cheyatirunnpalarum tangallude pusatkangalle chudtukallanju ; avayude vilkannakyu koodtiyarre ambatinayiram vellikyashu ennu kandu .
ingane kattravinte vachanam shtiyode parannu prbalappedtu .
itu kajhyinjidtu pelos makyedonayyilum akhayayilum koodi kadannu yerooshalemilekyum pokennam ennu manassill nischayichau : njan avide chennasheksham rromayum kannennam ennu parranju .
tanikyu shushrookshcheyaunnavarill timotheyos , erasetas ennrandu pere makyedonayyilekyu ayachaidtu tan kurre kyalam aasayyill tamasichau .
akalattu i maggrtte cheealli valiykalaham undayi .
vellikondu attermis deviyude kshetr roopangalle tiikyrunndemetriyos enntadtan tojhyilkyakyru vallare labham varuttivannu .
avan avareyum avakayill ullppedt velakyareyum koodti varutti : purukshanmare , nammude sambadaym i tojhyi ll kondu aakunnu ennu ningallkyu boddhy malela .
ennall i pelos ennavan kayaall tiittrtu devanmar allennu parranju kondu ephesosill matrmalla , mikyvarrum aasayyill okyeyum vallare janangalle sammtippichau marrichau kallanju ennu ningall kandum kedtum irikyunnu valela .
atinall nammude i kayarrm aakshepattill aakuvan aduttirikyunnatu mallate attermis mahadeviyude kshetrm eetumillennu varikayum aasay mujhyuvanum bhootalvum bhajichau porunnavallude mahatmym odungippokayum cheyaum ennu parranju .
avar itu kedtu rekadham nirranjvarayi : ephesayrude attermis mahadevi ennu aattru .
padtnnam mujhyuvanum kalaham kondu nirranju , avar pelosinte koodtu yatrkyaraygayos , arisatheras ennmakyedonayre pidichaukondu ramgasthlattekyu orumanappedtu panju chennu .
pelos janasamoohattill chelluvan bhavichaarre shikshaynmar avane vidtillal .
aasaydhipanmarill chilar avante senhitanmar aakayall ; ramgasthlattu chennu pokarutu ennu avarum avante adukyll aallayachau apekshichau .
janasamgham kalakyttilayi mikyperum tangall vannukoodiysamgati entennu arriyaykayall chilar inganeyum chilar anganeyum aattru .
yehoodanmar mubodtu untikyondu vannalaksantarine puruksharattill chilar samsarippan utsahippichau ; alaksantar aamgaym kadti janasamoohattodu prtivadi ppan bhavichau .
ennall avan yehoodan ennu arrinjppoll : ephesayrude attermis mahadevi ennu ellavarum koodi randumanni nerattollam eekshabdattode aattru kondirunnu .
pinne padtnnamenavan puruksharatte amattri parranjtu : ephesaypurukshanmare , ephesospadtnnam attermis mahadevikyum deyavill ninnu viinnbimbattinnum kshetr palakennu arriyatt manukshayn aar ?
itu etir mojhyiyillatttakayall ningall tidukymayi onnum cheyaate adangippakyerndatakunnu .
i purukshanmare ningall koodtikyondu vannu valela ; avar kshetrm kavachaar cheyaunnavaralla , nammude deviye dukshikyunnavarumalla .
ennall demetriyosinnum koodeyulltojhyilkyakyrum vallavanteyum nere oru samgati undekkill visatardivasangall vechaidtundu , deshadhipatikallum undu ; tammill vayvaharikydte .
verre kayarrm cholali aakunnu vadam ekkill dhammr sabhayill tiikyramalela .
innatte kalahattinnu karannamillaykayall atu nimittm nammude perill kuttm chumattuvan idayundu spashtam ; i aallkyoodtttinnu uttram parravan namukyu vakonnumillalela .
ingane parranju avan sabhaye pirichau vidtu .
kalaham shamichasheksham pelos shikshaynmare koodtivarutti prbodhippichaidtu yatr parranju makyedoneykyu purrappedtu poyi .
aprdeshangallill koodi sanchrichau avare eerriyonnu prbodhippichaidtu yavanadeshattu etti .
avide moonnu masam kajhyichaidtu surriyekyu kappll kayarri ppokuvan bhavikyuboll yehoodanmar avante nere koodtukedtu undakyukayall makyedonay vajhyiyayi madangi ppokuvan nischayichau .
berovayile purrosinte makan soparetasum tesslonikyyrayarisatherasum sekyuntosum deberrkyaranaygayosum timotheyosum aasaykyaraytuhikyosum retaphimosum aasayvare avanodu koode poyi .
avar mube poyi retavasill njangallkyayi kattirunnu .
njangallo pullippillatt appttinte perunall kajhyinji dtu philippi yill ninnu kappll kayarri anchu divasam kondu retavasill avarude adukyll etti , eejhyu divasam avide pattru .
avadtttinte onnam divasattill njangall appm nurrukyuvan koodivannappoll pelos pittennall purrappeduvan bhavichaatu kondu avarodu sambhakshichau patiravareyum prsamgam niidti .
njangall koodiyirunnmallikayill vallare villakyu undayi runnu . avide yoottikyos ennyevanakyaran killivatilkyll irunnu gaddhanidr pidichau ,
pelos vallare neram sambhakshikyyall nidravashanayi moonnam tadtill ninnu tajhye viinnu ; avane marichaavanayi eduttu kondu vannu .
pelos irrangicheennu avante mell viinnu tajhyuki bhrmikyenda ; avante prannan avanill undu ennu parranju .
pinne avan kayarricheennu appm nurrukyi tinnu pularu vollam sambhakshichau purrappedtu poyi .
avar abalane jiivanullavanayi kondu vannu atayntam aashsichau .
njangall mumbayi kappll kayarri pelosine assosill vechau kayatti kyollvan vicharichau avidekyu oadi ; avan kall nadayayi varuvan vicharichau ingane chadtm kedtiyirunnu .
avan assosill njangallodu chennarppoll avane kayatti mitulenayill etti ;
avide ninnu niikyi , pittennall khiyos diipinte tookyill etti , marrunall samos diipill annanju . pittennu milettosill etti .
kajhyiyum ekkill pentakosnallekyu yerooshalemill ettendatinnu pelos baddhppedukayall aasayyill kalatamasam vararutu ennu vechau ephesosill adukyate oadennam ennu nischayichairunnu .
milettosill ninnu avan ephesosilekyu aallaychau sabhayile mooppnmare varutti .
avar avante adukyll vannappoll avan avarodu parranjtu : njan aasayyill vannonnam nall mutall ellayepajhyum ningallodukoode enganeyirunnu ennum
vallare tyodum kannuniirodum yehoodanmarude koodtukedtukallall enikyu undaykashtangallodum koode kattravine sevichau vannu ennum
pryojanamullatu onnum marrechau vekyate parasaymayum viidu torrum ningallodu arriyikyyum upadeshikyyum cheyatu ennum
daivattikklekyullmanasantaravum tammude kattravayyeshukrisatuvilullvishasavum yehoodanmakyrum yavananmakyrum sakshiikarichau ennum ningall arriyunnu valela .
ippoll itnjan aatmavinall bandikyppedtvanayi yerooshalemilekyu pokunnu .
bandnangallum kashtangallum enikyayi kattirikyunnu ennu parishuddhatmavu padtnnam torrum sakshaym parrayunnatallte avide enikyu neriduvanullatu onnum njan arri yunnillal .
ekkilum njan ente prannane vilayerriytayi ennunnilla ; ente odtvum daivakrapayude suvishekshattinnu sakshaym parrayendatinnu kattravayyeshu tannshushrookshayum tikekyennam enne enikyullu .

phesetas samsthanattill vannidtu moonnu nall kajhyinj sheksham kaisayaaryill ninnu yerooshalemilekyu poyi .
appoll mahapurohitanmarum yehoodanmarude prdhanikallum pelosinte nere avante sannidhiyill anayayam bodhippichau ;
daycheyatu avane yerooshalemilekyu varuttendatinnu avar pelosinnu prtikoolamayi avanodu apekshichau ;

ningallill prapatiyullavar koode vannu amanukshaynte nere anayayam undekkill bodhippikydte ennu uttram parranju .

avan vannarre yerooshalemill ninnu vannyehoodanmar chuttum ninnu avante nere katthinkuttm palatum bodhi ppichau .
peloso : yehoodanmarude nayayaprmannattodakadte daivalayattodakadte kaisarodakadte njan oru kuttvum cheyatidtillennu prtivadichaarre akuttngalle telliyippan avakyru kajhyinjillal .
ennall phesetas yehoodanmarude priiti sambadippan ichchichau pelosinodu : yerooshalemilekyu chennu avide ente mumbill vechau i samgatikalle kyurrichau visataram nadappan ninakyu sammtamundo ennu chodichaati nnu pelos
njan kaisarude nayayasanattinnu mumbake nilkyunnu ; avade enne visatrikyendatakunnu ; yehoodanmarodu njan oru anayayavum cheyatidtilla ; atu niiyum nallavannm arrinjirikyunnu :
njan anayayam cheyatu marannyogaymayatu vallatum prvrttichaidtundekkill marannshiksheelkyunnatinnu enikyu virodhamilla . ivar ente nere bodhippikyunnanayayam nerallennu varikilo enne avakyru eelpichau koduppan aakyrum kajhyiyunnatallal ;
njan kaisare abhayam chollannu ennu parranju . appoll phesetas tante aalochansabhayodu samsarichaidtu : kaisare nii abhayam chollayirikyunnu ; kaisarude adukylekyu nii pokum ennu uttram parranju .
odtu nall kajhyinj sheksham agripprajavum bennariiky yum phesetasine vandnam cheyvan kaisayaayill etti .

njan yerooshalemill chennappoll yehoodanmarude mahpurohitanmarum mooppnmarum ente adukyll vannu avante nere anayayam bodhippichau vidhikyu apekshichau .

aakayall avar ivide vannu koodiyarre njan odtum tamasiyate pittennu tanne nayayasanattill irunnu apurukshane kondu varuvan kalpichau .
vadikall avante chuttum ninnu njan niroopichairunnkuttm onnum bodhippikyate
sntmatatte kyurrichaum jiivichairikyunnu ennu pelos parrayunnmarichau poyyeshu ennoruvane kyurrichaum chiltakyrsamgatikalle kondu vannateyullu .

ennall pelos chakrvattri tirumanassile vidhikyayi tanne sookshikyennam ennu abhayam chollukayall kaisarude adukyll ayakyuvollam avane sookshippan kalpichau .
amanukshaynte prsamgam kellppan enikyum aagrhamundayirunnu ennu agrippavu phesetasinodu parranjtinnu ; nalle kellkyam ennu avan parranju .

appoll phesetas parranjtu : agripprajave , ivide vannu koodiyirikyunnsakalpurukshanmarumayu llore , yehoodanmarude samooham ellam yerooshalemilum ivideyum vechau ennodu apekshikyyum avane jiivanode vecheekyrutu ennu nilavillikyyum cheyat i manukshayne ningall kannunnuvalela .
avan marannayogaymayatu onnum cheyatidtillennu njan grhichau ; avan tanneyum chakrvattri tirumanassile abhayam chollukayall avane ayakyennam ennu vidhichairikyunnu .
avane kyurrichau tirumenikyu ejhyutuvan enikyu nischaymayatu onnumilla ; atukondu visataram kajhyinjidtu ejhyutuvan vallatum undakendatinnu avane tingallude mumbilum , vishekshall agripprajave , tirumumbilum varuttiyirikyunnu .
tadavukarane ayakyuboll avante perilullkuttm kannikyatirikyunnatu yuktamallennu tonnunnu .
agrippavu pelosinodu : ninte kayaarm parravan anuvadam undu ennu parranjppoll pelos kai niidti prtivadichaatentennall :
agripprajave , yehoodanmar ente mell chumattunnellkuttngalleyum kurrichau innu tirumumbake prtivadippan idavannatu kondu ,
vishekshall nii yehoodanmarude idayile aacharangallum takyrngallum ellam arriyunnavan aakayall njan bhagayvan ennu niroopikyunnu ; atu kondu ente prtivadam kshamayode kellkyennamennu apekshikyunnu .
ente jatikyarude idayilum yerooshalemilum aadi mutall balaym tudangiyullente nadappu yehoodanmar ellavarum arriyunnu .

daivattall nammude pitakynmakyru labhichaatum
nammude pantrndu gotrngallum rappkall shrddhyode aaradhichau kondu ettippidippan aashikyunnatum aayvagdattttilullprtayashhetuvayidtretnjan ippoll visatarattill aayirikyunnatu . aprtayashaye cheealli aakunnu rajave , yehoodanmar ente mell kuttm chumattunnatu .
daivam marichaavare uyipprikyunnatu vishasayogaymallennu ningallkyu tonnunnatu entu ?
nasarrayanayyeshuvinte namattinnu virodhamayi palatum prvattrikyennam ennu njanum vicharichau sataym .
atu njan yerooshalemill cheyatidtumundu ; mahapurohitnmarodu adhikarapatrm vangi vishuddhnmarill palareyum tadavill aakyi adechau ; avare nigrhikyunnsamayam njanum sammtam koduttu .

ingane cheyatuvarikayill njan mahapurohitanmarude adhikarattodum ayodum koode damaskyosilekyu yatr pokuboll ,
rajave , nadtucheekyu njan vajhyiyill vechau sooyaarnte prkashatte kavinjoru vellichaam aakashattill ninnu enneyum ennodu koode yatr cheyaunnavareyum chutti prkashikyunnatu kandu .
njangall ellavarum nilattu viinnappoll shele , shele , nii enne upadrvikyunnatu entu ? mullinte nere utekyunnatu ninnakyu vikshamam aakunnu ennu ebrayabhakshayill ennodu parrayunnoru shabdam njan kedtu .
nii aarakunnu kattrave , ennu njan chodichaatinnu kattravu : nii uvadrvikyunnyeshu tanne njan ;
ekkilum ejhyunnettu nivinnaru nilky ; nii enne kandati nnum ini njan ninakyu prtaykshan aavanirikyunnatinnum ninne shushrookshakanum sakshiyumayi niyamippan njan ninakyu prtaykshanayi .
janattinteyum jatikalludeyum kayaill ninnu njan ninne rakshikyum .
avakyru papamochanavum ennilullvishasattall shuddhii karikyppedtvarude idayill avakashavum labhikyendatinnu avarude kannu turrappanum avare irullill ninnu vellichaattilekyum sattante adhikarattill ninnu daivattikklekyum tirippanum njan ippoll ninne avarude adukyll ayakyunnu ennu kalpichau .
atu kondu agripprajave , njan sggriiydasharnatti nnu anusarannakyedu kannikyate

ingane prtivadikyyill phesetas : pelose , ninakyu bhrantundu ; vidayabahutttall ninakyu bhrantu pidichairikyunnu ennu urrakye parranju .
atinnu pelos : rajashrii phesetase , enikyu bhrantilla ; njan satayvum subodhavumayvakyretsamsarikyunnatu .

kappll kattinte nere nilpan kajhyiyatvannm kudungukyall njangall kaividtu angane parrippoyi .

avar vallare padtinni kidannsheksham pelos avarude naduvill ninnu kondu parranjtu : purukshanmare , ente vakyu anusarichau rekattyill ninnu niikyateyum i kashtanashtangall sambadikyateyum irikyendatayirunnu .

patinnalam ratriyayappoll njangall adriyakydalill alayunneram addhr ratriyill oru karekyu samiipikyunnu ennu kapplkyakyru tonni .

atu kondu aaharam kajhyikyennam ennu njan ningallodu apekshikyunnu ; atu ningallude rakshekyullatlela ; ningallill oruttnteyum talayile oru romam po lum nashtamakayillnischayam ennu parranju .

avidatte babarranmar njangallkyu asadharanndaykannichau majhyayum shiitavum nimittm tii koodti njangalle okyeyum kaikyondu .

avano ajantuvine tiiyill kudanju kallanju , doksham onnum pattiyillal .

avade sahodaranmare kandu tangallodu koode eejhyu nall tamasikyennam ennu avar apekshichau ; pinne njangall rromayill etti .

rromayill ettiysheksham tanikyu kavalaypadayalliyodu koode verridtu pappran pelosinnu anuvadam kidti .
moonnu divasam kajhyinjidtu avan yehoodanmarill prdhanikallayavare villippichau . avar vannu koodiyappoll avarodu parranjtu : sahodaranmare , njan janattinno pitakynmarude aacharangallkyo virodhamonnum cheyatidti llatirikye enne yerooshalemill ninnu baddhnayi rromkyarude kayaill eelpichau .
avar visatrichaarre marannayogaymayatu onnum ennill kannaykayall enne vidtyappan avakyru manassundayi runnu .

avar avanodu : ninte samgatikyu yehoodayyill ninnu njangallkyu ejhyuttu varikayo sahodaranmarill aarum vannu ninnekyondu yatoru dokshavum parrakayo cheyatidtillal .
ekkilum i matabhedattinnu ellayidattum virodham parrayunnu ennu njangall arriyunnatinnall ninte matam innatu ennu nii tanne parranju kellppan aagrhikyunnu ennu parranju .
oru divasam nischayichaidtu palarum avante pappridattill avante adukyll vannu ; avarodu avan daivarajay ttinnu sakshaym parranju mosheyude nayayaprmannavum prvachakapusatkangallum aadharamakyi yeshuvinekyurrichau avakyru bodham varumarru ravile tudangi sandyvare vivarichau ;
avan parranjtu chilar sammtichau ; chilar vishsichaillal .
avar tammill yojikyate pirinju pokuboll pelos avarodu oru vakyu parranjtentennall :
" ningall chevikondu kedtidtum grhikyatirikyum ; kannukondu kandidtum kannatirikyum ; kannu kondu kannateyum chevikondu kellkyateyum hradayam kondu grhichau manantiriyateyum
njan avare sekhaymakyateyum irikyendatinnu i janattinte hradayam tadichairikyunnu . avarude chevi kellppan mandmayirikyunnu ; avarude kannu adechairikyunnu ennu i janattinte adukyll poyi parraka " enningane parishuddhatmavu yeshayaprvachakan mukhantaram ningallude pitakynmarodu parranjirikyunnatu shari tanne .
aakayall daivam tante i rakshjatikallkyu ayachairikyunnu ; avar kellkyum ennu ningall arrinju kollvin .

poonnr pragatdyttode vighm koodate daivarajaym prsamgichaum kattravayyeshukrisatuvine kyurrichau upade shichaum ponnu .
