tante prvachakanmar mukhantaram mumbukoodti vagdattm cheyat suvishekshattinnayi vertirichau villikyppedt apposatlanum yeshukrisatuvinte dasanumaypelos
rromayill daivattinnu priyarum villikyppedt vishuddhnmarumayellavakyrum ejhyutunnatu :
nammude pitavaydaivattikkll ninnum kattravayyeshukrisatuvikkll ninnum ningallkyu krapayum samadhanavum undakadte .
jaddam sambandichau daviidinte santatiyill ninnu janikyyum marichaidtu uyitterjhyunnelkyyall vishuddhiyude aatmavu sambandichau daivaputrn ennu shtiyode ninnryikyppedukayum cheyatirikyunnavanalalel
njangall avante namattinnayi sakalajatikalludeyum idayill vishasattinnu anusarannam varuttendatinnu krapayum apposatlatvum prapichaatu .
avarill yeshukrisatuvinnayi villikyppedt ningallum ullppedtirikyunnu .
ningallude vishasam savaar lokattilum prsiddhmayiri kyunnatinall njan aadaym tanne ente daivattinnu yeshukrisatu mukhantaram ningallkyellavakyrum vendi setatrm cheyaunnu .
njan idavidate ningalle oattrukondu daiveshtttall eppoll ekkilum ningallude adukyll varuvan sadhikyendatinnu ente pratthrnayill eppojhyum yachikyunnu
ennullatinnu avante putrnekyurrichaullsuvishekshagho kshannattill njan ente aatmavill aaradhikyunndaivam enikyu sakshi .
ningallude sthiriikarannattinnayi aatmikavaram vallatum ningallkyu nalkendatinnu ,
atayatu ningallkyum enikyum ottorumichaullvishasttall ningallodukoode enikyum aashasam labhikyendtinnu njan ningalle kannman vanchikyunnu .
ennall sahodaranmare , enikyu sheksham jatikallill ennapole ningallilum vallphalavum undakendatinnu ningallude adukyll varuvan palappojhyum bhavichau ekkilum ituvare mudakym vannu ennu ningall arriyatirikyrutu ennu njan aagrhikyunnu .
yavananmakyrum babarranmakyrum njanikallkyum buddhihiinakyrum njan kadakyaran aakunnu .
angane rromilullningallodum suvisheksham arriyippan ennall aavollam njan orungiyirikyunnu .
suvishekshattekyurrichau enikyu lyilla ; vishsikyunneevannum aadaym yehoodannum pinne yavanannum atu rakshekyayi daivashtiyakunnuvalela .
atill daivattinte niiti vishasam hetuvayum vishasattinnayikyondum vellippedunnu . " niitiman vishasattall jiivikyum " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnuvalela .
aniitikondu sataytte tadukyunnmanukshayrude sakalabhtikyum aniitikyum nere daivattinte kopam sggrttill ninnu vellippedunnu .
daivattekyurrichau arriyakunnatu avakyru vellivayiri kyunnu ; daivam avakyru vellivakyiyalela .
avante nitayshtiyum divaytvumayi avante adrashay lakshannangall lokasrashti mutall avante prvrattikallall buddhikyu vellivayi vellippedtu varunnu ; avakyru prtivdamillatirikyendatinnu tanne .
avar daivatte arrinjidtum avane daivamennu oattru mahatiikarikyyo nandi kannikyyo cheyaate tangallude niroopannangallill vaytthrrayittiinnaru , avarude vivekami llatt hradayam irundu poyi .
njanikall ennu parranju kondu avar mooddharayippoyi ;
akshayanaydaivattinte tejassine avar kshayamullmanukshayn , pakshi , nalkyali , ijhyajati ennivayude roopasadrashaymayi mattikyllanju .
atu kondu daivam avare tangallude hradayangallile mohangallill sntashariirangalle tammill tammill avamani kyendatinnu ashuddhiyill eelpichau .
daivattinte sataym avar vayajamakyi mattikyllanju , srashtichaavanekyall srashtiye bhajichau aaradhichau ; avan ennekyum vajhyttppedtvan , aamen .
atukondu daivam avare avamanaragangallill eelpichau ; avarude srtiikall sabhavikabhogatte sbhavaviruddhmkyikyllanju .
avaannm purukshanmarum sabhaviksrtiibhogamvidtu aneynaym kamam jlichau aannodu aan avalakshannamayatu prvattrichau . ingane avar tangallude vibhrmattinnu yogaymayprtiphalam tangallill tanne prapichau .
daivatte parinjanattill dharippan ishtamillanjtinnu takyvannm daivam avare uchitamallatttu cheyvan nikrashtabuddhiyill eelpichau .
avar sakalaniitiyum dushtatayum atayagrhavum dubaaru ddhiyum nirranjvar ; asooya , kula , pinnakym , kapadam , dushshiilam ennivtingiyavar ,
kurallakyar , eekshannikyar , daivadevkshikall , nikshtthooranmar , gavaarikshtthanmar , aatmprshamsakyar , putudoksham sakklpikyu nnavar , matapitakynmare anusarikyattvar , buddhihiinar ,
niyamalamghikall , vlaymillattvar , kanivattvar .
i vakprvrattikyunnavar marannayogayr ennulldaivanayayam avar arrinjidtum avaye prvattriky matrmallprvattrikyunnavarill prsadikyyumkoode cheyaunnu .
atukondu vidhikyunneetu manukshaynumayullove , ninakyu prtivadam parravan illa ; anayne vidhikyunnatill nii ninnettnne kuttm vidhikyunnu ; vidhikyunnnii atu tanne prvattrikyunnuvalela .
ennall aavakprvattrikyunnavarude nere daivattinte vidhi satayanusarannayayirikyunnu ennu nam arriyunnu .
aavakprvattrikyunnavare vidhikyyum atu tanne prvattrikyyum cheyaunnmanukshaya , nii daivattinte vidhiyill ninnu tetti ojhyiyum ennu ninekyunnuvo ?
alla , daivattinte dayninne manasantarattilekyu nadattunnu ennu arriyate nii avante daya , kshama , diigharkshanti ennivayude eeshyaarm nirasikyunnuvo ?
ennall ninte katthinayttalum anutapamillatt hradayattalum nii daivattinte niitiyullvidhi vellippedunnkopadivasattekyu ninakyu tanne kopam charatichau vekyunnu .
avan oaroruttnnu avanavante prvrattikyu taky pakaram cheyaum .
nallprvrattikyu vendunnsthiratpoondu tejassum manavum akshayatayum anevkshikyunnavakyru nitayjiivanum ,
shatthaym poondu sataym anusarikyate aniiti anusarikyunnavakyru kopavum rekadhavum kodukyum .
tinmprvattrikyunneetu manukshayatmavinnum kashtavum sakkdavum aadaym yehoodannum pinne yavanannum varum .
nanmprvattrikyunneevannum mahatvum manavum samadhanavum aadaym yehoodannum pinne yavanannum labhikyum .
daivattinte pakyll mukhapaksham illalela .
nayayaprmannam illate papam cheyatvar okyeyum nayayaprmannam koodate nashichau pokum ; nayayaprmannam undayidtu papam cheyatvar okyeyum nayayaprmannattall vidhikyppedum .
nayayaprmannam kellkyunnavaralldaivasannidhiyill niitimanmar ; nayayaprmannam aacharikyunnavararetniitiikarikyppedunnatu .
nayayaprmannamillatt jatikall nayayaprmannattilullatu sbhavattall cheyauboll nayayaprmannamillatt avar tangallkyu tanne oru nayayaprmannam aakunnu .
avarude manassakshikoode sakshaym parranjum avarude vicharangall tammill kuttm chumattukayo prtivadikyyo cheyatumkondu avar nayayaprmannattinte prvratti tangallude hradayattill ejhyutiyirikyunnatayi kannikyunnu ;
daivam yeshukrisatumukhantaram manukshayrude rahasayngalle ente suvishekshaprkaram nayayam vidhikyunnnallill tanne .
niiyo yehoodan ennu per kondum nayayaprmannttill aashryichaum
daivattill prshamsichaum nayayaprmannattill ninnu patthikyyall avante ishtam arrinjum bhedabhedangall vivechichaum
njanattinteyum satayttinteyum sroopam nayayaprmannttill ninnu ninakyu labhichaatu kondu nii kurudakyru vajhyi kadtunnavan ,
irudtilullavakyru vellichaam , mooddhare patthippikyunnavan , shishukyllkyu upadeshtavu ennu urrechaumirikyunnekkill - he ,
anayne upadeshikyunnavane , nii ninnettnne upadeshi kyatttu entu ? moshtikyrutu ennu prsamgikyunnnii moshtikyunnuvo ?
vaybhicharam cheyaarutu ennu parrayunnnii vaybhicharam cheyaunnuvo ? vigrhangalle verrukyunnnii kshetrm kavachaar cheyaunnuvo ?
nayayaprmannattill prshamsikyunnnii nayayaprmannlamghanattall daivatte apamanikyunnuvo ?
" ningall nimittm daivattinte namam jatikallude idayill dukshikyppedunnu " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnuvalela .
nii nayayaprmannam aacharichaall pariedanpryojanamulltu sataym ; nayayaprmannlamghiyayalo ninte parie danagrchammrmayittiinnur .
agrchammri nayayaprmannattinte niyamangalle prmannichaall avante agrchammrm pariedanennu ennukayillayo ?
sbhavattall agrchammriyayavan nayayaprmannam anukshtthikyunnu ekkill aksharavum pariedanayumullnayayaprmannalamghiyayninne avan vidhikyyillayo ?
purrame yehoodanayavan yehoodanalla ; purrame jaddattilullatu pariedanayumallal ;
akame yehoodanayavanaretyehoodan ; aksharattilallaatmavilullhradayapariedanayaretpariedana ; avannu manukshayralalldaivattall tanne puk labhikyum .
ennall yehoodannu entu vishekshata ? alla , pariedanyall entu pryojanam ?
sakalvidhattilum vallare undu ; onnamatu daivattinte arullappadukall avarude pakyll samapprichairikyunnatu tanne .
chilar vishsichaillekkill avarude avishasattall daivattinte vishsattekyu niikym varumo ? oru nallum illal .
" ninte vakyukallill nii niitiikarikyppeduvanum , ninte nayayvisatarattill jayippanum " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnatu pole daivam satayvan , sakalmanukshayrum bhokshkyu parrayunnavar enne varoo .
ennall nammude aniiti daivattinte niitiye prsiddh makyunnu ekkill nam entu parrayum ? shikshnadattunndaivam niitiyillattvan enno ? - njan manukshariiti yill parrayunnu - oru nallumallal ;
alelkkill daivam lokatte engane vidhikyum ?
daivattinte sataym ente bhokshkyinall avante mahat ttinnayi adhikam tellivayi ekkill enne papi ennu vidhikyunnatu entu ?
nallatu varendatinnu tiiyatu cheykennu parrayaruto ? njangall angane parrayunnu ennu chilar njangalle dukshichau parrayunnuvalela . ivakyru varunnshikshavidhi niitiyullatu tanne .
aakayall entu ? namukyu vishekshatayundo ? ashekshmilla ; yehoodanmarum yavananmarum oru pole papattin kiijhyakunnu ennu nam mube telliyichauvalela ;
" niitiman aarumilla . oruttn polumillal .
grhikyunnavan illa , daivatte anevkshikyunnavanum illal .
ellavarum vajhyitetti oru pole kollarutattvarayi ttiinnur . nanmcheyaunnavanilla , oruttn polum illal .
avarude tondturrannshavakyujhyi ; navu kondu avar chatikyunnu ; sapprviksham avarude adharangallkyu kiijhye undu .
avarude vayill shapavum kaippum nirranjirikyunnu .
avarude kall rtam choriyuvan baddhppedunnu .
nashavum arishtatayum avarude vajhyikallill undu .
samadhanmaggrm avar arrinjidtillal .
avarude drashtiyill daivabhayam illa " enningane ejhyutiyirikyunnuvalela .
nayayaprmannam parrayunnatu ellam nayayaprmannattin kiijhyullavarodu prsatavikyunnu ennu nam arriyunnu . angane eetu vayum adanju savaar lokavum daivasnnidhiyill shikshyogaymayittiirendatareta .
atukondu nayayaprmannattinte prvrattikallall oru jaddavum avante sannidhiyill niitiikarikyppedukayilla ; nayayaprmannattall papattinte parinjanamaretvarunnatu .
ippojhyo daivattinte niiti , vishsikyunnellavakyrum yeshukrisatuvikkle vishasattalulldaivaniiti tanne , nayayaprmannam koodate vellippedtu vannirikyunnu .
atinnu nayayaprmannavum prvachakanmarum sakshaym parrayunnu .
oru vaytayasavumilla ; ellavarum papam cheyatu daivtejassu illattvarayittiinnur ,
avante krapayall krisatuyeshuvikkle viindeduppumoolam sejanaymayaretniitiikarikyppedunnatu .
vishsikyunnavakyru avan tante rtam moolam prayitt makuvan daivam avane parasaymayi nirruttiyirikyu nnu . daivam tante porrumayill munkajhyinj papangalle shikshikyate viduknimittm tante niitiye prdasharippi ppan ,
tan niitimanum yeshuvill vishsikyunnavane niitiikari kyunnavanum aakendatinnu ikyalattu tante niitiye prdasharippippan tanne angane cheyattu .
aakayall prshamsevide ? atu poyepayi . eetu maggrttall ? kammrmaggrttalo ? alla , vishasamaggr ttalareta .
angane manukshayn nayayaprmannattinte prvratti koodate vishasattall tanne niitiikarikyppedunnu ennu nam anumanikyunnu .
alla , daivam yehoodanmarude daivam matrmo ? jatiklludeyum daivamallayo ? ate jatikalludeyum daivam aakunnu .
daivam eekanalela ; avan vishasam moolam pariedanakyreyum vishasattall agrchammrikalleyum niitiikarikyunnu .
aakayall nam vishasattall nayayaprmannatte dubaarlmakyunnuvo ? oru nallum illa ; nam nayayaprmannatte urrappikyyaretcheyaunnu .
ennall nammude poovaarpitavayabraham jaddaprkaram entu prapichau ennu parrayendu ?
abraham prvrattiyall niitiikarikyppedtu ekkill avannu prshamsippan samgati undu ; daivasannidhiyill illatanum , tiruvejhyuttu entu parrayunnu ?
" abraham daivatte vishsichau ; atu avannu niitiyayi kannakyidtu " ennu tanne .
ennall prvattrikyunnavannu kooli kannakyidunnatu krapayayidtllkadamayidtreta .
prvattrikyattvan ekkilum abhtane niitiikarikyunnvanill vishsikyunnavanno avante vishasam niitiyayi kannakyidunnu .
daivam prvratti koodate niiti kannakyidunnmanukshaynte bhagaym daviidum vannrikyunnatu :
" adhammrm mochichaum papam marrechaum kidtiyavar bhagayvnmar .
kattravu papam kannakyidatt manukshayn bhagayvan . "
i bhagay vannrnam pariedanekyo ? agrchammrttinnu koodeyo ? abrahaminnu vishasam niitiyayi kannakyidtu ennalelnam parrayunnatu .
engane kannakyidttu ? pariedanayilo ? agrchammrtti lo ? pariedanayilalla . agrchammrttilate .
agrchammrttill vechau undayirunnvishasaniitikyu mudr yayi pariedanennadayallam avannu labhichaatu agrchmmrttode vishsikyunnavakyrum koode niiti kannakyidappedu vantakyvannm tan avakyru ellavakyrum pitavayirikye ndatinnum
pariedanmatrmullavarallnammude pitavayabrahminnu agrchammrttill vechaau undayirunnvishasatte anugamikyunnavarumaypariedanakyakyru pitavayiri kyendatinnum tanne .
lokavakashi aakum ennullvagdattm abrahami nno avante santatikyo nayayaprmannattalallvishsattinte niitiyalalellabhichaatu .
ennall nayayaprmannamullavar avakashikall ekkill vishasam vaytthrvum vagdattm dubaarlavum ennu varum .
nayayaprmannamo kopattinnu hetuvakunnu ; nayayaprmannam illattedattu lamghanavumillal .
atukondu krapadanam ennu varendatinnu vishasttalaretavakashikall aakunnatu ; vagdattm sakalsantatikyum , nayayaprmannamullavakyru matrmalla , abrahminte vishasamullavakyrum koode urrappakendatinnu tanne .
marichaavare jiivippikyyum illatttine ullatineppole villikyyum cheyaunnavanayi tan vishsichadaivattinte drashtiyill avan namukyellavakyrum pitavakendatinnu tanne . " njan ninne bahujatikallkyu pitavakyive chau " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnuvalela .
" ninte santati ivaannm aakum " ennu arullicheeyatirikyu nnatu pole tan bahujatikallkyu pitavakum ennu avan aashekyu virodhamayi aashayode vishsichau .
avan eekadesham noorru vayassullavanakayall tante shariiram nijjariivamayippeyatum sarrayude gabharpatrttinte nijjariivatvum grhichaidtum vishasattill kshiinnichaillal .
daivattinte vagdattttikkll avishasattall samshayikyate vishasattill shtippedtu daivattinnu mahatm koduttu ,
avan vagdattm cheyattu prvattrippanum shtan ennu poonnrmayi urrechau .
atukondu atu avannu niitiyayi kannakyidtu .
avannu kannakyidtu ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnatu avane vicharichau matrm alla , namme vicharichaum koode aakunnu .
nammude atikrmangall nimittm marannattinnu eelpichaum nammude niitiikarannattinnayi uyipprichaumirikyunna
nammude kattravayyeshuvine marichaavarill ninnu uyippri chaaavanill vishsikyunnnamukyum kannakyiduvanullatakyall tanne .
vishasattall niitiikarikyppedtidtu nammude kattravayyeshukrsatumoolam namukyu daivattodu samadhanam undu .
nam nilkyunni krapayilekyu namukyu avanmoolam vishasattall prveshanavum labhichairikyunnu ; nam daivatejassinte prtayashayill prshamsikyunnu .
atu tanne alla , kashtatsahikshnnatayeyum sahikshnnatsiddhtayeyum siddhtprtayashayeyum ullavakyunnu ennu arrinju
nam kashtangallilum prshamsikyunnu .
prtayashekyo bhamgam varunnilla ; daivattinte senham namukyu nalkappedt parishuddhatmavinall nammude hradayangallill pakannaririkyunnuvalela .
nam balahiinar aayirikyuboll tanne krisatu taky samayattu abhtakyru vendi marichau .
nitimannu vendi aarekkilum marikyunnatu dullarbham ; gunnavannu vendi pakshe marippan tuniyumayirikyum .
krisatuvo nam papikall aayirikyuboll tanne namukyu vendi marikyyall daivam tanikyu nammodullsenhatte prdasharippikyunnu .
avante rtattall niitiikarikyppedtshekshamo nam avanall etr adhikamayi kopattill ninnu rakshikyppedum .
shatrukyllayirikyuboll tanne namukyu avante putrnte marannattall daivattodu nirappu vannu ekkilum nirannasheksham nam avante jiivanall etr adhikamayi rakshikyppedum .
atryumalla , namukyu ippoll nirappu labhichaatinnu karannamaynammude kattravayyeshukrisatu mukhantaram nam daivattill prshamsikyyum cheyaunnu .
atukondu eekmanukshaynall papavum papattall marannavum lokattill kadannu . ingane ellavarum papam cheykayall marannam sakalmanukshayrilum parannirikyunnu .
papamo nayayaprmannamvare lokattill undayirunnu ; ennall nayayaprmannam illatirikyuboll papatte kannakyidunnilla .
ekkilum varuvanullavante prtiroopamayaadaminte lamghanattinnu tulaymayi papam cheyaattvarilum marannam aadam mutall moshe vare vannirunnu .
ennall lamghanattinte kayaarvum krapavarattinte kayaarvum oru poleyall eekante lamghanattall anekar marichau ekkill daivakrapayum eekmanukshaynayyeshukrsatuvinte krapayalulldanavum anekakyru vendi eettvum adhikam kavinjirikyunnu .
eekan papam cheyattinte phalavum danattinte kayaarvum oru poleyalla ; eekante papam shikshavidhi kalpippan hetuvayittiinnaru . krapavaramo aneklamghanangalle mochikyunnniitiikarannavidhikyu hetuvayittiinnur .
eekante lamghanattall marannam aeekan nimittm vannu ekkill krapayudeyum niitidanattinteyum samraddhi labhikyu nnavar yeshukrisatu enneekan nimittm eettvum adhikamayi jiivanill vajhyum .
angane eeklamghanattall sakalmanukshaykyrum shikshavi dhi vannatupole eekaniitiyall sakalamanukshaykyrum jiivkarannamayniitiikarannavum vannu .
eekmanukshaynte anusarannakyedinall anekar papikllayittiinnartu pole eekante anusarannattall anekr niitimanmarayittiirum .
ennall lamghanam perukendatinnu nayayaprmannavum idayill chennaru vannu ; ekkilum papam perukiyedattu krapatayntam vaddhrichau .
papam marannattall vannatu pole krapayum nammude kattravayyeshukrisatu mukhantaram niitiyall nitayjiivannayi vajhyendatinnu tanne .
aakayall nam entu parrayendu ? krapperukendatinnu papam cheyatu kondiriky enno ?
oru nallum arutu . papasambandmayi marichaavaraynam ini atill jiivikyunnatu engane ?
alla , yeshukrisatuvinodu cheruvan sanam eettvaraynam ellavarum avante marannattill pakkallikallakuvan sanam eettirikyunnu ennu ningall arriyunnillayo ?
angane nam avante marannattill pakkallikallayittiinnar sanattall avanodukoode kujhyichaidappedtu ; krisatu marichaidtu pitavinte mahimayall jiivicheejhyunnetttu pole namum jiivante putakyttill nadakyendatinnu tanne .
avante marannattinte sadrashayttodu nam eekiibhavichaavaryekkill punarutthanattinte sadrashayttodum eekiibhavi kyum .
nam ini papattinnu adimappedatavannm papashariirttinnu niikym varendatinnu nammude pajhyaymanukshayn avanodukoode krooshikyppedtu ennu nam arriyunnu .
angane marichaavan papattill ninnu mochanam prapichairikyunnu .
nam krisatuvinodu koode marichau ekkill avanodukoode jiivikyum ennu vishsikyunnu .
krisatu marichaidtu uyitterjhyunnettirikyyall ini marikyyilla ; marannattinnu avante mell ini kattrrtmillennu nam arriyunnuvalela .
avan marichaatu papasambandmayi orikylayidtu marichau ; avan jiivikyunnato daivattinnu jiivikyunnu .
avaannm ningallum papasambandmayi marichaavar ennum krisatuyeshuvill daivattinnu jiivikyunnavar ennum ningallettnne ennuvin .
aakayall papam ningallude mataryshariirattill atinte mohangalle anusarikyumarru ini vajhyarutu ,
ningallude avayavangalle aniitiyude aayudhangallayi papattinnu samapprikyyum arutu . ningallettnne marichaidtu jiivikyunnavarayum ningallude avayavangalle niitiyude aayudhangallayum daivattinnu samapprichau kollvin .
ningall nayayaprmannattinnalla , krapekyretadhiinarakayall papam ningallill kattrrtm nadattukayillalela .
ennall entu ? nayayaprmannattinnallkrapekyretadhiinarakayall nam papam cheykenno ? oru nallum arutu .
ningall dasanmarayi anusarippan ningallettnne samapprikyyum ningall anusarichau porukayum cheyaunnavannu dasanmar aakunnu ennu arriyunnillayo ? onnukill marannattinnayi papattinte dasanmar , alelkkill niitikyayi anusarannattinte dasanmar tanne .
ennall ningall papattinte dasanmar aayirunnuve kkilum ningalle patthippichupadesharoopatte hradayapoovaarm anusarichau
papattill ninnu satantrym labhichau niitikyu dasanmarayittiinnartu kondu daivattinnu setatrm .
ningallude jaddattinte balahiinatnimittm njan manukshriitiyill parrayunnu . ningallude avayavangalle adhammrttinnayi ashuddhikyum adhammrttinnum adimakallakyi samapprichaatu pole ippoll ningallude avayavangalle vishuddhiikarannattinnayi niitikyu adimakallakyi samapprippin .
ningall papattinnu dasanmarayirunnappoll niitiye sambandichau stantrrayirunnuvalela .
ningallkyu annu entoru phalam undayirunnu ? ippoll ningallkyu l tonnunnatu tanne . atinte avasanam marannamalela .
ennall ippoll papattill ninnu satantrym prapichau daivattinnu dasanmarayirikyyall ningallkyu labhikyunnphalam vishuddhiikarannavum atinte antam nitayjiivanum aakunnu .
papattinte shamballam marannamareta ; daivattinte krapavaramo nammude kattravayyeshukrisatuvill nitayjiivan tanne .
sahodaranmare , nayayaprmannam arriyunnavarodalelnjan samsarikyunnatu : manukshayn jiivanodirikyum kalattokyeyum nayayaprmannattinnu avante mell adhikaramundu ennu ningall arriyunnillayo ?
bhattravullsrtii jiivichairikyunnbhattravinodu nayayaprmnnattall bandikyppedtirikyunnu . bhattravu marichaall avall bhattrrnayayaprmannattill ninnu ojhyivullavallayi .
bhattravu jiivichairikyuboll avall verre purukshannu aayall vaybhicharinni ennu per varum ; bhattravu marichau ekkilo avall verre purukshannu aayall vaybhicharinni ennu varatavannm nayayprmannattill ninnu stantr yakunnu .
atu kondu sahodaranmare , nam daivattinnu phalam kaykyumarru marichaidtu uyitterjhyunnettvanayverroruvannu aakendatinnu ningallum krisatuvinte shariiram mukhantaram nayayaprmannasambandmayi marichairikyunnu .

ippojhyo , nammepidichaadakyiyirunnnayayaprmannam sambandichau marichairikykondu aksharattinte pajhyakyttilallaatmavinte putukyttill tanne sevikyendatinnu nam nayayaprmannattill ninnu ojhyivullavarayirikyunnu .
aakayall nam entu parrayendu ? nayayaprmannam papam enno ? orunallum arutu . ekkilum nayayaprmannttall allate njan papatte arrinjilla ; mohikyrutu ennu nayayaprmannam parrayatirunnekkill njan mohatte arrikayillayirunnu .
papamo avasaram labhichaidtu kalpanayall ennill sakalvidhmohatteyum janippichau ; nayayaprmannam koodate papam nijjariivamakunnu .
njan oru kalattu nayayaprmannam koodate jiivichairunnu ; ennall kalpanvannappoll papam viindum jiivikyyum njan marikyyum cheyatu .
ingane jiivannayi labhichairunnkalpanenikyu marannhetuvayittiinnaru ennu njan kandu .
papam avasaram labhichaidtu kalpanayall enne chatikyyum kollukayum cheyatu .
aakayall nayayaprmannam vishuddhm ; kalpanvishuddhvum nayayavum nallatum tanne .
ennall nanmayayullatu enikyu marannakarannamayittiinnur enno ? oru nallum arutu , papamaretmarannamayittiinnar tu ; atu nanmayayullatinekyondu enikyu marannam ullavakyunnatinall papam ennu telliyendatinnum kalpanayall atayntam papamayittiirendatinnum tanne .
nayayaprmannam aatmikam ennu nam arriyunnuvalela ; njano jaddamayan , papattinnu dasanayi vilky ppedtvan tanne .
njan prvattrikyunnatu njan arriyunnilla ; njan ichchikyu nnatine allpakekyunnatine aretcheyaunnatu .
njan ichchikyatttine cheyaunnu ekkilo nayayaprmnnam nallatu ennu njan sammtikyunnu .
aakayall atine prvattrikyunnatu njanallennill vasikyunnpapamareta .

angane nanmcheyvan ichchikyunnnjan tinmente pakyll undu ennoru prmannam kannunnu .
ullam kondu njan daivattinte nayayaprmannattill rasikyunnu .

atukondu ippoll krisatuyeshuvilullavakyru oru shikshavidhiyum illal .

daivatmavu nadattunnavar eevarum daivattinte makyll aakunnu .

avaannm tanne aatmavu nammude balahiinatekyu tunnani lkyunnu . vendumpole pratthrikyendatu entennu nam arriyunnillalela . aatmavu tanne uchaarichau koodatt njarakyngallall namukyu vendi pakshavadam cheyaunnu .
ennall aatmavu vishuddhkyruvendi daivahitaprkaram pakshavadam cheyaunnatukondu aatmavinte chintinnatennu hradayangalle parishodhikyunnavan arriyunnu .
ennall daivatte senhikyunnavakyru , ninnryaprkaram villikyppedtvakyru tanne , sakalavum nanmekyayi koodi vayaparikyunnu ennu nam arriyunnu .
avan munnarrinjvare tante putrn anekam sahodaranmarill aadayjatan aakendatinnu avante sroopattodu anurooparakuvan munniyamichaumirikyunnu .
munniyamichaavare villichaum villichaavare niitiikarichaum niitiikarichaavare tejaskyrichaumirikyunnu .
itu sambandichau nam entu parrayendu ? daivam namukyu anukoolam ekkill namukyu prtikoolam aar ?
sntputrne aadarikyate namukyu ellavakyrum vendi eelpichau tannavan avanodukoode sakalavum namukyu nalkatirikyumo ?
daivam tiranjeduttvare aar kuttm chumattum ? niitiikarikyunnavan daivam .
shikshvidhikyunnavan aar ? krisatu yeshu marichaavan ; marichaidtu uyitterjhyunnettvan tanne ; avan daivattinte valattubhagattirikyyum namukyu vendi pakshavadam kajhyikyyum cheyaunnu .
krisatuvinte senhattill ninnu namme verpirikyunnatar ? kashtatayo sakkdamo upadrvamo padtinniyo ntayo aapatto vallo ?
" ninte nimittm njangalle idavidate kollunnu ; arruppanullaadukalleppole njangalle ennunnu " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnuvalela .
namo namme senhichaavan mukhantaram itill okyeyum poonnrjayam prapikyunnu .
marannattinno jiivanno dootanmakyervkallkyo adhikarangallkyo ippojhyullatinno varuvanullatinno

njan krisatuvill sataym parrayunnu ; njan parrayunnatu bhokshkylla ;
enikyu valiydu : khavum hradayattill idavidate novum undu ennu ente manassakshi enikyu parishuddhatmavill sakshiyayirikyunnu .

avar yisrayelayr ; putrtvum tejassum niyamangallum nayayaprmannavum aaradhanayum vagdattngallum avakyru llava ;

aamen , daivavachanam vrathavayippoyi ennalla ; yisrayelill ninnu utdvichaavar ellam yisrayelayr ennum

atryumalla , rribekyyum nammude pitavayyishakyu enneekanall gabharm dharichau ,

aakayall nam entu parrayendu ? daivattinte pakyll aniiti undo ? orunallum illa .

atu kondu ichchikyunnavanalumalla , oadunnavanalumalla , karunntonnunndaivattalaretsakalavum sadhikyu nnatu .

angane tanikyu manassullavanodu avannu karunntonnunnu ; tanikyu manassullavare avan katthinanakyunnu .

ayeea , manukshaya , daivattodu prtayuttram parrayunnnii aar ? mananjirikyunnatu mananjvanodu : nii enne ingane chamechaatu entu ennu chodikyumo ?
alla , kushavannu ate pindttill ninnu oru patrm manattinnum mattoru patrm apamanattinnum undakyu van manninmell adhikaram illayo ?

yehoodanmarill ninnu matrmalla , jatikallill ninnum villichau tejassinnayi munnorukyiykarunnapatrngallaynammill
tante tejassinte dhanam vellippeduttuvanum ichchichaidtu nashayogaymaykopapatrngalle vallare diigharkshamyode sahichau ekkill entu ?
" ente janamallattvare ente janam ennum priyayallatt valle priyennum njan villikyum .
ningall ente janamallennu avarodu parranj idattill avar jiivanulldaivattinte makyll ennu villikyppedum " ennu hosheyapusatkattilum arullicheeyaunnuvalela .

aakayall nam entu parrayendu ? niitiye pintudaratt jatikall niiti prapichau , vishasattalullniiti tanne .
niitiyude prmannam pintudannar yisrayelo aprmannattikkll ettiyillal .

" ita , njan siiyonill idachaarkyllum tadangall parrayum vekyunnu ; avanill vishsikyunnavan lichau pokyillal "
sahodaranmare , avar rakshikyppedennam ennu tanne ente hradayavancchayum avakyru vendi daivattodullyachanayum aakunnu .
avar parinjanaprkaramalelkkilum daivatte sambandi chau erivullavar ennu njan avakyru sakshaym parrayunnu .

hradayam kondu niitikyayi vishsikyyum vayi kondu rakshekyayi eettuparrakayum cheyaunnu .

yehoodan ennum yavanan ennum vaytayasamilla ; ellavakyrum kattravu oruvan tanne ; avan tanne villichaapekshikyunnellavakyrum nalkuvantakyvannm sambannan aakunnu .

aakayall vishasam kellviyalum kellvi krisatuvinte vachanattalum varunnu .

ennall yisrayell grhichaillayo ennu njan chodikyu nnu . " janamallattvarekyondu njan ningallkyu erivu varuttum ; mooddhajatiyekyondu ningallkyu kopam jani ppikyum " ennu onnamatu moshe parrayunnu .
yeshayaavo : " enne anevkshikyattvar enne kande tti ; enne chodikyattvakyru njan prtaykshanayi " ennu dhaiyaarttode parrayunnu .
yisrayelinekyurrichee " anusarikyatttum marruttu parrayunnatumayjanattikklekyu njan idavidate kai niidti " ennu avan parrayunnu .
ennall daivam sjanatte tallikyllanjuvo ennu njan chodikyunnu . oru nallum illa ; njanum yisraye laynalela ; abrahaminte santatiyill benayamiin gotrttill janichaavan tanne .
daivam munnarrinjidtulltante janatte tallikyllanjidtilla . eeliiyavinte charitrttill tiruvejhyuttu parrayunnatu arriyunnillayo ?

angane i kalattilum krapayalulltiranjeduppin prkaram oru shekshippundu .

aakayall entu ? yisrayell tan tiranjtu prapichailla ; tiranjedukyppedtvar atu prapichau ; shekshamullavaro katthinappedtirikyunnu .

avarude kannu kannatavannm irundu pokadte ; avarude mutuku ellayepajhyum kuniyikyenname " ennu daviidum parrayunnu .
ennall avar viijhyendatinno idarriyatu ennu njan chodikyunnu . orunallum alla ; avakyru erivu varuttuvan avarude lamghanam hetuvayi jatikallkyu rakshvannu enneyullu .
ennall avarude lamghanam lokattinnu dhanavum avarude nashtam jatikallkyu sambattum varuvan karannamayi ekkill avarude yathasthanam etr adhikam ?
ennall jatikallayningallodu njan parrayunnatu : jatikallude apposatlanayirikyyall
njan ente sjatikyakyru vallavidhenayum spaddhr janippichau , avarill chilare rakshikyamekkilo ennu vechau tanne njan ente shushrookshaye pukajhyttunnu .
avarude bhrmsham lokattinte nirappinnu hetuvayi ekkill avarude amgiikarannam marichaavarude uyippernnallate entakum ?
aaday bhagam vishuddhm ekkill pindm mujhyuvanum angane tanne ; ver vishuddhm ekkill kombukallum angane tanne .
kombukallill chilatu odichaidtu kadtoliivayninne avayude idayill odtichau chettru oliivu marattinte phalaprdamayverinnu pakkalliyayittiinnur ekkilo ,
kombukallude nere prshamsikyrutu ; prshamsikyunnu vekkill nii verine allver ninneyaretchumakyunnu ennu oakyr .

avishasattill nilanilkyanjall avareyum koode odtikyum ; avare viindum odtippan daivam shtanalela .

suvisheksham sambandichau avar ningall nimittm shatrukyll ; tiranjeduppu sambandicheepitakynmar nimittm priyanmar .
daivam tante krapavarangalleyum villiyeyum kurrichau anutapikyunnillalela .
ningall mube daivatte anusarikyatirunnidtu avarude anusarannakyedinall ippoll karunnlabhichaatu pole ,
ningallkyu labhichakarunnayall avakyru karunnlabhikyendtinnu avarum ippoll anusarikyatirikyunnu .
daivam ellavarodum karunncheyeendatinnu ellavareyum anusarannakyedill adechau kallanju .
ha , daivattinte dhanam , njanam , arrivu ennivayude aajhyame ! avante nayayvidhikall etr aprmeyavum avante vajhyikall etr agocharavum aakunnu .
kattravinte manassu arrinjvan aar ? avannu mantriyayirunnavan aar ?
avannu vallatum mube koduttidtu prtiphalam vangunnavan aar ?
sakalavum avanill ninnum avanalum avakklekyum aakunnuvalela ; avannu ennekyum mahatm aamen .
sahodaranmare , njan daivattinte manasslivu opprichau ningalle prbodhippikyunnatu : ningall buddhiyullaaradhanayayi ningallude shariirangalle jiivanum vishuddhiyum daivattinnu prsadavumullyagamayi samapprippin .
i lokattinnu anuroopamakate nanmayum prsadavum poonnrtayumulldaivahitam innatennu tirichaarriyendatinnu manassu putukyi roopantarappeduvin .
bhavikyendatinnu miite bhavichauyarate daivam avanavannu vishasattinte allavu pakkidttu pole subodhamakum vannm bhavikyennamennu njan enikyu labhichakrapayall ningallill oaroruttnodum parrayunnu .
oru shariirattill namukyu palavayavangall undalela ; ellavayavangallkyum prvratti onnallatanum ;
atupole palaraynam krisatuvill oru shariiravum ellavarum tammill avayavangallum aakunnu .
aakayall namukyu labhichakrapekyu ottvannm veveerre varam ullatu kondu prvachanam ekkill vishasattinnu ottvannm ,
shushrookshekkill shushrookshayill , upadeshikyunnavan ekkill upadeshattill , prbodhippikyunnavan ekkill prbodhanattill ,
danam cheyaunnavan eekagrtayode , bharikyunnavan utsahttode , karunnacheyaunnavan prsannatayode aakadte .
senham nivayrajam aayirikydte : tiiyatine verruttu nallatinodu pattikyollvin .
sahodarapriitiyill tammill sthayipoondu bahumanikyu nnatill aneyanaym munnidtukollvin .
utsahattill maduppillate aatmavill erivullavarayi kattravine sevippin .
aashayill santokshippin ; kashtatayill sahikshnnatkannippin ;
pratthrnayill uttirippin ; vishuddhnmarude aavashayngallill koodtay kannikyyum atithisalkyaram aacharikyyum cheyvin .
ningalle upadrvikyunnavare anugrhippin ; shapikyate anugrhippin .
santokshikyunnavarodukoode santokshikyyum karayunnavarodukoode karakayum cheyvin .
tammill eekamataymullavarayi valippm bhavikyate elliyavarodu chennurkollvin ; ningallettnne buddhimanmar ennu vicharikyrutu .
aakyrum tinmekyu pakaram , tinmcheyaate sakalmanukshayrudeyum mumbill yogaymayatu munkaruti ,
kajhyiyumekkill ningallall aavollam sakalamanukshayrodum samadhanamayirippin .
priyamullavare , ningall tanne prtikaram cheyaate daivakopattinnu idam koduppin ; prtikaram enikyullatu ; njan pakaram cheyaum ennu kattravu arullicheeyaunnu , ennall
" ninte shatruvinnu vishakyunnu ekkill avannu tinman koduky ; dahikyunnu ekkill kudippan koduky ; angane cheyatall nii avante talamell tiikynall kunnikyum " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnuvalela .
tinmayodu tolkyate nanmayall tinmaye jayikyuka .
eetu manukshaynum reshakshanadhikarangallkyu kiijhyadangadte . daivttalallate oradhikaravumillalela ; ulladhikarangallo daivattall niyamikyppedtirikyunnu .
aakayall adhikarattodu marrukyunnavan daivavayvasth yodu marrukyunnu . marrukyunnavaro shikshavidhi prapikyum .
vajhyunnavar sallprvrattikylldukshprvrattikyretbhayakkram . adhikarasthne bhayappedatirippan ichchikyunnuvo ? nanmcheyk ennall avanodu puklabhikyum .
ninte nanmekyayidtlelavan daivashushrookshakyaranayi rikyunnatu . nii tinmcheyatalo bhayappeduka ; verrute allavan vall vahikyunnatu ; avan doksham prvattrikyunnavante shikshekyayi prtikariyaydaivashushrookshakyaran tanne .
atu kondu shikshaye matrmallmanassakshiyeyum vicharichau kiijhyadangukaavashaym .
atukondu ningall nikutiyum kodukyunnu . avar daivshushrookshakanmarum akayaarm tanne nokyunnavaru makunnu .
ellavakyrum kadamayullatu koduppin ; nikuti kodukye ndavannu nikuti ; chukkm kodukyendavannu chukkm ; bhayam kannikyendavannu bhayam ; manam kannikyendavannu manam .
aneyanaym senhikyunnatu allate aarodum onnum kadbedtirikyrutu ; anayne senhikyunnavan nayayaprmannam nivattrichairikyunnuvalela .
vaybhicharam cheyaarutu , kulcheyaarutu , moshtikyrutu , mohikyrutu ennullatum mattu eetu kalpanayum koodtukarane ninneppole senhiky ennii vachanattill samkshepichai rikyunnu .
senham koodtukarannu doksham prvattrikyunnilla ; aakayall senham nayayaprmannattinte nivratti tanne .
itu cheyeendatu urrakyttill ninnu unnaruvan najhyikvannirikyunnu enningane ningall samayatte arrikayall tanne ; nam vishsichasamayattekyall rakshippoll namukyu adhikam aduttirikyunnu .
ratri kajhyivarrayi pakall aduttirikyunnu ; atukondu nam irudtinte prvrattikalle vechaukallanju vellichaatti nte aayudhavaggrm dharichau kollka .
pakall samayattu ennpole nam mayaaradayayi nadaky ; verrikyoottukallilum madaypanangallilumalla , shayanmohangllilum dukshkyamangallilumalla , pinnakyttilum asooyayilu mallal .
kattravayyeshukrisatuvinettnne dharichaukollvin . mohangall janikyumarru jaddattinnayi chintikyrutu .
samshayvicharangalle vidhikyate vishasattill balahiinnayavane chettru kollvin .
oruvan ellam tinnamennu vishsikyunnu ; balahiinano sasayadikalle tinnunnu .
tinnunnavan tinnattvane dhikyrikyrutu ; tinnattvan tinnunnavane vidhikyrutu ; daivam avane kaikyondiri kyunnuvalela .
mattoruttnte dasane vidhippan nii aar ? avan nilkyunnato viijhyunnato sntayajamanannareta ; avan nilkyum tanum ; avane nilkyumarrakyuvan kattravinnu kajhyiyumalela .
oruvan oru divasattekyall mattoru divasatte manikyu nnu ; verroruvan sakaldivasangalleyum manikyunnu ; ororuttn tantante manassill urrechairikydte .
divasatte aadarikyunnavan kattravinnayi aadarikyunnu ; tinnunnavan kattravinnayi tinnunnu ; avan daivatte satutikyunnuvalela ; tinnattvan kattravinnayi tinnatirikyunnu ; avanum daivatte satutikyunnu .
nammill aarum tanikyayi tanne jiivikyunnilla ; aarum tanikyayi tanne marikyunnatumillal .
jiivikyunnu ekkill nam kattravinnayi jiivikyunnu ; marikyunnu ekkill kattravinnayi marikyunnu ; atu kondu jiivikyunnu ekkilum marikyunnu ekkilum nam kattravinnu llavar tanne .
marichaavakyrum jiivichairikyunnavakyrum kattravu aakendati nnalelkrisatu marikyyum uyikyryum cheyattu .
ennall nii sahodarane vidhikyunnatu entu ? alla , nii sahodarane dhikyrikyunnatu entu ? nam ellavarum daivattinte nayayasanattinnu mumbake nilkyendi varum .
" ennannente mumbill ellmujhyakkalum madangum , ellnavum daivatte satutikyum ennu kattravu arullicheeyau nnu " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnuvalela .
aakayall nammill oaroruttn daivattodu kannakyu bodhippikyendivarum .
atu kondu nam ini aneyanaym vidhikyrutu ; sahodarannu idachaaryo tadangalo vekyatirippan matrm urrechaukollvin .
yatonnum stave malinamallennu njan kattravayyeshuvill arrinjum urrechaumirikyunnu . vallatum malinam ennu ennunnavannu matrm atu malinam aakunnu .
ninte bhakshannam nimittm sahodarane vaysanippichaall nii senhaprkaram nadakyunnilla . aakyruvendi krisatu marichauvo avane ninte bhakshannam kondu nashippikyrutu .
ningallude nanmekyu dookshannam varuttrutu .
daivarajaym bhakshannavum paniiyavumalla , niitiyum samadhanavum parishuddhavill santokshavum areta .
atill krisatuvine sevikyunnavan daivatte prsadi ppikyunnavanum manukshaykyru kollakunnavanum tanne .
aakayall nam samadhanattinnum aneyanaym aatmikvaddhrnekyum ullatinnu shrmichau kollka .
bhakshannam nimittm daivanimmrannatte ajhyikyrutu . ellam shuddhm tanne ; ekkilum idachaar varuttumarru tinnunnmanukshaynnu atu dokshamareta .
mamsam tinnateyum viinju kudikyateyum sahodarannu idachaar varuttunnyatonnum cheyaateyum irikyunnatu nallatu .
ninakyullvishasam daivasannidhiyill ninakyu tanne irikydte ; tan siikarikyunnatill tannettan vidhikyttvan bhagayvan .
ennall samshayikyunnavan tinnunnu ekkill atu vishasattill ninnu utbhavikyaykakondu avan kuttkyaranayirikyunnu . vishasattill ninnu utbhavikyatttokyeyum papamareta .
ennall shtaraynam ashtarude balahiinatakalle chumakyukayum nammill tanne prsadikyatirikyyum vennam .
nammill oaroruttn koodtukarane nanmekyayidtu aatmikvaddhrnekyu vendi prsadippikyennam
" ninne nindikyunnavarude nind ente mell viinnu " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnatu pole krisatuvum tannill tanne prsadichaillal .
ennall munnejhyutiyirikyunnatu okyeyum nammude upadeshattinnayidtu , namukyu tiruvejhyuttukallall ullavakyunnsthiratayalum aashasattalum prtayashundakendatinnu tanne ejhyutiyirikyunnu .
ennall ningall eekamatayppedtu , nammude kattravaysheukrisatuvinte pitavaydaivatte eekmanassode oru vayinall mahatiikarikyendatinnu
sthiratayum aashasavum nalkunndaivam ningallkyu krisatuyeshuvinnu anuroopamayi tammill eekchintayodi rippan krapnalkumarrakadte .
atukondu krisatu daivattinte mahatttinnayi ningalle kaikyondatu pole ningallum aneyanaym kaikyollvin .
pitakynmakyru labhichavagdattngalle urrappikyendatinnu
krisatu daivattinte sataym nimittm pariedanekyu shushrookshakyaranayittiinnaru ennum jatikall daivatte avante karunnnimittm mahatiikarikyennam ennum njan parrayunnu .
" atukondu njan jatikallude idayill ninne vajhytti ninte namattinnu satuti padum "
ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnuvalela . mattoredattu : " jatikalle , avante janattodu onnichau aanandippin " ennum parrayu nnu . " sakaljatikallumayullore , kattravine satutippi n , sakalvamshangallum avane satutikydte " ennum parrayu nnu .
" yishyiyude verum jatikalle bharippan ejhyunnelkyu nnavanumayavan undakum ; avanill jatikall prtayashvekyum "
ennu yeshayaavu parrayunnu . ennall prtayashnalkunndaivam parishuddhatmavinte shtiyall ningall prtayashyill samraddhiyullavarayi vishsikyunnatilullsakalsantokshavum samadhanavum kondu ningalle nirrekyu marrakadte .
sahodaranmare , ningall tanne dayapoonnrrum sakalnjanavum nirranjvarum aneyanaym prbodhippippan prapatrum aakunnu ennu njan ningallekyurrichau urrechairi kyunnu .
ekkilum jatikall ennvajhyipadu parishuddhatmavinall vishuddhiikarikyppedtu prsadakaramayittiiruvan njan daivattinte suvishekshaghokshannam purohitanayi anukshanichau kondu jatikallill krisatuyeshuvinte shushrookshakanayirikyendatinnu
daivam enikyu nalkiykrapnimittm ningalle oammr ppeduttum vannm njan chiledattu atidhaiyaarmayi ningallkyu ejhyutiyirikyunnu .
krisatuyeshuvill enikyu daivasambandmayi prshamsundu .
krusatu njan mukhantaram jatikallude anusarannattinnayi dtu vachanattalum prvrattiyalum adayallangalludeyum atbhutangalludeyum shtikondum parishuddhatmavinte shtikondum prvattrichaatu allate mattonnum mindu van njan tuniyukayillal .
angane njan yerooshalem mutall illuyaardeshattollam chutti sanchrichau krisatuvinte suvishekshaghokshannam poorippichairikyunnu .
njan mattoruvante adisthanattinmell panniyatirikye ndatinnu krisatuvinte namam arrinjidtullidattilallal ,
" avanekyurrichau arrivu kidtiidtillattvar kannum ; kedtidtillattvar grhikyum " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnatu pole areta , suvisheksham arriyippan abhimanikyunnatu .
atukondu tanne njan ningallude adukyll varunnatinnu palappojhyum mudakym vannu .
ippojhyo enikyu i dikyukallill ini sthlamillaykyalum angodtu varuvan aneksamvramayi vanchundakakondum ,
njan spanayyilekyu yatr cheyauboll pokunnvajhyikyu ningalle kanmanum aadaym ningalle kandu santokshichasheksham ningallall yatr ayakyppeduvanum aashikyunnu .
ippojhyo njan vishuddhnmakyru shushrookshcheyvan yerooshalemilekyu yatryakunnu .
yerooshalemile vishuddhnmarill daridrrayavakyru eetanum dhammerapakaram cheyvan makyedonayyilum akhayayilum ullavakyru ishtam tonni .
avakyru ishtam tonni ennu matrmalla , atu avakyru kadavum aakunnu ; jatikall avarude aatmikananmakallill koodtallikall aayekkill eehikananmakallill avakyru shashrookshcheyvan kadabedtirikyunnuvalela .
njan atu nivattrichau i phalam avakyru eelpichau boddhym varuttiyasheksham ningallude vajhyiyayi spanayyilekyu pokum .
njan ningallude adukyll varuboll krisatuvinte anugrhapoottriiyode varum ennu njan arriyunnu .
ingane njan daiveshtattall santokshattode ningallude adukyll vannu ningallodukoode manam tannukyendatinnum ningall enikyu vengi daivattodullpratthrnayill ennodukoode poradennam ennu
nammude kattravayyeshukrisatuvineyum aatmavinte senhatteyum oapprichau njan ningalle prbodhippikyu nnu .
samadhanattinte daivam ningallellavarodum koode irikyumarrakadte . aamen .
nammude sahodariyum kemrekayasabhayile shashrookshakyarttiyumayphebaye
ningall vishuddhnmakyru yogaymam vannm kattravinte namattill kaikyondu , avallkyu ningallude sahayam vendunneetu kayaarttilum sahayikyendatinnu njan ningalle bharamelpikyunnu . avallum palakyrum vishekshall enikyum sahayam cheyatirikyunnu .
krisatuyeshuvill ente koodtu velakyaraypriskayeyum akilaveyum vandnam cheyvin .
avar ente prannannu vendi tangallude kajhyuttu vechau koduttvarakunnu ; avakyru njan matrmalla , jatikallude sakalasabhakallum koode nandi parrayunnu .
avarude viidtile sabhayeyum vandnam cheyvin ; aasayyi ll krisatuvinnu aadayphalamayi enikyu priyanayeppai nattosinnu vandnam cholluvin .
ningallkyayi vallare addhvanichaavallaymarriyekyu vandnam cholluvin .
ente chachaarkyarum sahabaddhnmarayarentanikyosi nnum yooniyavinnum vandnam cholluvin ; avar apposat tlanmarude idayill perkondavarum enikyu mube krisatuvill vishsichaavarum aakunnu .
kattravill enikyu priyanayamlpiyattosinnu vand nam cholluvin .
krisatuvill njangallude koodtu velakyaranayubaaranosi nnum enikyu priyanaysatakyuvinnum vandnam cholluvin .
krisatvill sammtanayappelesinnu vandnam cholluvi n . arisetaboolosinte bhavanakyakyru vandnam cholluvi n .
ente chachaarkyaranayherodiyonnu vandnam cholluvi n ; nakyrissosinte bhavanakyarill kattravill vishsichaavkyru vandnam cholluvin .
kattravill addhvanikyunnavaraytruphainekyum truphosekyum vandnam cholluvin . kattravill vallare addhvanichaavallaypriypesarisinnu vandnam cholluvin .
kattravill prsiddhnayroophosineyum enikyum amm yayavante ammyeyum vandnam cheyvin .
asumkritosinnum pelgonnum hemmerasinnum paretbasinnum hemmrasinnum koodeyullsahodaranmakyrum vandnam cholluvin .
philologosinnum yooliyekyum nereyusinnum avnte sahodarikyum olumbasinnum avarodukoodeyullsakalvishuddhnmakyrum vandnam cholluvin .
vishuddh chumbanam kondu aneyanaym vandnam cheyvin . krisatuvinte sakalsabhakallum ningalle vandnam cheyaunnu .
sahodaranmare , ningall patthichupadeshattinnu vipariitamydndvpakshangalleyum idachaarkalleyum undakyunnavare sookshichau kollennamennu njan ningalle prbodhippi kyunnu . avarodu akannu marruvin .
anganeyullavar nammude kattravaykrisatuvine alla , tangallude vayattineyaretsevikyyum chakyravakyum mukhsatutiyum parranju sadhukyllude hradayangalle vanchichau kallakayum cheyaunnu .
ningallude anusarannam parakye ellavakyrum prsiddhmayi rikyunnu ; atu kondu njan ningall nimittm santokshikyunnu ; ekkilum ningall nanmekyu njanikallum tinmekyu nmarum aakennam ennu njan ichchikyunnu .
samadhanattinte daivamo vegattill sattane ningllude kalkyiijhye chatechau kallayum . nammude kattravayyeshukrisatuvinte krapningallodu koode irikyumarrkadte .
ente koodtu velakyaranaytimotheyosum ente chachaarkyaraylookeyasum yasonum sosiparetasum ningalle vandnam cheyaunnu .
i lekhanam ejhyutiyteteras ennnjan ningalle kattravill vandnam cheyaunnu .
enikyum savaarsabhekyum atithisalkyaram cheyaunngayos ningalle vandnam cheyaunnu . padtnnattinte bhandaravicharakanayerasetasum sahodaranayktterasum ningalle vandnam cheyaunnu .
poovaarkalangallill marranjirunnidtu ippoll vellippedtu vanntum nitaydaivattinte niyogaprkaram sakalajatikall kyum vishasattinte anusarannattinnayi prvachakanmaru de ejhyuttukallall
arriyichairikyunnatumaymammrttinte vellippadinnu anusrannamayullente suvishekshattinnum yeshukrisatuvine kyurrichaullprsamgattinnum ottvannm ningalle sthirappe duttuvan kajhyiyunn
eekaniyaydaivattinnu yeshukrisatu mukhantaram ennennekyum mahatm undakumarrakadte . aamen .

daiveshtattall yeshukrisatuvinte apposatlanayi villikyppedt pelosum sahodaranaysosetnesum korintilulldaivasabhekyu ,
krisatuyeshuvill vishuddhiikarikyppedtvarum avideyum ivi deyum evideyum nammude kattravayyeshukrisatuvinte namatte villichaapekshikyunneevarodum koode villikyppe dt vishuddhnmarumayavakyru tanne , ejhyutunnatu ;
nammude pitavaydaivattikkll ninnum kattravayyeshukrisatuvikkll ninnum ningallkyu krapayum samadhanvum undakadte .
ningallkyu krisatuyeshuvill nalkappedt daivakrapnimittm njan ente daivattinnu ningalle kyurrichau eppojhyum setatrm cheyaunnu .
krisatuvinte sakshaym ningallill urrappayirikyunnatu pole
avanill ningall sakalattilum vishekshall sakalvachanttilum sakalparinjanattilum sambannarayittiinnaru .
ingane ningall oru krapavarattilum kurravillattvarayi nammude kattravayyeshukrisatuvinte prtaykshatkatti rikyunnu .
nammude kattravayyeshukrisatuvinte nallill kuttmillattvarayirikyendatinnu avan ningalle avasanattollam urrappikyum .
tante putrnum nammude kattravayyeshukrisatuvinte koodtayyilekyu ningalle villichairikyunndaivam vishsatn .
sahodaranmare , ningall ellavarum onnu tanne samsari kyyum ningallude idayill bhinnatbhavikyate eekamanassilum eekabhiprayattilum yojichairikyyum vennam ennu njan ningalle nammude kattravayyeshukrisatuvinte namam cholli prbodhippikyunnu .
sahodaranmare , ningallude idayill pinnakym undennu kelavayude aallukallall enikyu arrivu kidtiyirikyunnu .
ningallill oaroruttn : njan pelosinte pakshakyran , njan appolelasinte pakshakyaran , njan kephvinte pakshakyaran njan krisatuvinte pakshakyaran enni ngane parrayunnu poll .
krisatu vibhagikyppedtirikyunnuvo ? pelos ningall kyu vendi krooshikyppedtuvo ? alla , pelosinte namattill ningall sanam eettuvo ?
ente namattill njan sanam kajhyippichau ennu aarum parrayatavannm
krisepasineyum gayosineyum ojhyike ningallill aareyum njan sanam kajhyippikyaykayall njan daivattinnu setatrm cheyaunnu .
setphanasinte bhavanakyareyum njan sanam kajhyippichau ; atallate mattu vallavareyum sanam kajhyippichauvo ennu njan oakyrunnillal .
sanam kajhyippippan allsuvisheksham arriyippanaretkrisatu enne ayachaatu ; krisatuvinte krooshu vaytthrmakati rikyendatinnu vakchatuyaarttode allatanum .
krooshinte vachanam nashichau pokunnavakyru bhokshatvum rakshikyppedunnnamukyo daivshtiyum aakunnu .
" njanikallude njanam njan nashippkyyum buddhimanmrude buddhi dubaarlamakyukayum cheyaum " ennu ejhyutiyiri kyunnuvalela .
njani evide ? shasrti evide ? i lokattile takyrikan evide ? lokattinte njanam daivam bhokshatmakyiyillayo ?
daivattinte njanattill lokam njanattall daivtte arriyaykkondu vishsikyunnavare prsamgatti nte bhokshatttall rakshippan daivattinnu prsadam tonni .
yehoodanmar adayallam chodikyyum yavananmar njanam anevkshikyyum cheyaunnu ;
njangallo krooshikyppedt krisatuvine prsamgikyunnu ; yehoodanmakyru idachaaryum jatikallkyu bhokshatvu
mekkilum yehoodanmarakadte yavananmarakadte villikyppedt eevakyrum daivashtiyum daivanavumaykrisatuvine tanne .
daivattinte bhokshatm manukshayrekyall njanamerriyatum daivattinte balahiinatmanukshayrekyall balamerriyatum aakunnu .
sahodaranmare , ningallude villiye nokyuvin : lokbhi prayaprkaram njanikall eerreyilla , balavanmar eerre yilla , kuliinanmarum eerreyilla .
njanikalle lippippan daivam lokattill bhokshat mayatu tiranjeduttu ; balamullatine lippippan daivam lokattill balahiinamayatu tiranjeduttu .
ullatine illayyakyuvan daivam lokattill kulahii navum nikrashtavumayatum eetumillatttum tiranjeduttu ;
daivasannidhiyill oru jaddavum prshamsikyatirikyendati nnu tanne .

" daivam tanne senhikyunnavakyru orukyiidtullatu kannu kandidtilla , chevi kedtidtilla , oru manukshaynteyum hradayatti ll tonniidtumilla " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnatu pole tanne .
namukyo daivam tante aatmavinall vellippeduttiyiri kyunnu ; aatmavu sakalatteyum daivattinte aajhyangalle yum aarayunnu .

ningallude idayill iksharyyum pinnakyvum irikye , ningall jaddikanmarum sheksham manukshayreppole nadakyunnvarumallayo ?
oruttn : njan pelosinte pakshakyaran ennum mattoruttn : njan appolelasinte pakshakyaran ennum parrayuboll ningall sadharannamanukshayrallayo ?

njangall daivattinte koodtu velakyar ; ningall daivatti nte krakshi , daivattinte grahanimmrannam .

yeshukrisatu ennidtirikyunnadisthanamallate mattonnu iduvan aakyrum kajhyikayillal .

adushtane ningallude idayill ninnu niikyikyllavin .

alla , ningall anayayam cheykayum nashtam varuttukayum cheyaunnu ; atum sahodaranmakyru tanne .
anayayam cheyaunnavar daivarajaym avakashamakyukayillennu arriyunnillayo ? ningallettnne vanchikyatirippi n ; dunnardappukar , vigrharadhikall , vaybhicharikall , sybhogikall , purukshakamikall ,
kallanmar , atayagrhikall , madaypanmar , vavikshanannakyar , pidichauparrikyar , ennivar daivarajaym avakashamakyukyillal .

bhayaar bhattravine verrupiriyarutu ; pirinju ennu varikilo vivaham koodate pakyernnam ; alelnnu varikill bhattravodu nirannu kollennam ; bhattravu bhayaarye upekshikyyumarutu .
ennall shekshamullavarodu kattravallnjan tanne parrayunnatu : oru sahodarannu avishasiyaybhayaar undayirikyyum avall avanodu koode pappran sammtikyyum cheyatall avalle upekshikyrutu .
avishasiyaybhattravulloru satiiyum , avan avallodu koode pappran sammtikyunnu ekkill , bhattravine upekshikyrutu .
avishasiyaybhattravu bhayaar mukhantaram vishuddhiikariky ppedtum avishasiyaybhayaar sahodaran mukhantaram vishuddhiikarikyppedtumirikyunnu ; alelkkill ningallude makyll ashuddhr ennu varum ; ippojhyo avar vishuddhr aakunnu .

alla , kevalam namukyu vendi parrayunnato ? ate , ujhyunnavan aashayode ujhyukayum metikyunnavan patam kidtum ennullaashayode metikyyum vendatakayall namukyu vendi ejhyutiyirikyunnatareta .
njangall aatmikamayatu ningallkyu vitechaidtu ningallude eehikamayatu koyatall valiykayaarmo ?

daivalayakammrngall nadattunnavar daivalayam kondu upajiivikyunnu ennum yagapiitthattikkll shushrookshcheyaunnvar yagapiitthattile vajhyipadukallill oaharikyar aakunnu ennum ningall arriyunnillayo ?
atu pole kattravum suvisheksham arriyikyunnavar suvishekshattall upajiivikyennam ennu kalpichairikyunnu .
ekkilum itu onnum njan pryogichaidtilla ; ingane enikyu kidtennam ennu vechau njan itu ejhyutunnatum alla ; aarekkilum ente prshamsvrathavakyunnatine kyall mariky tanne enikyu nallatu .
njan suvisheksham arriyikyunnu ekkill enikyu prshamsi ppan onnumilla . nibaarndm ente mell kidakyunnu . njan suvisheksham arriyikyunnillekkill enikyu ayeekashtam !
njan atu manpoovaarm nadattunnu ekkill enikyu prtiphlam undu ; manpoovaarmalelkkilum kayaarm ekkll bharamelpichairi kyunnu .
ennall ente prtiphalam entu ? suvisheksham arriyi kyumboll suvishekshghokshannattilulladhikaram mujhyuvanum upayogikyate njan suvishekshaghokshannam chelavu koodate nadattunnatu tanne .
ingane njan kevalam stantrn ekkilum adhikam pere nedendatinnu njan ennettnne ellavakyrum dasanakyi .

itu namukyu drashtantamayi sambhavichau ; avar mohichaatu pole namum dummerahikall aakatirikyendatinnu tanne .
" janam ninnuvanum kudippanum irunnu , kallippan ejhyunne ttu " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnprkaram avarill chilare ppole ningall vigrharadhikall aakarutu .
avarill chilar parasamgam cheyatu oru divasattill irupattumoovayiram per viinnu poyatu pole nam parasamgam cheyaarutu .
avarill chilar pariikshichau sapprngallall nashichau poyatu pole nam kattravine pariikshikyrutu .
avarill chilar pirrupirruttu samhariyall nashichau poyatu pole ningall pirrupirrukyyumarutu .
itu drashtantamayidtu avakyru sambhavichau , lokavasanam vannettiyirikyunnnamukyu buddhyupadeshattinnayi ejhyutiyumirikyunnu .
aakayall tan nilkyunnu ennu tonnunnavan viijhyatiri ppan nokyikyolladte .

atu kondu priyanmare , vigrharadhanvidtoduvin :
ningall vivekikall ennu vechau njan parrayunnu ; njan parrayunnatu vivechippin .

alla , jatikall balikajhyikyunnatu daivattinnallbhootangllkyu kajhyikyunnu ennareta ; ennall ningall bhootangallude koodtallikall aakuvan enikyu manassillal .

sakalattinnum enikyu kattrvaym undu ; ekkilum sakalavum pryojanamullatalla . sakalattinnum enikyu kattrvaym undu ; ekkilum sakalavum aatmikvaddhrnvaruttunnilla .
ororuttn sntgunnamalla , mattullavante gunnam anevkshi kydte .
angadiyill vilkyunnatu entekkilum manassakshi nimittm onnum anevkshannam kajhyikyate tinnuvin .
bhoomiyum atinte poonnrtayum kattravinnullatalela .

aakayall ningall tinnalum kudichaalum entu cheyatalum ellam daivattinte mahatttinnayi cheyvin .
yehoodanmakyrum yavananmakyrum daivasabhekyum idachaaryallatt varakuvin .
njanum ente gunnamalla , palar rakshikyppendetinnu avrude gunnam tanne anevkshichau kondu ellavareyum e llam kondum prsadippikyunnuvalela .
njan krisatuvinte anukariyayirikyunnatu pole ningallum ente anukarikall aakuvin .
ningall sakalattilum enne oakyrukayum njan ningalle eelpichakalpanakalle prmannikyyum cheyatall ningalle pukajhyttunnu .
ennall eetu purukshanteyum talkrisatu , srtiiyude talpurukshan , krisatuvinte taldaivam ennu ningall arriyennam ennu njan aagrhikyunnu .
moodupadam idtu pratthrikyyo prvachikyyo cheyaunneetu purukshanum tante talaye apamanikyunnu .
moodupadamillate pratthirkyyo prvachikyyo cheyaunneetu srtiiyum tante talaye apamanikyunnu ; atu avall ksheram cheyaichaatu poleyalela .
srtii moodupadamidunnilelkkill mudi katrichau kallayadte . katrikyu nnato ksheram cheyaikyunnato srtiikyu lyekkill moodupadam idtukolladte .
purukshan daivattinte prtimayum tejassum aakayall moodupadam idendatalla . srtiiyo purukshante tejas aaku nnu .
purukshan srtiiyill ninnallalelsrtii purukshanill ninnaretundayatu .
purukshan srtiikyayidtllsrtii purukshannayidtlelsrashtiky ppedttu .
aakayall srtiikyu dootanmar nimittm talamell adhiinatlakshaym undayirikyennam .
ennall kattravill purukshane koodute srtiiyumillsrtiiye koodate purukshanumilla .
srtii purukshanill ninnu undayatu pole purukshanum srtii mukhantaram ullavakunnu ; ennall sakalattinnum daivam karannabhootan .
ningall tanne vidhippin ; srtii moodupadam idate daivttodu pratthrikyunnatu yogaymo ?
purukshan mudi niidtiyall atu avannu apamanam ennum
srtii mudi niidtiyalo atu moodupadattinnu pakaram nalkiyiriky kondu avallkyu manam aakunnu ennum prkrati tanne ningalle patthippikyunnillayo ?

bhakshannam kajhyikyyill oaroruttn tantante attajhyam mube kajhyikyunnu . angane oruvan vishannum mattoruvan laharipidichaum irikyunnu .

avaannm tanne attajhyam kajhyinjsheksham avan panaptrvum eduttu ; i panapatrm ente rtattill puti yaniyamam aakunnu ; itu kudikyumbojhyokyeyum ente oammrkyayi cheyvin ennu parranju .
angane ningall i appm tinnukayum panapatrm kudikyyum cheyaubojhyokyeyum kattravu varuvollam avante marannatte prsatavikyunnu .
atu kondu ayogaymayi appm tinnukayo kattravinte panapatrm kudikyyo cheyaunnavan ellam kattravinte shariiravum rtavum sambandichau kuttkyaran aakum .
manukshayn tannettan shodhancheyatidtu vennam i appm tinnukayum panapatrttill ninnu kudikyyum cheyvan .
tinnukayum kudikyyum cheyaunnavan shariiratte vivechikynjall tanikyu shikshavidhi tinnukayum kudikyyum cheyau nnu .
itu hetuvayi ningallill palarum balahiinarum rogikllum aakunnu ; anekarum nidrkollunnu .
nam nammettnne vidhichaall vidhikyppedukayilla .
vidhikyppedunnu ekkilo nam lokattodukoode shikshvidhiyill akappedatirikyendatinnu kattravu namme blashikshkajhyikyyakunnu .
aakayall sahodaranmare , ningall bhakshannam kajhyippan kooduboll aneyanaym kattirippin .
vallavannum vishakyunnu ekkill ningall orumichau koodunnatu nayayvidhikyu hetuvakatirikyendatinnu avan viidtill vechau bhakshannam kajhyikydte , sheksham kayaarngalle njan vannidtu krmappeduttum .
sahodaranmare , aatmikavarangalle kyurrichau ningallkyu arrivillatirikyrutu ennu njan aagrhikyunnu .
ningall jatikall aayirunnappoll ningalle nadattiyatu pole umavigrhangallude adukyll pokpativayiru nnu ennu ningall arriyunnuvalela .
aakayall daivatmavill samsarikyunnavan aarum yeshu shapikyppedtvan ennu parrakayilla ; parishuddhatmavill allate yeshu kattravu ennu parravan aakyrum kajhyikayu millennu njan ningalle grhippikyunnu .
ennall krapavarangallill vaytayasam undu ;
aatmavu onnareta . shushrookshakallill vaytayasam undu ;
kattravu oruvan . viiyaar prvrattikallill vaytayasam undu ; ekkilum ellavarilum ellam prvattrikyunndaivam oruvan tanne .
ennall oaroruttnnu aatmavinte prkashanam potu pryojanattinnayi nalkappedunnu .
oruttnnu aatmavinall njanattinte vachanavum mattoruttnnu ate aatmavinall parijjanattinte vachanavum nalkappedunnu ;
verroruttnnu ate aatmavinall vishasam , mattoru vannu ate aatmavinall rogashantikallude varam ;
mattoruvannu viiyaarprvrattikall ; mattoruvannu prvachanam ; mattoruvannu aatmakyllude vivechanam ; verroruvannu palavidhbhakshakall ; mattoruvannu bhakshakallude vayakhayanam .
ennall itu ellam prvattrikyunnatu tan ichchikyum pole avanavannu atatu varam pakuttu kodukyunnore aatmavu tanne .
shariiram onnum , atinnu avayavam palatum shariirattinte avayavam palatayirikye ellam oru shariiravum aayirikyunnatu pole aakunnu krisatuvum .
yehoodanmaro yavananmaro dasanmaro stantrro nam ellavarum eekshariiramakumarru ore aatmavill sanam eettum ellavarum ore aatmavine panam cheyatumirikyunnu .
shariiram oru avayavamallpalatareta .
njan kai allaykakondu shariirattilullatallennu kall parrayunnu ekkill atinall atu shariirattilullatallennu varikayilla .
njan kannu allaykakondu shariirattilullatallennu chevi parrayunnu ekkill atinall atu shariirattilulltallennum varikayilla .
shariiram mujhyuvan kannayall shrvannam evide ? mujhyuvan shrvannam aayall ghrannam evide ?
daivamo tante ishtaprkaram avayavangalle shariirattill vekhavaarrayvechairikyunnu .
sakalavum oru avayavam ekkill shariiram evide ?
ennall avayavangall palatekkilum shariiram onnu tanne .
kanninnu kayeeadu : ninne kyondu enikyu aavashaymillennum talekyu kalukallodu : ningallekyondu enikyu aavashaymillennum parranjukooda .
shariirattill balam kurranjvennu tonnunnavayavangall tanne aavashaymullavayakunnu .
shariirattill manam kurranjvennu tonnunnavekyu nam adhikam manam anniyikyunnu ; nammill ajhyaku kurranjve kyu adhikam ajhyaku varuttunnu ;
nammill ajhyakullavayavangallkyu atu aavashaymillalela .
shariirattill bhinnatvarate avayavangall aneyanaym oru pole karutendatinnayi daivam kurravullatinnu adhi kam manam koduttu kondu shariiratte koodticheettririkyu nnu .
atinall oru avayavam kashtam anubhavikyunnu ekkill avayavangall okyeyum koode kashtam anubhavikyunnu ; oru avayavattinnu manam vannall avayavangall okyeyum koode santokshikyunnu
ennall ningall krisatuvinte shariiravum , oaroruttn veveerrayi avayavangallum aakunnu .
daivam sabhayill onnamatu apposatlanmar , rangamatu prvachakanmar moonnamatu upadeshtakynmar ingane ororuttre niyamikyyum pinne viiyaarprvrattikall , rogashantikallude varam , sahayam cheyvanullvaram , paripalanavaram , vividhabhakshavaram ennivnalkukayum cheyatu .
ellavarum apposatlanmaro ? ellavarum prvachakanmro ? ellavarum upadeshtakynmaro ? ellavarum viiyaarpr vrattikall cheyaunnavaro ?
ellavakyrum rogashantikyullvaram ungo ? ellavarum anaybhakshakallill samsarikyunnuvo ?
ellavarum vayakhayanikyunnuvo ? reshakshanvarangalle vanchippin ; ini atireshakshanmayoru maggrm njan ningallkyu kannichautaram .
njan manukshayrudeyum dootanmarudeyum bhakshakallill samsarichaalum enikyu senhamillekkill njan mujhyangunnchebo chilambunnkaittallamo areta .
enikyu prvachanavaram undayidtu sakalmammrngallum sakalnjanavum grhichaalum malakalle niikyuvan taky vishasam undayalum senhamillekkill njan eetumilla .
enikyullatellam annadanam cheyatalum ente shariiram chuduvan eelpichaalum ; senham illekkill enikyu oru pryojanavum illa .
senham diigharmayi kshamikyyum daykannikyyum cheyaunnu ; senham spaddhrikyunnillal .
senham nigallikyunnilla . chiikyrunnilla ; ayogaymayi nadakyu nnilla . satthrm anevkshikyunnilla , devkshayppedunnilla , doksham kannakyidunnilla ;
aniitiyill santokshikyate satayttill santokshikyu nnu :
ellam porrukyunnu , ellam vishsikyunnu , ellam prtayashikyunnu , ellam sahikyunnu .
senham orunallum utinnaru pokayilla . prvachanavaramo , atu niingippokum ; bhakshavaramo , atu ninnupokum ; njanamo , atu niingippokum .
amshamayi matrm nam arriyunnu ; amshamayi matrm prvachikyunnu ;
poonnrmayatu varubojhyo amshamayatu niingippokum .
njan shushuvayirunnappoll shishuvineppole samsari chau , shishuvineppole chintichau , shishuvineppole niroo pichau ; purukshanayshekshamo njan shishuvinnullatu tayji chau kallanju .
ippoll nam kannadiyill kadamojhyiyayi kannunnu ; ppoll mukhamukhamayi kannum ; ippoll njan amshamayi arriyunnu ; appojhyo njan arriyappedttu pole tnne arriyum ,
aakayall vishasam , prtayasha , senham i moonnum nilanilkyunnu ; ivayill valiyato senham tanne .
senham aacharippan utsahippin ! aatmikavarangallum vishekshall prvachanavaravum vanchippin .
anaybhakshayill samsarikyunnavan manukshayrodalldaivttodaretsamsarikyunnu ; aarum tirichaarriyunnillalela ; ekkilum avan aatmavill mammrngalle samsarikyunnu .
prvachikyunnavano aatmikavaddhrnekyum prbodhanattinnum aashasattinnumayi manukshayrodu samsarikyunnu .
anaybhakshayill samsarikyunnavan tanikyutan aatmikavddhrnvaruttunnu ; prvachikyunnavan sabhekyu aatmikavaddhrnvaruttunnu .
ningall ellavarum anaybhakshakallill samsarikyennam ennum vishekshall prvachikyennam ennum njan ichchikyu nnu . anaybhakshakallill samsarikyunnavan sabhekyu aatmikvaddhrnlabhikyendatinnu vayakhayanikyunnilelkkill prvachikyu nnavan avanekyall valiyavan .
sahodaranmare , njan vellippadayidto njanamayidto prvachanamayidto upadeshamayidto ningallodu samsarikyte anaybhakshakallill samsarichau kondu ningallude adu kyll vannall ningallkyu entu pryojanam varum ?
kujhyall , viinnenningane nadam kodukyunnnijjariivsadhnangall tanneyum nadabhedam kannikyanjall utiyato miidtiyato entennu engane arriyum ?
kahallam tellivillatt nadam koduttall padekyu aar orungum ?
atu pole ningallum navukondu tellivayvakyu uchaarikyanjall samsarikyunnatu entennu engane arri yum ? ningall kattinodu samsarikyunnavar aakumalel
lokattill vividhbhakshakall anavadhi undu ; avayill onnum tellivillatttalla .
njan bhaksharriyanjall samsarikyunnavannu njan bbaarran aayirikyum ; samsarikyunnavan enikyum babaarran aayirikyum .
avaannm ningallum aatmvarangalle kyurrichau vanchayullavrakayall sabhayude aatmikvaddhrnekyayi saphalanmar aakuvan shrmippin .
atu kondu anaybhakshayill samsarikyunnavan vayakhaynvarattinnayi pratthrikydte .
njan anaybhakshayill pratthrikyunnu ekkill ente aatmvu pratthrikyunnu ; ente buddhiyo aphalamayirikyunnu .
aakayall entu ? njan aatmavu kondu pratthrikyum ; buddhi kondum pratthrikyum ; aatmavu kondu padum ; buddhi kondum padum .
alla , nii aatmavu kondu setatrm cholliyall aatmvramillattvan nii parrayunnatu tiriyatirikye ninte settrttinnu engane aamen parrayum ?
nii nannayi setatrm chollunnu sataym ; mattvannu aatmikvaddhrnvarunnillatanum .
ningallellavarilum adhikam njan anaybhakshakallill samsarikyunnatu kondu njan daivatte satutikyunnu .

mosheyude pusatkam vayikyuboll moodupadam inneyo llam avarude hradayattinmell kidakyunnu .
kattravikklekyu tiriyuboll moodupadam niingippokum .
kattravu aatmavakunnu ; kattravinte aatmavulledattu satantrym undu .
ennall moodupadam niingiymukhattu kattravinte tejassi ne kannadi pole prtibimbikyunnavarayi nam ellvarum aatmavakunnkattravinte danamayi tejassinmell tejassu prapichau ate prtimayayi roopantarappedunnu .
atu kondu njangallkyu karunnlabhichaidtu i shushrookshundakayall njangall adhaiyaarppedate
lakaramayrahasayngalle tayjichau upayam pryogi kyateyum daivvachanattill koodtu chekyrateyum sataym vellippeduttunnatinall daivasannidhiyill sakalamanukshay rudeyum manassakshikyu njangalle ttnne boddhymakyunnu .

njangallettnne alla , krisatuyeshuvine kattravu ennum njangalleyo yeshu nimittm ningallude dasanmar ennum aretnjangall prsamgikyunnatu .
irudtill ninnu vellichaam prkashikyennam ennu arullicheeyat daivam yeshukrisatuvinte mukhattilulldaivatejassinte parinjanam villangikyendatinnu njangallude hradayangallill prkashichairikyunnu .

aakayall njangall ellayepajhyum dhaiyaarppedtum shariirattill vasikyuboll okyeyum kattravinodu akannu paradeshi kall aayirikyunnu ennu arriyunnu .
kyall allvishasattalaretnjangall nadakyunnatu .

atu kondu shariirattill vasichaalum shariiram vidtalum njangall avane prsadippikyunnavar aakuvan abhimani kyunnu .
avanavan shariirattill irikyuboll cheyattu nallatakilum tiiyatakilum atinnu takyvannm prapikyendatinnu nam ellavarum krisatuvinte nayayasanattinte mumbake velli ppedendatakunnu .

njangall pinneyum njangallettnne ningallodu lshaghikyylla , hradayam nokyiidtlla , mukham nokyiidtu prshamsikyunnavrodu uttram parravan ningallkyu vakundakendatinnu njangallekyurrichau prshamsippan ningallkyu karannam tarikyaretcheyaunnatu .
njangall vivashanmar ennu varikill daivattinnum subodhamullavar ennu varikill ningallkyum aakunnu .

oruttn krisatuvilayall avan putiysrashti aakunnu ; pajhyayatu kajhyinju poyi , ita , atu pututayi tiinnariri kyunnu .

papam arriyattvane , nam avanill daivattinte niiti aakendatinnu , avan namukyu vendi papam aakyi .

du : khitarekkilum eppojhyum santokshikyunnavar ; daridrrekki lum palareyum sambannar aakyunnavar ; onnum illattvar ekkilum ellam kaivashamullavarayittnne .
allayo korintayre , njangallude vayi ningallodu turrannirikyunnu ; njangallude hradayam vishalamayirikyunnu .
njangallude ullill ningallkyu idukymilla , ningallude hradayngallill aretidukymullatu .
itinnu prtiphalamayi ningallum vishalatayullavarayirippi n ennu njan makyllodu ennpole ningallodu parryunnu .
ningall avishasikallodu innayallappinnkoodarutu ; niiti kyum adhammrttinnum tammill entoru chechaar ? vellichaattinnu irullodu entoru koodtaym ?
krisatuvinnum beliiyalinnum tammill entu poruttm ? alla , vishasikyu avishasiyumayi entu oahari ?
daivalayattinnu vigrhangallodu entu yojayta ? nam jiivanulldaivattinte aalayamalela . " njan avarill vasikyyum avarude idayill nadakyyum cheyaum ; njan avakyru daivavum avar enikyu janavum aakum " ennu daivam arullicheeyatirikyunnuvalela .
atu kondu " avarude naduvill ninnu purrappedtu vepperdtirippin ennu kattravu arullicheeyaunnu ; ashuddhmayatu onnum todarutu ; ennall njan ningalle kaikyondu
ningallkyu pitavum ningall enikyu putrnmarum putrimarum aayirikyum " ennu savaarshtanaykattravu arullicheeyaunnu .
priyamullavare , i vagdattngall namukyu ullatu kondu nam jaddhattileyum aatmavileyum sakalkanmakshavum niikyi nammettnne vedippakyi daivabhayattill vishuddhiye tikechau kollka .

ekkilum elliyavare aashsippikyunndaivam tiitosi nte varavinall njangalle aashsippichau .

njan lekhanattall ningalle du : khippichau ennu varikilum njan anutapikyunnilla ; alekhanam ningalle kurraynerattekyekkilum du : khippichau ennu kannunnatu kondu mube anutapichau ekkilum ippoll njan santokshikyu nnu ;
ningall du : khichaatinalalla , manasantarattinnayi du : khichatinall areta . ningallkyu njangallall onnilum chetam varatavannm daivahitprkaramalelningall du : khichaatu .
daivahitaprkaramulldu : kham anutapam varatt manasntaratte rakshekyayi ullavakyunnu . lokattinte du : khmo marannatte ullavakyunnu .

atu kondu njangallkyu aashasam vannirikyunnu ; njangllude aashasamojhyike tiitosinte manassinnu ningalle llavaralum tannuppu vannatu kondu avannundaysanto ksham nimittm njangall etryum adhikam santokshichau .

abraham daivattill vishsichau ; atu avannu niiti yayi kannakyidtu ennundalela .
atu kondu vishasikall aretabrahaminte makyll ennu arriyin .

angane vishasikall vishasiyayabrahaminodu koode anugrhikyppedunnu .
ennall nayayaprmannattinte prvrattiyill aashryikyunneevarum shapattin kiijhyakunnu ; nayayaprmannapusatkattill ejhyutiyirikyunnatu okyeyum cheyvan takyvannm atill nilanilkyattvan ellam shapikyppedtvan ennu ejhyuti yirikyunnuvalela .
ennall nayayaprmannattall aarum daivasannidhiyill nii tiikarikyppedunnillennatu spashtam ; " niitiman vishasttall jiivikyum " ennalelullatu .
nayanaprmannattinno vishasamallaadharamayirikyunnatu ; " atu cheyaunnavan atinall jiivikyum " ennundalela .
" marattinmell toongunnavan ellam shapikyppedtvan " ennu ejhyutiyirikyunnatu pole krisatu namukyuvendi shapamyittiinnaru . nayayaprmannattinte shapattill ninnu namme vilekyu vangi .
abrahaminte anugrham krisatuyeshuvill jatikallkyu varendatinnu nam aatmavennvagdattvikshayam vishasttall prapippan tanne .
sahodaranmare , njan manukshayrude idayill nadappulloru drashtantam parrayam : oru manukshaynte niyamam aayalum , tinnu urrappu vannasheksham aarum dubaarlamakyukayo ati nodu vallatum koodtikylpikyyo cheyaunnilla .
ennall abrahaminnum avante santatikyum vagdatt ngall labhichau ; santatikallkyum ennu anekare kyurrichaalla , ninte santatikyum ennu eekane kyurrichaaretparrayunnatu ; atu krisatutanne .
njan parrayunnatinte talpayaarmo : nanoottimupptu aandu kajhyinjidtu undaynayayaprmannam vagdatttte niikyuvn takyvannm atu daivam mumbu urrappakyiyniyamatte dubaarlamakyunnilla .
avakasham nayayaprmannattall ekkill vagdattttalallvarunnatu ; abrahaminno daivam atine vagdattm moolam nalki .
ennall nayayaprmannam entinnu ? vagdattm labhichasntati varuvollam atu lamghanangall nimittm koodticheett rtum dootanmar mukhantaram maddhysthnte kayaill eelpichaatumreta .
oruttn matrm ekkill maddhysthn vendivarikayilla ; daivamo oruttn matrm .
