ennall nammude rakshitavaydaivattinte dayayum manu kshaypriitiyum udichaappoll
avan namme nam cheyat niitiprvrattikallalalla , tante karunnaprkaramaretrakshichaatu .
nam avante krapayall niitiikarikyppedtidtu prtayashaprkram nitayjiivante avakashikallayittiirendatinnu punr nanasanam kondum
nammude rakshitavayyeshukrisatu moolam nammude mell dharallamayi pakannar parishuddhatmavinte naviikarannam kondum tanne .
i vachanam vishasayogaym ; daivattill vishsichaavar sallprvrattikallill utsahikallayirippan karutendati nnu nii itu urrappichau parrayennam ennu njan ichchikyunnu . itu shubhavum manukshaykyru upakaravum aakunnu .
meddhaytakyrvum vamshavalikallum kalahavum nayayaprmannttekyurrichaullvadavum ojhyinjunilky . ivnikshrpyojnavum vaytthrvumalela .
sabhayill bhinnatvaruttunnmanukshaynodu onnu randu vadtm buddhi parranj sheksham avane ojhyiky ;
inganeyullavan vakrbuddhiyayi papam cheyatu tanne ttan kuttm vidhichairikyunnu ennu ninakyu arriyamalela .
njan attermasineyo tihikyosineyo ango dtu ayakyuboll nikyoppolisill vannu ennodu che ruvan shrmiky . avide njan shiitakalam kajhyippan ni schayichairikyunnu .
nayayashasrtiyaysenasinnum appolelasinnum oru mudtum varatavannm utsahichau vajhyiyatr ayaky .
namukyullavarum phalamillattvar aakate atayavashaysamgtikallill sallprvrattikallkyu mumbarayirippan patthikydte .
ennodu koodeyullavar ellavarum ninakyu vandnam chollunnu . njangalle vishasattill senhikyunnavakyru vandnam cholluka . krapningallodellavarodum koode irikyumarrakadte .
krisatiyeshuvinte baddhnaypelosum sahodaranaytimotheyosum njangallude priyanum koodtu velakyaranu mayphilemon ennninakyum
sahodariyayappiyekyum njangallude sahabhadanaykyripposinnum ninte viidtile sabhekyum ejhyutunnatu :
nammude pitavaydaivattikkll ninnum kattravayyeshukrisatuvikkll ninnum ningallkyu krapayum samadhanvum undakadte .
kattravayyeshuvinodum sakalavishuddhnmarodum ninakyu llsenhatteyum vishasatteyum kurrichau njan kedtidtu
nammilullellnanmayudeyum parinjanattall ninte vi shasattinte koodtay krisatuvinnayi saphalamakendati nnu
ente pratthrnayill ninne oattru eppojhyum ente daivattinnu setatrm cheyaunnu .
sahodara , vishuddhnmarude hradayam nii tannuppichaatu nimi ttm ninte senhattill enikyu vallare santokshavum ashasavum undayi .
aakayall yuktamayatu ninnodu kalpippan krisatuvill enikyu vallare dhaiyaarm undekkilum
pelos ennvayassnum ippoll krisatuyeshuvinte baddhnumayirikyunni njan senham nimittm ape kshikyyaretcheyaunnatu .
tadavill irikyuboll njan janippichaente makanayo nesimosinnu vendi aakunnu ninnodu apekshikyunntu .
avan mube ninakyu pryojanamillattvan aayirunnu ; ippoll ninakyum enikyum nallpryojanamullavan tnne .
enikyu prannapriyanayavane njan madakyi ayachairi kyunnu .
suvisheksham nimittmulltadavill enne shushrookshikyendati nnu avane ninakyu pakaram ente adukyll tanne nittri kyollvan enikyu aagrhamundayirunnu .
ekkilum ninte gunnam nibaarndttall ennapole alla , manassode aakendatinnu ninte sammtam koodate onnum cheyvan enikyu manassillayirunnu .
avan alpakalam verruvidtu poyatu avane sadakalttekyum ninakyu labhikyendatinnu aayirikyum ;
avan ini dasanalla , dasannu miite priysahodaran tanne ; avan vishekshall enikyu priyan ekkill ninakyu jaddasambandmayum kattrrsambandmayum etr adhikam ?
aakayall nii enne koodtalli ennu karutunnu ekkill avane enneppole chettrukollka .
avan ninnodu vallatum anayayam cheyatidto kadampedti dto undekkill atu ente perill kannakyidtu kollka .
pelos ennnjan sntakayaall ejhyutiyirikyunnu ; njan tannu tiikyram . nii ninne tanne enikyu taruvan kadam pedtirikyunnu ennu njan parrayennam ennillalela .
ate sahodara , ninnekyondu enikyu kattravill oranubhavam vendiyirikyunnu ; krisatuvill ente hradayam tannuppiky .
ninte anusarannattepptti enikyu nischayam undu ; njan parrayunnatilumadhikam nii cheyaum ennarrinjidtakunnu njan ejhyutunnatu .
itallate ningallude pratthrnayall njan ningallkyu nalkappedum ennu prtayashundakakondu enikyu pappridam orukyikyollka .
krisatuyeshuvill ente sahabaddhnayeppphrasum
ente koodtuvelakyaranaymakyerasum arisatkyerasum demasum lookyosum ninakyu vandnam chollunnu .
nammude kattravayyeshukrisatvinte krapningallude aatmavodukoode irikyumarrakadte . aamen .
daivam pandu bhagam bhagamayidtum vividhamayidtum prvachaknmar mukhantaram pitakynmarodu arullicheeyatidtu
i antaykalattu putrn mukhantaram nammodu arullichee yatirikyunnu . avane tan sakalattinnum avakashiyakyi vechau ; avan mukhantaram lokatteyum undakyi .
avan avante tejassinte prbhayum tatttinte mudryum sakalatteyum tante shtiyullvachanattall vahikyunnavnum aakakondu papangallkyu pariharam undakyiysheksham uyarattill mahimayude valattubhagattu irikyyum
avan daivadootanmarekyall vishishtamaynamattinnu avkashiyayatinnu ottvannm avarekyall reshakshannayittiiru kayum cheyatu .
" nii ente putrn ; njan innu ninne janippichairikyunnu " ennum " njan avannu pitavum avan enikyu putrnum aayirikyum " ennum dootanmarill aarodekkilum vallappo jhyum arullicheeyatidtundo ?
aadayjatane pinneyum bhootalattilekyu prveshippikyu boll : " daivattinte sakaldootanmarum avane namasky rikyennam " ennu tan arullicheeyaunnu .
" avan kattukalle tante dootanmarum ijalaye tante shushrookshakanmarum aakyunnu " ennu dootanmarekyurrichau parrayu nnu .
putrnodo : " daivame , ninte simhasanam ennum e nnekyumullatu ; ninte rajatttinte chekkoll nerullchekkoll .
nii niitiye ishtappedukayum dushtataye devkshikyyum cheyati rikyyall daivame , ninte daivam ninte koodtukarill pramayi ninne aanandtailam kondu abhikshekam cheyatiri kyunnu " ennum
" kattrave , nii poovaarkalattu bhoomikyu adisthanam idtu , aakashavum ninte kaikallude prvratti aakunnu .
avnashikyum ; niiyo nilanilkyum ; avellam vasrtm pole pajhyakippokum ;
uduppupole nii avaye churudtum ; vasrtmpole avmarrippokum ; niiyo ananayn ; ninte samvrangall avasanikyyumilla " ennum parrayunnu .
" njan ninte shatrukylle ninakyu padapiitthamakyuvollam nii ente valattu bhagattiriky " ennu dootanmarill aarode kkilum vallappojhyum arullicheeyatidtundo ?
avar okyeyum rakshprapippanullavarude shushrookshekyu ayakyppedunnsevakatmakyllallayo ?
atukondu nam vallappojhyum ojhyukippokatirikyendati nnu kedttu adhikam shrddhyode karutikyollvan aavshaymakunnu .
dootanmar mukhantaram arullicheeyat vachanam sthiramayirikyyum oaroro lamghanattinnu anusarannakyedinnum nayayamayprtiphalam labhikyyum cheyatu ekkill
kattravu tan parranjutudangiyatum daivam adayallangalllum atbhutangallalum vividhviiyaarprvrattikallalum tante ishtaprkaram parishuddhatmavine nalkikyondum sakshi ninnatum kedtvar namukyu urrappichau tannatumay
itr valiyrakshnam gannaymakyate poyall engane tetti ojhyiyum ?
nam prsatavikyunnbhavi lokatte avan dootanmakyrlllelkiijhyepduttiyatu .
ennall " manukshayne nii oakyerndatinnu avan entu ? manukshayputrne sandsharikyendatinnu avan entumatrm ?
nii avane dootanmarekyall alpam matrm tajhytti ; tejssum bahumanavum avane anniyichairikyunnu ; ninte kaikallude prvrattikallkyu nii avane adhipati aakyi ,
sakalavum avante kalkyiijhyakyiyirikyunnu " ennu oruvan oredattu sakshaym parrayunnu . sakalavum avannu kiijhyakyi yatill onnineyum kiijhyepduttate vidtidtilla ; ennall i ppoll sakalavum avannu kiijhyepdttayi kannunnilla .
ekkilum daivakrapayall ellavakyrum vendi marannam aasdippan dootanmarilum alpam oru tvannavanayyeshu marannam anubhavichaatukondu avane mahatvum bahumanavum anninjvanayi nam kannunnu .
sakalattinnu lakyum sakalattinnum karannabhootanumayavan anekam putrnmare tejassilekyu nadattuboll avaru de rakshanayakane kashtanubhavangallall tikanjvanakyunntu yuktam aayirunnu .
vishuddhiikarikyunnavannum vishuddhiikarikyppedunnavakyrum ellam oruvanalelpitavu ; atu hetuvayi avan avare sahodaranmar ennu villippan likyate :
" njan ninte namatte ente sahodaranmarodu kiittri kyum ; sabhamaddhey njan ninne satutikyum " ennum
" njan avanill aashryikyum " ennum " itnjanum dai vam enikyu tannmakyllum " ennum parrayunnu .
makyll jaddartangallodu koodiyavar aakakondu avanum avareppole jaddartangallodu koodiyavanayi marannatti nte adhikariyaypishachine tante marannattall niikyi
jiivapayaarntam marannabhiitiyall adimakallayirunnavare okye yum viduvichau .
dootanmare samrakshannacheyvanallabrahaminte santati ye samrakshanncheyvanaretavan vannatu .
atukondu janattinte papangallkyu prayittm vruttuvan avan karunnayullavanum daivakayaarttill vi shsat mahapurohitanum aakendatinnu sakalattilum tnte sahodaranmarodu sadrashanayittiiruvan aavashaymyirunnu .
tan tanne pariikshitanayi kashtamanubhavichairikyyall parii kshikyppedunnavakyru sahayippan kajhyivullavan aakunnu .
atukondu vishuddh sahodaranmare , sggriiyvillikyu oaharikyarayullore , nam siikarichau parrayunnappo satlanum mahapurohitanumayyeshuvine shrddhichau no kyuvin .
moshe daivabhavanattill okyeyum vishsatnayirunnatu pole yeshuvum tanne niyamichaakyiyavannu vishsatn aakunnu .
bhavanattekyallum bhavanam chamechaavannu adhikam manamullatu pole yeshuvum mosheyekyall adhikam mahatttinnu yogayn ennu ennyirikyunnu .
eetu bhavanavum chameppan orall vennam ; savaarvum chamechaavn daivam tanne .
avante bhavanattill okyeyum moshe vishshatnayirunnatu arullicheeyvanirunnatinnu sakshaym parrayunnbhrataynayidt reta .
krisatuvo avante bhavanattinnu adhikariyayputrnyidtu tanne ; prtayashayude dhaiyaarvum prshamsayum nam avasanattollam murrukeppidichau kondall nam tanne avante bhavanam aakunnu .
atu kondu parishuddhatmavu arullicheeyaunnatu pole :
" innu ningall avante shabdam kellkyunnuvekkill marubhoomiyill vechau pariikshdivasattile mrattill ennapole ningallude hradayam katthinamakyrutu .
avidevechau ningallude pitakynmar enne pariikshichau nalpatu aandu ente prvrattikalle kandidtum enne sho dhancheyatu .
atukondu enikyu atalamurrayodu niirasam undayi . avar eppojhyum tettippokunnhradayamullavar ennum njan parranju ;
avar ente ssthtayill prveshikyyillennu njan ente rekadhattill sataym cheyatu . "
sahodaranmare , jiivanulldaivatte tayjichau kallayatiri kyendatinnu avishasamulldushtahradayam ningallill aakyrum undakatirippan nokyuvin .
ningall aarum papattinte chatiyall katthinappedatirikye ndatinnu " innu " ennu parrayunnedattollam nalltorrum aneyanaym prbodhippichau kollvin .
aadayvishasam avasanattollam murrukeppidichau ko ndall nam krisatuvill pakkallikallayittiinnaririkyunnuvalela .
" innu ningall avante shabdam kellkyunnuvekkill mrttill ennpole ningallude hradayangalle katthinamakyru tu "
ennu parrayunnatill aarakunnu kedtidtu mrichaavar ? misryiimill ninnu moshe mukhantaram purrappedtu vannavar ellavarumalela .
nalpatu aandu aarodum kruddhichau ? papam cheyatvarodallyo ? avarude shavangall marubhoomiyill viinnu poyi .
ente ssthtayill prveshikyyillennu aannayidttu anusarannam kedtvarodallate pinne aarodakunnu ?
ingane avishasam nimittm avakyru prveshippan kajhyinjillennu nam kannunnu .
avante ssthtayill prveshippanullvagdattm shekshi chairikyyall ningallill aakyerkkilum atu labhikyate po yi ennu varatirippan nam bhayappeduka .
avareppole namum oru sadttrmanam kedtvar aaku nnu ; ekkilum kedtvarill vishasamayi parinnamikyaykkondu kedt vachanam avakyru upakaramayi vannilla .
vishsichaavaraynamalelssthtayill prveshikyunnu ; loksthapanattikkll prvrattikall tiinnarupoyashekshvum : " avar ente ssthtayill prveshikyyillennu njan ente kopattill sataym cheyatu " ennu arullichee yatirikyunnuvalela .
" eejhyam nallill daivam tante sakalprvrattikallill ninnu nivrattnayi " ennu eejhyam nallinekyurrichau oredattu parrnjirikyunnu .
" ente ssthtayill avar prveshikyyilla " ennu ivide pinneyum arullicheeyaunnu .
atu kondu chilar atill prveshippan idshekshichairi kyyalum mube sadttrmanam kedtvar anusarannakyedu nimittm prveshikyate pokayalum
itr kalattinte sheksham daviid mukhantaram : " innu avnte shabdam kellkyunnu ekkill ningallude hradayam katthinmakyrutu " ennu mube parranjtupole " innu " e nnoru divasam pinneyum nischayikyunnu .
yoshuvavakyru ssthtvarutti ekkill mattoru divasttekyurrichau pinnattetill kalpikyyillayirunnu ;
aakayall daivattinte janattinnu oru shabaattnubhavam shekshichairikyunnu .
daivam tante prvrattikallill ninnu ennapole avnte ssthtayill prveshichaavan tanum tante prvrattikllill ninnu nivrattnayittiinnaru .
atukondu aarum anusarannakyedinte samdrashtantatti nnottvannm viijhyatirikyendatinnu nam assthtayill prveshippan utsahiky .
daivattinte vachanam jiivanum chaitanayvumullatayi iru vayttlayulleetu vallinekyallum moochaaryerriyatum prnnaneyum aatmavineyum sandimkalleyum verruviduvi kyum vare tullechau chellunnatum hradayattile chintananglleyum bhavangalleyum vivechikyunnatum aakunnu .
avannu marranjirikyunnoru srashtiyumilla ; sakalavum avnte kanninnu nvum malannartumayi kidakyunnu ; avanumayi dtakunnu namukyu kayaarmullatu .
aakayall daivaputrnayyeshu aakashattill koodi kadnnu poyoru reshakshanmahapurohitanayi namukyu ulltu kondu nam nammude siikaram murrukeppidichau koll ka .
namukyullmahapurohitan nammude balahiinatakallill sahatapam kannippan kajhyiyattvanalla ; papam ojhyike savaarttilum namukyu tulaymayi pariikshikyppedtvanaretnamukyullatu .
atukondu karunnlabhippanum tmayattu sahayatti nnullkrapprapippanumayi nam dhaiyaarttode krapsanattinnu aduttu chelluka .
manukshayrude idayill ninnu edukyunneetu mahapurohi tanum papangallkyayi vajhyipadum yagavum apprippan daivakayaarttill manukshaykyru vendi niyamikyppedunnu .
tanum balahiinatpoondavanakayall arrivillattvarodum vajhyi tettippokunnavarodum sahatapam kannippan kajhyi yunnavanum
balahiinatnimittm janattinnu vendi ennapole tnikyu vendiyum papayagam apprikyendiyavanum aakunnu .
ennall aharoneppole daivam vallikyunnavanallate aarum asthanam stave edukyunnilla .
avaannm krisatuvum mahapurohitan aakuvanullmahtm stave eduttidtill " nii ente putrn ; innu njn ninne janippichairikyunnu " ennu avanodu arullichee yatvan avannu kodutttareta .
angane mattoredattum : " nii malkyiisedekyinte krmapr karam ennekyum oru purohitan " ennu parrayunnu .
krisatu tante eehikjiivakalattu tanne marannattill ni nnu rakshippan kajhyiyunnavanodu urrechanilavilliyodum knnuniirodum koode apekshayum abhayayachanayum kajhyiky yum bhayabhti nimittm uttram labhikyyum cheyatu .
putrn ekkilum tan anubhavichakashtangallall anusarnnam patthichau
tikanjvanayi tanne anusarikyunneevakyrum nitayrakshyude karannabhootanayittiinnaru .
malkyiisedekyinte krmaprkaram mahapurohitan ennu llnamam daivattall labhichaumirikyunnu .
itinekyurrichau njangallkyu vallare parravanundu ; ekkilum ningall kellppan mandymullavarayi tiinnartukondu te lliyichautaruvan vikshamam .
kalam nokyiyall ippoll upadeshtakynmar aayirikye ndunnningallkyu daivattinte arullappadukallude aaday patthangalle tanne viindum upadeshichau taruvan aavashaymyirikyunnu ; kadtiyayullaaharamalla , palaretningallkyu aavashaymennu vannirikyunnu .
pall kudikyunnavan ellam niitiyude vachanattill parichyamillattvanareta ; avan shishuvalela .
kadtiyayullaaharam nanmatinmakalle tirichaarrivan tajhyaky ttall abhaysichindriyangallullavarayi prayam tikanjvkyer pattukayullu .
atukondu nijjariivaprvrattikallekyurrichaullmanasantram , daivattikkle vishasam , sanangallekyurrichaullupdesham , kaiveppu , marichaavarude punarutthanam ,
nitayshikshavidhi enninganeyulladisthanam pinneyum idate nam krisatuvinekyurrichaullaadayvachanam vidtu prinjanapoottri prapippan shrmikyuka .
daivam anuvadikyunnpaksham nam atu cheyaum .
orikyll prkashanam labhichaidtu sggriiyadanam aasdikyyum parishuddhatmavine prapikyyum
daivattinte nallvachanavum varuvanulllokattinte shtiyum aasdikyyum cheyatvar pinmarrippoyall
tangallkyu tanne daivaputrne viindum krooshikyunnavarum avannu lokapavadam varuttunnavarum aakakondu avare pinneyum manasantarattilekyu putukyuvan kajhyivullatalla .
palappojhyum peyat majhyakudichaidtu bhoomi krakshi cheyaunnavakyru hitamaysasayadikalle villayikyunnu ekkill daivatti nte anugrham prapikyunnu .
mullum njerinjilum mulleppichaalo atu kollaruttttum shapattinnu adutttum aakunnu ; chudtukallakaretatinte avasanam .
ennall priyamullavare , njangall ingane samsarikyunnu ekkilum ningallekyurrichau shubhamerriyatum rakshekyu utakunntum vishsikyunnu .
daivam ningallude prvrattiyum vishuddhnmare shushrookshichaati nalum shushrookshikyunnatinalum tante namattodu kannichasenhavum marrannukallavan takyvannm aniitiyullavanalla .
ennall ningall oaroruttn prtayashayude poonnrnischyam prapippan avasanattollam orupole utsaham kannikyennamennu njangall aagrhikyunnu .
angane ningall mandtayullavarakate vishasattalum diigharkshamayalum vagdattngalle avakashamakyunnavarude anukarikallayittiirum .
daivam abrahaminodu vagdattm cheyauboll tanne kyall valiyavanekyondu sataym cheyvan illanjidtu tannekyondu tanne sataym cheyatu :
" njan ninne anugrhikyyum ninne vaddhrippikyyum che yaum " ennu arullicheeyatu .
angane avan diigharkshamayodirunnu vagdattvikshayam prapichau .
tangallekyall valiyavanekyondalelmanukshayr sataym che yaunnatu ; aannavakyru urrappinnayi sakalvadattinteyum tiichaaryakunnu .
atukondu daivam vagdattttinte avakashikallkyu tante aalochanmarratttu ennu adhikam spashtamayi kannippan ichchichau oru aannayalum urrappu koduttu .
angane nammude mumbill vechaidtullprtayashpidichauko llvan sharannattinnayi oadivannnam marrippokatttum daivattinnu bhokshkyuparravan kajhyiyatttumayrandu kayaarngallall shtiyullprbodhanam prapippan idavaru nnu .
aprtayashnamukyu aatmavinte oru nakkooram tanne ; tu nischayavum sthiravum tirashiilekykattekyu kadakyunnatu makunnu .
avidekyu yeshu malkyiisedekyinte krmaprkaram enne kyum mahapurohitanayi mumbukoodti namukyu vendi prve shichairikyunnu .
shalemrajavum atayunnatanaydaivattinte purohi tanumayi malkyiisedek rajakynmare jayichau madngivarunnabrahamine etitteu anugrhichau ;
abraham avannu sakalattilum pattilonnu kodu ttu . avante perinnu aadaym niitiyude rajavennum pinne shalemrajavu ennu vechaall samadhanattinte rajavu ennum atthrm .
avannu pitavilla , matavilla , vamshavaliyilla , jiivarambhvum jiivavasanavum illa ; avan daivaputrnnu tulaynyi ennekyum purohitanayirikyunnu .
ivan etr mahan ennu nokyuvin ; gotrpitavayabraham koodeyum avannu kollayude vishekshasadhanngallill pattilonnu koduttuvalela .
leviputrnmarill perohitaym labhikyunnavakyru nayayprmannaprkaram janattodu dashamsham vanguvan kalpanundu ; atu abrahaminte kadiprdeshattill ninnu utbhvichasahodaranmarodu aakunnu vangunnatu .
ennall avarude vamshavaliyill ullppedattvan abrhaminodu tanne dashamsham vangiyum vagdattngall prpichaavane anugrhichaumirikyunnu .
uyannarvan tannavane anugrhikyunnu ennatinnu takyrm eetumillalela .
ivide marikyunnmanukshayr dashamsham vangunnu ; avadeyo jiivikyunnu ennsakshaym prapichaavan tanne .
dashamsham vangunnleviyum abraham mukhantaram dashamsham koduttirikyunnu ennu oru vidhattill parrayam .
avante pitavine malkyiisedekyu etirettppoll levi avante kadiprdeshattu undayirunnavalela .
levayperohitayttall samboonnrtvannekkill - ati nkiijhyaleljanam nayayaprmannam prapichaatu - aharo nte krmaprkaram ennu parrayate malkyiisedekyinte kr maprkaram verroru purohitan varuvan entoravshaym ?
perohitaym marrippokunnpaksham nayayaprmannatti nnumkoode mattm varuvan aavashaym .
ennall itu aarekyurrichau parranjirikyunnuvo avan verroru gotrttilullavan ; agotrttill aarum ygapiitthattikkll shushrookshcheyatidtilla .
yehoodayillninnu nammude kattravu udichau ennu spashtamlela ; agotrttodu moshe perohitaym sambndichau onnum kalpichaidtilla .
jaddasambandmaykalpanayude prmannattall alla , ajhyi njupokatt jiivanteshtiyall ullavayverre oru purohitan
malkyiisedekyinnu sadrashanayi udikyunnu ekkill atu eettvum adhikam telliyunnu .
nii malkyiisedekyinte krmaprkaram ennekyum purohi tan ennalelsakshiikarichairikyunnatu .
mumbilatte kalpanekyu atinte balahiinatayum nikshrpyo janavum nimittm niikyvum -
nayayaprmannattall onnum poottriprapichaidtillalel-nam daivattodu adukyunnatinulleerre nallprtayashekyu sthapanavum vannirikyunnu .
avar aannkoodate purohitanmarayittiinnaru .
ivano " nii ennekyum purohitan ennu kattravu sataym cheyatu , anutapikyyumilla " ennu tannodu arullicheeyatvan idt aannayodu koode tanne .
aannkoodateyallennatinnu ottvannm vishekshamerriyniyamattinnu yeshu uttravadiyayi tiinnaririkyunnu .
marannamnimittm avakyru nilanilpan mudakym varikakondu purohitanmar aayittiinnarvar anekar aakunnu .
ivano , ennekyum irikyunnatukondu marratt pe rohitaym aakunnu prapichairikyunnatu .
atukondu tan mukhantaramayi daivattodu adukyu nnavakyru vendi pakshavadam cheyvan sadjiivikyunnavnakayall avare poonnrmayi rakshippan , avan prapat tnakunnu .
inganeyullmahapurohitanalelnamukyu vendiyatu : pavitrn , nidterakshan , nimmrlan , papikallodu verruvidtvn , sggrttekyall unnatanayittiinnarvan ;
amahapurohitanmareppole aadaym sntapapangall kyayum pinne janattinte papangallkyayum dinamprti yagam kajhyippan aavashaymillattvan tanne . atu avan tannettan apprichaukondu orikylayidtu cheyatuvalela .
nayayaprmannam balahiinamanukshayre mahapurohitanmarkyunnu ; nayayaprmannattinnu pimbullaannayude vachanamo ennekyum tikenjvanayittiinnar putrne purohatankyunnu .
nam i parrayunnatinte saram entennall . sggrttill mahimasanattinte valattu bhagattu irunnavanayi ,
vishuddhsthlattinteyum manukshaynallkattravu sthapichasataykoodarattinteyum shushrookshakanaymahapurohitan namukyundu .
eetu mahapurohitanum vajhyipadum yagavum apprippan niyamikyppedunnu ; aakayall apprippan ivannum vallatum vennam .
avan bhoomiyill aayirunnekkill purohitan aakayillyirunnu ; nayayaprmannaprkaram vajhyipadu apprikyunnavar undalela .
koodaram tiippran moshe aarambhichaappoll " pavaartattill ni nakyu kannichamatrakaprkaram nii sakalavum cheyvan nokyuka " ennu avanodu arullicheeyattupole avar sggriiyattinte drashtantavum nijhyalumayatill shushrookshcheyau nnu .
avano vishekshatayerriyvagdattngallinmell sthapiky ppedt niyamattinte maddhysthnakayall atinte vishekshtekyu ottvannm vishekshatayerriyshushrookshayum prapichai rikyunnu .
onnamatte niyamam kurravillatttayirunnu ekkill randamttetinnu idam anevkshikyyillayirunnu .
ennall avan avare aakshepichau kondu arullicheeyau nnatu : " njan yisrayellgrahattodum yehoodagrahttodum putiyoru niyamam cheyaunnkalam varum ennu kattravinte arullappadu .
njan avarude pitakynmare kaikyu pidichau misryiim deshattuninnu konduvannnallill njan avarodu che yat niyamampole alla ; avar ente niyamattill nilani nnilla ; njan avare aadarichaatumillennu kattravinte rullappadu .
i kalam kajhyinjsheksham njan yisrayell grahattodu cheyvanirikyunnniyamam ingane aakunnu : njan ente nayayaprmannam avarude ullilakyi avarude hradayangalli ll ejhyutum ; njan avakyru daivamayum avar enikyu jnamayum irikyum .
ini avarill aarum tante koodtukaraneyum tante saho daraneyum kattravine arrikennu upadeshikyyilla ; avr aabalavraddhm ellavarum enne arriyum .
njan avarude akratayngallekyurrichau karunnayullavan aakum ; avarude papangalle ini oakyryumillennu kattravinte arullappadu . "
putiyatu ennu parrayunnatinall aadayttetine pajhyayatkyiyirikyunnu ; ennall pajhyayatakunnatum jiinnrikyunnatum e llam niingippokuvan aduttirikyunnu .
ennall aaday niyamattinnum aaradhanekyullchadtngallum lekikamayvishuddhmandiravum undayirunnu .
oru koodaram chamechau ; atinte aadaybhagattu nilavillakyum meshayum kyappvum undayirunnu . atinnu vishuddhsth lam ennu per .
randam tirashiilekyu pinnilo ativishuddhm ennkoodaram undayirunnu .
atill ponnukondulldhoopakalashavum mujhyuvanum po nnu potinj niyamapedtkavum atinnakattu mannidtuve chapon patrvum aharonte tallittr vadiyum niyamttinte kalpalakakallum
atinnu miite krapasanatte moodunntejassinte keroobu kallum undayirunnu . atu ippoll oronnayi vivarippn kajhyivilla .
ivingane tiinnar sheksham purohitanmar nitaym mun koo darattillchennu shushrookshkajhyikyum .
randamattetilo aandill orikyll mahapurohitan mtrm chellum ; rtam koodate alla ; atu avan tanteyum janattinteyum abaddhngallkyu vendi apprikyum .
mukkoodaram nilkyunnedattollam vishuddhmandirattilekyullvajhyi vellippedtillennu parishuddhatmavu itinall soochi ppikyunnu .
akoodaram i kalattekyu oru sadrashaymareta . atinnu ottvannm aaradhanakyarannu manassakshiyill poonnrsamadhnam varuttuvan kajhyiyatt vajhyipadum yagavum apprichau porunnu .
avbhakshayngall , paniiyangall , vividhsanangall ennivyodu koode ganniikarannakalattollam chumattiyirunnjaddi kniyamangallareta .
krisatuvo varuvanullnanmakallude mahapurohitanayi vannidtu : kaippnniyallatttayi ennuvechaall i srashti yill ullppedatttayi valippvum tikavumerriyoru koodrattill koodi
aadtukottnmarudeyum pashukyidakylludeyum rtattalalla , sntartattall tanne orikylayidtu vishuddh mandirattill prveshichau ennekyumulloru viindeduppu sadhippichau .
aadtukottnmarudeyum kallakalludeyum rtavum malinappedt varude mell tallikyunnpashubhasvum jaddikashuddhi varuttu nnu ekkill
nitayatmavinall daivattinnu tannettan nikshkyllakknyi apprichakrisatuvinte rtam jiivanulldaivatte aardhippan ningallude manassakshiye nijjariivprvrattikalle pokyi etr adhikam shuddhiikarikyum ?
atu nimittm aadayniyamattile lamghanangallill ninnullviindeduppinnayi oru marannam undayidtu nitayavakashatti nte vagdattm villikyppedtvakyru labhikyendatinnu avan putiyniyamattinte maddhysthn aakunnu .
niyamam ulledattu niyamakattravinte marannam tellivan aavashaym .
marichashekshamalelniyamam sthiramakunnatu ; niyamakattravi nte jiivakalattollam atinnu urrappilla .
atukondu aadayniyamavum rtam koodate prtikshanichaatlla .
moshe nayayaprmannaprkaram kalpanokyeyum sakalajanttodum prsatavichasheksham pashukyidakylludeyum aadtuko ttnmarudeyum rtatte vellavum chuvannaadtu romavum isoppumayi eduttu pusatkattinmelum sakaljanttinmelum tallichau :
" itu daivam ningallodu kalpichaniyamattinte rtam " ennu parranju .
angane tanne avan koodarattinmelum aaradhanekyullupakarannangallinmelum ellam rtam tallichau .
nayayaprmannaprkaram eekadesham sakalavum rtattall shu ddhiikarikyppedunnu ; rtam chorinjidtllate vimochanami lla .
aakayall sggrttilullavayude prtibimbangalle ivakyall shuddhmakyunnatu aavashaym . sggriiyamayavekyo ivyekyall nallyagangall aavashaym .
krisatu vasatvamayatinte prtibimbamayi kaippnniyayvishuddh mandirattilekylla , ippoll namukyu vendi daivsannidhiyill prtaykshanavan sggrttilekyretprveshi chaatu .
mahapurohitan aandutorrum anayrtattodukoode vishuddhmandirattill prveshikyunnatupole avan tannettan koodakyoode apprippan aavashaymilla .
anganeyayall lokasthapanam mutalkyu avan palppojhyum kashtamanubhavikyendiyirunnu . ennall avan lo kavasanattill sntyagamkondu papapariharam vruttuvan orikyll prtaykshanayi .
orikyll marikyyum pinne nayayavidhiyum manukshaykyru niymichairikyyall
krisatuvum angane tanne anekarude papangalle chumappan orikyll apprikyppedtu tanikyayi kattu nilkyunnavarude rakshekyayi avan papam koodate randamatu prtaykshanakum .
nayayaprmannam varuvanullnanmakallude nijhyalallate kayaarrrrr rngallude sakshall sroopamallaykakondu aandutorrum idavidate kajhyichauvarunnate yagangallall aduttu varu nnavakyru sallgunnapoottri varuttuvan oru nallum kajhyivulltalla .
alelkkill aaradhanakyakyru orikyll shuddhivannatinte she ksham papangallekyurrichaullmanobodham pinne illaykkondu yagam kajhyikyunnatu ninnu pokayillayo ?
ippojhyo aandutorrum avayall papangallude oammr undakunnu .
kallakalludeyum aadtukottnmarudeyum rtattinnu papngalle niikyuvan kajhyiyunnatalla .
aakayall lokattill varuboll : " hananayagavum vajhyi padum nii ichchichailla ; ennall oru shariiram nii enikyu oru kyiyirikyunnu .
savaaramgahomangallilum papayagangallilum nii prsadichai lla .
appoll njan parranju : ita , njan varunnu ; pusatkachau rullill ennekyurrichau ejhyutiyirikyunnu ; daivame , ninte ishtam cheyvan njan varunnu " ennu avan parrayunnu .
nayayaprmannaprkaram kajhyichauvarunnyagangallum vajhyipadum savaaramgahomangallum papayagangallum nii ichchichaillavayi ll prsadichaatumillenningane parranjsheksham :
ita , njan ninte ishtam cheyvan varunnu ennu parrnjukondu avan randamattetine sthapippan onnamttetine niikyikyllayunnu .
ishtattill nam yeshukrisatu orikylayi kajhyichashariiryagattall vishuddhiikarikyppedtirikyunnu .
eetu purohitanum divasenshushrookshichaum papangalle priharippan orunallum kajhyiyatt ate yagangalle koodakyoo de kajhyichaaumkondu nilkyunnu .
yeshuvo papangallkyu vendi eekayagam kajhyichaidtu enne kyum daivattinte valattu bhagattu irunnukondu
tante shatrukyll tante padapiittham aakuvollam kattirikyu nnu .
eekayagattall avan vishuddhiikarikyppedunnavakyru sadaklattekyum sallgunnapoottri varuttiyirikyunnu .
atu parishuddhatmavum namukyu sakshiikarikyunnu .
" i kalam kajhyinjsheksham njan avarodu cheyvaniri kyunnniyamam inganeyakunnu : ente nayayaprmannam varude ullilakyi avarude hradayangallill ejhyutum ennu kattravinte arullappadu " ennu arullicheeyatsheksham :
" avarude papangalleyum akratayngalleyum njan ini oakyryumilla " ennu arullicheeyaunnu .
ennall ivayude mochanam ulledattu inimell papangllkyu vendi oru yagavum aavashaymilla .
atukondu sahodaranmare , yeshu tante deham ennti rashiilayill koodi namukyu prtikshanichajiivanullputuvajhyiyyi , tante rtattall
vishuddhmandirattilekyullprveshanattinnu dhaiyaarvum
daivalayattinmell oru mahapurohitanum namukyullatu kondu
nam dummrnassakshi niingumarru hradayangallill tallikyppedtvrum shuddhvellattall shariiram kajhyukappedtvarumayi vishasttinte poonnrnischayam poondu paramatthrhradayattode duttu chelluka .
prtayashayude siikaram nam murruke pidichaukollka ; vagdattm cheyatvan vishsatnalela .
chilar cheyaunnatupole nammude sabhayogangalle upe kshikyate tammill prbodhippichaukondu senhattinnum salaprvrattikallkyum
utsaham vaddhrippippan aneyanaym sookshichaukollka . nall samiipikyunnu ennu kannum torrum atu adhikamdhikamayi cheyeendatakunnu .
satayttinte parinjanam labhichaasheksham nam manpoovaarm ppam cheyatall papangallkyu vendi ini oru yagavum she kshikyate
nayayavidhikyayi bhayakkramayoru prtiikshayum etiriklle dahippippanullrekadhiyumeyullu .
mosheyude nayayaprmannam anusarikyattvannu karunnkoodate randu moonnu sakshikallude vamojhyi kedtu marannshikshkalpikyunnuvalela .
daivaputrne chavidtikyllakayum tanne vishuddhiikarichaniyamrtatte malinam ennu niroopikyyum krapayude aatmavi ne nindikyyum cheyatvan etr katthinamerriyshikshekyu patrmakum ennu vicharippin .
" prtikaram enikyullatu , njan pakaram viidtum " ennum " kattravu tante janatte nayayam vidhikyum " ennum arullicheeyatvane nam arriyunnuvalela .
jiivanulldaivattinte kayaill viijhyunnatu bhayakkram .
ennall ningall prkashanam labhichaasheksham nindkallalum pii ddakallalum koottukyayi bhavichaum
avakanubhavikyunnavakyru koodtallikallayittiinnarum ingne kashtangallall vallare poradtm kajhyichapoovaarkalam ottrukollvin .
tadavukarodu ningall sahatapam kannichaatallate sggr ttill nilanilkyunnuttmasambattu ningallkyu undu e nnarrinju sambattukallude apaharavum santokshattode sahichauvalela .
atukondu mahprtiphalamullningallude dhaiyaarm tllikyllayarutu .
daiveshtam cheyatu vagdattm prapippan sahikshnnatningallkyu aavashaym .
" ini etryum alpakalam kajhyinjidtu varuvanullavan varum tamasikyyumilla ; "
ennall " ente niitiman vishasattall jiivikyum ; pin marrunnu ekkill ente ullattinnu avanill prsadamilla " .
namo nashattilekyu pinmarrunnavarude koodtttilalla , vi shsichau jiivarakshprapikyunnavarude koodtttilaretaaku nnu .
vishasam ennato , aashikyunnatinte urrappum kannatt kayaarngallude nischayavum aakunnu .
atinalalelpoovaarnmakyru sakshaym labhichaatu .
i kannunnlokattinnu drashaymayatallkarannam ennu varumarru lokam daivattinte vachanattall nimmrikyppedtu ennu nam vishasattall arriyunnu .
vishasattall habell daivattinnu kayiintetilum u ttmamayyagam kajhyichau ; atinall avannu niitiman ennsakshaym labhichau ; daivam avante vajhyipadinnu sakshaym klpichau . marichaashekshavum avan vishsattall samsarichau kondirikyunnu .
vishasattall hanok marannam kannate edukyppedtu ; daivam avane eduttu kondatinall kannateyayi . avan daivatte prsadippichau ennu avan edukyppedt tinnu mube sakshaym prapichau .
ennall vishasam koodate daivatte prsadippippan kajhyiyunnatalla ; daivattrinte adukyll varunnavan daivam undu ennum tanne anevkshikyunnavakyru prtiphalam kodu kyunnu ennum vishsikyendatalela .
vishasattall nohatuvare kannattvayekyurrichau arullappadundayidtu bhayabhti poondu tante kudumbattinte rakshekyayidtu oru pedtkam tiittru ; atinall avan lo katte kuttm vidhichau vishasattalullniitikyu avakshiyayittiinnaru .
vishasattall abrham tanikyu avakashamayi kidtuvnirunndeshattekyu yatryavan villikyppedtarre anusrichau evidekyu pokunnu ennarriyate purrappedtu .
vishasattall avan vagdatt deshattu oru anaydeshttu ennpole chennu vagdattttinnu koodtvakashikllayyishakyinodum yakyobinodum koode koodarangllill pattrukondu
daivam shilpiyayi nimmrichaatum adisthanangallullatumaynagarattinnayi kattirunnu .
vishasattall sarrayum vagdattm cheyatvane vishsatn ennu ennukayall prayam kajhyinjidtum puretalpadanatti nnu shti prapichau .
atukondu oruvannu , mrataprayanayavannu tanne , perupp ttill aakashattile nakshatrngallpoleyum kadalpurrtte ennikyoodatt mannallpoleyum santati janichau .
ivar ellavarum vagdatt nivratti prapikyate doorattu ninnu atu kandu abhivandichaum bhoomiyill tangall anayrum paradeshikallum ennu eettuparranjumkondu vishsattill marichau .
ingane parrayunnavar oru pitradesham anevkshikyunnu ennu kannikyunnu .
avar vidtu ponnatine oattru ekkill madangippokuvan idundayirunnuvalela .
avaro adhikam nallatine , savaggriiyamayatine tanne , kamkshichairunnu ; aakayall daivam avarude daivam ennu villikyppeduvan likyunnilla ; avan avakyrayi oru nagaram orukyiyirikyunnuvalela .
vishasattall abraham tan pariikshikyppedtppoll yishakyine yagam apprichau .
yishakyill ninnu janikyunnavar ninte santati ennu villikyppedum ennu arullappadu labhichau vagdattngalle kaikyondavan tante eekajatane apprichau ;
marichaavarude idayill ninnu uyipprippan daivam shtan ennu ennukayum avarude idayill ninnu ejhyunnettvane ppole avane tirike prapikyyum cheyatu .
vishasattall yishak yakyobineyum eeshavine yum bhavikalam sambandichau anugrhichau .
vishasattall yakyob marannakalattikkll yosephi nte makylle iruvareyum anugrhikyyum tante vadiyude attttu charikyondunamaskyrikyyum cheyatu .
vishasattall yoseph tan maripparrayappoll yi srayell makyllude purrappadinte kayaarm oapprichau , tante asthikallekyurrichau kalpankoduttu .
vishasattall mosheyude jananattikkll shishu sundran ennu ammyappnmar kandu ; rajavinte kalpanbhayappedate avane moonnu masam ollippichauvechau .
vishasattall moshe tan vallannarppoll papattinte talkyalabhogattekyallum daivajanattodukoode kashtamanu bhavikyunnatu tiranjeduttu .
prtiphalam nokyiyatukondu pharravonte putriyude makan ennu villikyppedunnatu nirasikyyum
misryiimile nikshepangallekyall krusatuvinte nind vali ydhanam ennu ennukayum cheyatu .
vishasattall avan adrashaydaivatte kandatupole urrechau nilkyyall rajavinte kopam bhayappedate misryiim vidtu ponnu .
vishasattall avan kadinjoolukallude samharakan avare todatirippan pesahayum chorattlliyum aacharichau .
vishasattall avar karayill ennapole chekkdalill koodi kadannu ; atu misryiimayr cheyvan nokyiidtu mungi ppoyi .
vishasattall avar eejhyu divasam chuttinadannappoll yeriihomatill idinjuviinnu .
vishasattall rrahab ennveshay ottukare samadhanttode kaikyondu avishasikallodukoode nashikyati runnu .
ini entu parrayendu ? gideyan , barak , shimshon , yipatah , daviid ennavareyum shamoovell mutalayprvachkanmareyum kurrichau vivarippan samayam pora .
vishasattall avar rajayngalle adakyi , niiti nadatti , vagdattm prapichau , simhangallude vay adechau ,
tiiyude balam keduttu , vallinte vaykyu tetti , balahii natayill shti prapichau , yuddhttill viiranmarayatiinnaru , naynmarude sainayngalle oadichau .
srtikallkyu tangallude marichaavare uyitterjhyunnelpinall ti rike kidti ; mattu chilar eettvum nalelaru uyitterjhyunnelpu labhikyendatinnu uddharannam kaikyollate bhedaym eettu .
verre chilar parihasam , chammdti , changala , tadavu ivayalu llpariikshanubhavichau .
kalelrru eettu , ichaarvallall arrukyppedtu , pariikshikyppedtu , vallall kollappedtu , jadayadukalludeyum koladukallude yum toll dharichau , buddhimudtum upadrvavum kashtavum sahi chau ,
kadukallilum malakallilum guhakallilum bhoomiyude pillapprukllilum ujhyannu valanju ; lokam avakyru yogaymayirunni lla .
avar ellavarum vishasattall sakshaym labhichaidtum vag dattnivratti prapichailla .
avar namme koodate rakshapoottri prapikyatirikyendati nnu daivam namukyu vendi eettvum nallatonnu munkaruti yirunnu .
aakayall namum sakshikallude itr valiyoru samooham namukyu chuttum nilkyunnatu kondu sakalbharavum murru ke pattunnpapavum vidtu namukyu mumbill vechairikyunnoadtm sthiratayode oaduka .
vishsattinte nayakanum poottri varuttunnavanumayye shuvine nokyuka ; tante mumbill vechairunnsantoksham oattru avan apamanam alakshaymakyi krooshine sahiky yum daivasimhasanattinte valattubhagattu irikyyum cheyatu .
ningallude ullill kshiinnichau madukyatirippan papikallall tanikyu neridt inganeyullvirodham sahichaavane dhaynichau kollvin .
papattodu poradunnatill ningall ituvare pranntayagattollam etittru ninnidtilla .
" makane , kattravinte shikshnirasikyrutu ; avan shasi kyuboll mukshikayumarutu ,
kattravu tan senhikyunnavane shikshikyunnu ; tan kai kyollunneetu makaneyum tallunnu " enningane makyllo du ennpole ningallodu samvadikyunnprbodhanam ningall marrannu kallanjuvo ?
ningall balashikshsahichaall daivam makyllodu ennpole ningallodu perumarrunnu ; appn shikshikyatt makan evideyullu ?
ellavarum prapikyunnbalashikshkoodatirikyunnu ekki ll ningall makyllallkeladeyanmarareta .
nammude jaddasambandmaypitakynmar namme shikshichaappoll nam avare vannangipponnuvalela ; aatmakyllude pitavinnu eettvum adhikamayi kiijhyadangi jiivikyendatallyo ?
avar shikshichaatu kurrekyalavum tangallkyu bodhichapr karavumareta ; avano , nam avante vishuddhi prapikye ndatinnu nammude gunnattinnayi tanne shikshikyunnatu .
eetu shikshayum talkyalam santokshakaramalldu : khakaramaretennu tonnum ; pinnattetilo atinall abhayasam vannvakyru niiti ennsamadhanaphalam labhikyum .
aakayall tallannar kayaum kujhyanj mujhyakkalum nivittruvin .
mudantullatu ullukyippokate bhedamakendatinnu ningallude kalinnu patnirattuvin .
ellavarodum samadhanam aacharichau shuddhiikarannam prapi ppan utsahippin . shuddhiikarannam koodate aarum kattrvine kannukayilla .

aayjiivante vachanam sambandichau - jiivan prtaykshamayi , njangall kandu sakshiikarikyyum pitavinodukoodeyirunnu njangallkyu prtaykshamaynitayjiivane ningallodu arriyi kyyum cheyaunnu -
njangall kandum kedtumullatu ningallkyu njangallodu koodtay undakendatinnu ningallodum arriyikyunnu . njangallude koodtayyo pitavinodum avante putrnayyeshukri satuvinodum aakunnu .
nammude santoksham poonnrmakuvan njangall itu ningallkyu ejhyutunnu .
daivam vellichaam aakunnu ; avanill irudtu odtum ille nnullatu njangall avanodu kedtu ningallodu arriyikyunndootakunnu .
avanodu koodtay undu ennu parrakayum irudtill nadakyyum cheyatall nam bhokshkyu parrayunnu ; sataym prvattrikyunnatu milla .
avan vellichaattill irikyunnatu pole nam vellichaatti ll nadakyunnuvekkill namukyu tammill koodtay undu ; avante putrnayyeshuvinte rtam sakalpapavum pokyi namme shuddhiikarikyunnu .
namukyu papam illennu nam parrayunnu ekkill nammett nne vanchikyunnu ; sataym nammill illateyayi .
nammude papangalle eettu parrayunnu ekkill avan nammo du papangalle kshamichau sakalaniitiyum pokyi namme shuddhiikarippan takyvannm vishsatnum niitimanum aakunnu .
nam papam cheyatidtillennu parrayunnuvekkill avane asatayvadiyakyunnu ; avante vachanam nammill illateyyi .
ente kunjungalle , ningall papam cheyaatirippan njn itu ningallkyu ejhyutunnu . oruttn papam cheyut e kkilo , niitimanayyeshukrisatu ennkayaarsthn namukyu pitavinte adukyll undu .
avan nammude papangallkyu prayittm aakunnu ; nmmudetinnu matrm alla , savaarlokattinte papattinnum tanne .
avante kalpanakalle prmannikyunnu ekkill nam avane arrinjirikyunnu ennu atinall arriyunnu .
avane arrinjirikyunnu ennu parrakayum avante kalpankalle prmannikyatirikyyum cheyaunnavan kallan aakunnu ; sataym avanill illa .
ennall aarekkilum avante vachanam prmannikyunnu ekki ll avanill daivasenham vasatvamayi tikanjirikyunnu . nam avanill irikyunnu ennu itinall namukyu arri yam .
avanill vasikyunnu ennu parrayunnavan avan nadannatu pole nadakyendatakunnu .
priyamullavare , putiyoru kalpanayallaadimutall ningall kyullpajhyaykalpanayaretnjan ningallkyu ejhyutunnatu . apajhyaykalpanningall kedt vachanam tanne .
putiyoru kalpannjan ningallkyu ejhyutunnu ennum parryam . atu avanilum ningallilum sataymayirikyunnu ; i rudtu niingippokunnu ; satayvellichaam itprkashikyunnu .
vellichaattill irikyunnu ennu parrakayum sahodarane pkekyyum cheyaunnavan inneyollam irudtill irikyunnu .
sahodarane senhikyunnavan vellichaattill vasikyunnu ; idacheerkyu avanill karannamilla .
sahodarane pakekyunnavano irudtill irikyunnu ; irudti ll nadakyyum cheyaunnu . irudtu avante kannu kurudakyukyall evidekyu pokunnu ennu avan arriyunnilla .
kunjungalle , ningallkyu avante namam nimittm papangll mochichairikyyall njan ningallkyu ejhyutunnu .
pitakynmare , aadimutalullavane ningall arrinjiriky yall ningallkyu ejhyutunnu . balaykyare , ningall dushtne jayichairikyyall ningallkyu ejhyutunnu . kunjungalle , ningall pitavine arrinjirikyyall njan ningallkyu ejhyutiyirikyunnu .
pitakynmare , aadimutalullavane ningall arrinjiriky yall njan ningallkyu ejhyutiyirikyunnu . balaykyare , ningall shtarakayalum daivavachanam ningallill vasiky yalum ningall dushtane jayichairikyyalum njan ningall kyu ejhyutiyirikyunnu .
lokatteyum lokattilullatineyum senhikyrutu . oruvan lokatte senhikyunnuvekkill avanill pitvinte senham illa .
jaddamoham , kanmoham , jiivanattinte prtapam ingane lokattilullatu ellam pitavill ninnalla , lokattill ninnaretaakunnu .
lokavum atinte mohavum ojhyinju pokunnu ; daive shtam cheyaunnavano ennekyum irikyunnu .
kunjungalle , itu antaynajhyikaakunnu ; etir krisatu varunnu ennu ningall kedtidtundalela . ippoll anekam etir krisutkyll ejhyunnettirikyyall antaynajhyikaaku nnu ennu namukyu arriyam .
avar nammude idayill ninnu purrappedtu ekkilum namukyu llavar aayirunnilla ; avar namukyullavar aayirunnu ekki ll nammodukoode pakyrumayirunnu ; ennall ellavarum namu kyullavarallennu prsiddhmakendatalela .
ningallo parishuddhnall abhikshekam prapichau sakalavum arriyunnu .
ningall sataym arriyaykakondalla , ningall atu arrikyalum bhokshkyu onnum satayttill ninnu varaykayalumretnjan ningallkyu ejhyutiyirikyunnatu .
yeshuvine krisatuvallennu nikshedhikyunnavan allate kallan aar aakunnu ? pitavineyum putrneyum ni kshedhikyunnavan tanne etir krisatu aakunnu .
putrne nikshedhikyunnavannu pitavumilla ; putrne siikrikyunnavannu pitavum undu .
ningall aadimutall kedttu ningallill vasikydte . aadimutll kedttu ningallill vasikyunnu ekkill ningall putrni lum pitavilum vasikyum .
itakunnu avan namukyu tannvagdattm : nitayjiivan tanne .
ningalle tettikyunnavare oattru njan itu ningallkyu ejhyutiyirikyunnu .
avanall prapichabhikshekam ningallill vasikyunnu ; arum ningalle upadeshippan aavashaymilla ; avante abhikshe kam tanne ningallkyu sakalavum upadeshichau tarikayalum atu bhokshkyllsataym tanne aayirikyyalum atu ni ngalle upadeshichaatu pole ningall avanill vasippin .
iniyum kunjungalle , avan prtaykshanakuboll nam avante sannidhiyill lichau pokate avante prtay kshatayill namukyu dhaiyaarm undakendatinnu avanill vasi ppin .
avan niitiman ennu ningall grhichairikyunnu ekkill niiti cheyaunnavan okyeyum avanill ninnu janichairikyu nnu ennu ningall arriyunnu .
kanmin , nam daivamakyll ennu villikyppeduvan pitvu namukyu etr valaysenham nalkiyirikyunnu ; angane tanne nam aakunnu . lokam avane arrinjidtillaykkondu nammeyum arriyunnilla .
priyamullavare , nam ippoll daivamakyll aakunnu . nam innatu aakum ennu ituvare prtaykshamayilla . avan prtaykshanakuboll nam avane tan irikyum pole tanne kannunnatakakondu avanodu sadrashanmar aakum ennu nam arriyunnu .
avanill i prtayashayullavan ellam avan nimmrlanyirikyunnatu pole tannettnne nimmrliikarikyunnu .
papam cheyaunnavan ellam adhammrvum cheyaunnu ; papam adhammrm tanne .

avanill vasikyunnavan aarum papam cheyaunnilla . papam cheyaunnavan aarum avane kandidtilla . arrinjidtumilla .
kunjungalle , aarum ningalle tettikyrutu ; avan niitimnayirikyunnatu pole niiti cheyaunnavan niitiman akunnu .
papam cheyaunnavan pishachinte makan aakunnu . pishchu aadimutall papam cheyaunnuvalela . pishachinte prvrttikalle ajhyippan tanne daivaputrn prtaykshanayi .
daivattill ninnu janichaavan aarum papam cheyaunnilla ; avante vittu avanill vasikyunnu ; daivattill ninnu janichaatinall avannu papam cheyvan kajhyikayumilla .
daivattinte makyll aarennum pishachinte makyll aare nnum itinall telliyunnu ; niiti prvattrikyattvan arum sahodarane senhikyattvanum daivattill ninnullvanalla .
ningall aadimutall kedt dootu : nam aneyanaym senhikye nnam ennalelaakunnu .
kayiin dushtanill ninnullavanayi sahodarane konnatu pole alla ; avane kolluvan samgati entu ? tante prvratti dokshavum sahodarantetu niitiyumullatakako ndareta .
sahodaranmare , lokam ningalle pakekyunnu ekkill ayaarppedarutu .
nam marannam vidtu jiivanill kadannirikyunnu ennu sahodarnmare senhikyunnatinall namukyu arriyam . senhikyatt van marannattill vasikyunnu .
sahodarane pakekyunnavan ellam kulapatakan aaku nnu . yatoru kulapatakannum nitayjiivan ullill vasi chairippillennu ningall arriyunnu .
avan namukyu vendi tante prannane vechau koduttti nall nam senham entu ennu arrinjirikyunnu ; namum sahodaranmakyru vendi prannane vechau kodukyendatkunnu .
ennall i lokattile vasatuvakayullavan aarekkilum tante sahodarannu mudtullatu kandidtu avanodu manassli vu kannikyanjall daivattintesenham avanill engne vasikyum ?
kunjungalle , nam vakyinalum navinalum alla , prvrttiyilum satayttilum tanne senhikyuka .
nam satayttinte pakshattu nilkyunnavar ennu itinall arriyum ;
hradayam namme kuttm vidhikyunnu ekkill daivam nammude hradayattekyall valiyavanum ellam arriyunnavanum ennu nammude hradayatte avante sannidhiyill urrappikyam .
priyamullavare , hradayam namme kuttm vidhikyunnilelkkill namukyu daivattodu pragatbhaym undu .
avante kalpanakalle nam prmannichau avannu prsadamulltu cheyaunnatu kondu entu yachichaalum avakkll ninnu labhikyum .
avante kalpanayo , avante putrnayyeshukrisatuvinte namattrill nam vishsikyyum avan namukyu kalpantannatu pole aneyanaym senhikyyum vennam ennullatu tanne .
avante kalpanakalle prmannikyunnavan avanilum avan ivanilum vasikyunnu . avan nammill vasikyunnu ennu avan namukyu tannaatmavinall nam arriyunnu .
priyamullavare , kallaprvachakanmar palarum lokattile kyu purrappedtirikyyall eetu aatmavineyum vishsikyte aatmakyll daivattill ninnullavayo ennu shodhancheyvin .
daivatmavine itinall arriyam ; yeshukrisatu jaddatti ll vannu ennu siikarikyunnaatmavokyeyum daivatti ll ninnullatu .
yeshuvine siikarikyatt yatoru aatmavum daivatti ll ninnullatalla . atu etir krisatuvinte aatmavu tnne ; atu varum ennu ningall kedtidtundalela ; atu i ppoll tanne lokattill undu .
kunjungalle , ningall daivattill ninnullavar aakunnu ; avare jayichaumirikyunnu . ningallilullavan lokattill ullavanekyall valiyavanalela .
avar lekikanmar aakayall lekikamayatu samsari kyunnu ; lokam avarude vakyu kellkyunnu .

priyamullavare , nam aneyanaym senhiky ; senham daivttill ninnu varunnu . senhikyunnavanellam daivattill ninnu janichairikyunnu , daivatte arrikayum cheyaunnu .
senhikyattvan daivatte arrinjidtilla ; daivam senham tanne .
daivam tante eekajatanayputrne nam avanall jiivi kyendatinnu lokattilekyu ayachau ennullatinall dai vattinnu nammodullsenham prtaykshamayi .
nam daivatte senhichaatalla , avan namme senhichau tnte putrne nammude papangallkyu prayittm aaku van ayachaatu tanne sakshall senham aakunnu .
priyamullavare , daivam namme ingane senhichau ekkill namum aneyanaym senhikyendatakunnu .
daivatte aarum oru nallum kandidtilla . nam aneyanaym senhikyunnuvekkill daivam nammill vasikyunnu ; avante senham nammill tikanjumirikyunnu .
nam avanilum avan nammilum vasikyunnu ennu avan tante aatmavine tannatinall nam arriyunnu .
pitavu putrne lokarakshitavayidtu ayachairikyunnu ennu njangall kandu sakshaym parrayunnu .
yeshu daivaputrn ennu siikarikyunnavanill daivavum avan daivattilum vasikyunnu .
ingane daivattinnu nammodullsenhatte nam arri njum vishsichaumirikyunnu . daivam senham tanne ; senhttill vasikyunnavan daivattill vasikyunnu ; daivam vanilum vasikyunnu .
nayayavidhi divasattill namukyu dhaiyaarm undavan takyvnnm itinall senham nammodu tikanjirikyunnu . avan irikyunnatupole i lokattill namum irikyunnu .
senhattill bhayamilla ; bhayattinnu dandnam ullatinall tiknj senham bhayatte purrattakyikyllayunnu ; bhayappedunnavan senhattill tikanjvanalla .
avan aadaym namme senhichaatukondu nam senhikyu nnu .
njan daivatte senhikyunnu ennu parrakayum tante shodarane pakekyyum cheyaunnavan kallanakunnu . tan kandidtullsahodarane senhikyattvannu kandidtillatt daivatte senhippan kajhyiyunnatalla .
daivatte senhikyunnavan sahodaraneyum senhikye nnam ennii kalpannamukyu avakkll ninnu labhichairikyunnu .
yeshuvine krisatu ennu vishsikyunnavan ellam daivttill ninnu janichairikyunnu . janippichaavane senhikyunnvan ellam avanill ninnu janichaavaneyum senhikyunnu .
nam daivatte senhichau avante kalpanakalle anusarichau nadakyuboll daivamakylle senhikyunnu ennu atinall arriyam .

yeshu daivaputrn ennu vishsikyunnavan allate aarakunnu lokatte jayikyunnavan ?
jalattalum rtattalum vannavan ivan aakunnu : yeshu krisatu tanne ; jalattall matrmalla , jalattalum rtattlum tanne .
aatmavum sakshaym parrayunnu ; aatmavu sataymalela .
sakshaym parrayunnavan moovar undu : aatmavu , jalam , rtam ; i moonninteyum sakshaym onnu tanne .
nam manukshayrude sakshaym kaikyollunnu ekkill daivttinte sakshaym atilum valutakunnu . daivattinte sakshaymo avan tante putrnekyurrichau sakshiikarichairi kyunnatu tanne .
daivaputrnill vishsikyunnavannu ullill asakshaym u ndu . daivatte vishsikyattvan daivam tante putr nekyurrichau parranj sakshaym vishsikyaykayall avne asatayvadiyakyunnu .
asakshaymo daivam namukyu nitayjiivan tannu ; ajiivn avante putrnill undu ennullatu tanne .
putrnullavannu jiivan undu ; daivaputrnillattvannu jiivan illa .
daivaputrnte namattill vishsikyunnningallkyu njan itu ejhyutiyirikyunnatu ningallkyu nitayjiivan undennu ningall arriyendatinnu tanne .
avante ishtaprkaram nam entekkilum apekshichaall avan nammude apekshkellkyunnu ennullatu namukyu avanodulldhaiyaarm aakunnu .
nam entu apekshichaalum avan nammude apekshke llkyunnu ennarriyunnuvekkill avanodu kajhyichapekshnamukyu labhichau ennum arriyunnu .

eetu aniitiyum papam aakunnu ; marannattinnallatt papam undu tanum .

nam daivattill ninnullavar ennu nam arriyunnu . savaar lokavum dushtante adhiinatayill kidakyunnu .

namukyu pitavikkll ninnu kalpanlabhichaatupole avidtte makyllill chilar satayttill nadakyunnatu njan kandu atayntam santokshichau .
ini nayakiyare , nam aneyanaym senhikyennam ennu putiykalpanayayidtlla , aadimutall namukyu ullatayidtu tnne njan avidattekyu ejhyuti apekshikyunnu .
pnam avante kalpanakalle anusarichau nadakyunnatu tanne senham aakunnu . ningall aadimutall kedttu pole anusarichau nadappanullkalpanitareta .

njangallude pryatnphalam kallayate poonnr prtiphalam prpikyendatinnu sookshichau kollvin .
krisatuvinte upadeshattill nilanilkyate atir kadannu pokunnoruttnnum daivam illa ; upadeshattill nilani lkyunnavanno pitavum putrnum undu .
oruttn i upadeshavumkondu allate ningallude adukyll vannuvekkill avane viidtill kaikyollarutu ; avannu kushalam parrakayum arutu .
avannu kushalam parrayunnavan avante dukshrpvrattikallkyu koodtalliyalela .
ningallkyu ejhyutuvan palatum undu : ekkilum kadalassi lum makshikondum ejhyutuvan enikyu manassilla . ningallu de santoksham poonnrmakendatinnu ningallude adukyll vannu mukhamukhamayi samsarippan aashikyunnu .
avidatte manaysahodariyude makyll vandnam chollunnu .
priyane , ninte aatmavu shubhamayirikyunnatu pole nii sakalattilum shubhamayum sukhamayum irikyennam ennu njan pratthrikyunnu .

ente makyll satayttill nadakyunnu ennu kellkyunnatine kyall valiysantoksham enikyilla .
priyane , nii sahodaranmakyrum vishekshall atithikallkyum vendi addhvanikyunnatill okyeyum vishsattkannikyu nnu .

ennennekyum jiivichairikyunnavanayi simhasanattill i rikyunnavannu ajiivikall mahatvum bahumanavum setatr vum kodukyubojhyokyeyum
